# Critique session 39 — Round 1

## Section 1: Context bundle

### Background

This is the implementation plan for the MMS convergence test whose math
derivation went through critique session 38 (verdict APPROVED). The
derivation is at
`docs/solver/mms_pnpbv_muh_multi_ion_stern_derivation.md`; final
revision and 31-issue ledger are at
`docs/handoffs/CHATGPT_HANDOFF_38_mms-logc-muh-multi-ion-stern/FINAL_REVISION.md`.

Now we need to turn that derivation into runnable code. The plan below
sequences the implementation in dependency order, identifies pre-flight
checks (quadrature sweep, Newton-convergence sanity, R_ratio check,
θ_inner discrete-min check) that must happen BEFORE pytest assertions
land, and lists the risks I'm tracking.

### Stack reminder

- `formulation='logc_muh'`, primary unknowns `(u_O2, u_H2O2, μ_H, φ)`,
  `em·z_H = +1`.
- 3 dynamic species O₂, H₂O₂, H⁺ with physical hard-sphere `a_nondim`
  (1.49e−5, 2.42e−5, 6.65e−5).
- 2 analytic Bikerman counterions Cs⁺ + SO₄²⁻ under shared-θ closure.
- Stern Robin BC at electrode, C_S = 0.20 F/m² (production target).
- Parallel R2e (E°=0.695 V, α=0.627, n_e=2, reversible) + R4e
  (E°=1.23 V, α=0.5, n_e=4, irreversible); log-rate; cathodic_conc
  factors c_H power 2 / 4.
- `exponent_clip = 100`, `u_clamp = 100`.
- `enable_water_ionization=False`, `lambda_hydrolysis=0`.

### Key derivation outputs being implemented

1. Manufactured fields:
   - `c_i^ex = c0_i · [1 + δ_i cos(πx)(1−y)²]`, δ_i = 0.30.
   - `φ^ex = (1−y)(α₀ + α₁ cos πx) + γ·y(1−y) cos(πx)`, α₀=α₁=γ=0.5.
   - `μ_H^ex = ln c_H^ex + em·z_H·φ^ex`.
   - All bulk Dirichlets met automatically; side walls auto-zero-flux.
2. Four source terms to inject into F_res:
   - NP interior: `S_c_i = −∇·J_i^ex`.
   - NP electrode: `g_i^elec = J_i^ex·n − Σ_j s_{ij}·R_j^ex`.
   - Poisson interior: `S_φ = −ε_c ∇²φ^ex − ρ_c(z_H c_H^ex + Σ_k z_k c_k^ster,ex)`.
   - Stern Robin: `g_S = ε_c (∇φ^ex·n) − C_S^model(φ_app^model − φ^ex)`.
3. Pinned K0_R4e_factor = **1e−18** (not 1; full strength gives R4e/R2e ≈ e^46 ≈ 1e20).
4. Pinned V_RHE = +0.55 V (demo anchor).
5. Source builder composes its own UFL for the multi-ion shared-θ closure
   **independently** from `boltzmann.py:91–268`; does NOT consume
   production-side `steric_boltz` bundles.

### Critical things GPT should pressure-test

1. **Dependency ordering** — does step N truly require step N−1 to be
   finished? Are there opportunities for parallel execution / earlier
   shake-out?
2. **Factory misconfiguration** — does `make_sp_production_muh` correctly
   omit the demo's two-stage Stern anchor while still passing the
   stack-invariant asserts at step 6?
3. **Source-builder logic** — every detail of step 6: does the boundary
   normal sign convention match, does the proton case use `μ_H^ex` (not
   the reconstruction `u_H_recon_ex`) for the muh primary, does
   `fd.derivative` after F_res mutation give the right Jacobian?
4. **Pilot validation completeness** — step 10's four checks. Are any
   missing? (I'm explicitly thinking about: does the quadrature sweep
   need a separate side-by-side comparison against the existing logc
   MMS to confirm we're not regressing? Should the pilot include a
   "deliberately broken config" run to verify the stack-asserts catch
   them?)
5. **Threshold choices** — L2 slope ≥ 1.8, H1 slope ≥ 0.8, R² > 0.99.
   Existing MMS uses identical tolerances (rate_tol = 0.2 on expected
   2.0 / 1.0); is that appropriate for the muh+multi-ion+Stern stack or
   should I tighten/loosen?
6. **Error norm conventions** — for the proton, comparing
   `U.sub(h_idx)` against `μ_H^ex` (not `u_H^ex`). Have I got the
   semantics right? In particular: the L2/H1 error of μ_H tells us
   about the error in the *primary unknown*; should I additionally
   report the error in `c_H = exp(μ_H − em·z_H·φ)` so we can compare
   against the existing logc MMS's c_i_L2 reporting?
7. **Risk mitigation** — am I missing any risks in §5? What about:
   adjoint-mode work that depends on F_res being functional-of-U
   (the source terms are constants in U, so this should be fine — but
   call it out); test running in `pytest-xdist`-style parallel mode
   stomping on the shared cache dirs (`/tmp/firedrake-tsfc`).
8. **Acceptance criteria sufficiency** — is criterion 5 ("source builder
   asserts catch all §7 invariants on a deliberately broken config")
   robust enough? Should we write a separate `TestMMSAsserts` class
   that parametrizes broken configs?

Be aggressive about missing pre-flight checks, latent ordering bugs,
and anything that would only surface during the pilot and waste time.

## Section 2: Artifact under review

# Implementation Plan — MMS for `logc_muh` + multi-ion + Stern stack

**Status:** plan only; not yet executed.
**Backs:** `docs/solver/mms_pnpbv_muh_multi_ion_stern_derivation.md` (post-GPT-critique session 38, verdict APPROVED).
**Owner:** PNPInverse / forward-solver verification.
**Date:** 2026-05-14.

## 0. Scope & non-goals

Build a convergence-rate MMS test that verifies the production PNP–BV stack
used by `scripts/studies/solver_demo_slide15_no_speculative_cs.py`:
`logc_muh` formulation, 3 dynamic species (O₂, H₂O₂, H⁺) with physical
hard-sphere `a_nondim`, Cs⁺/SO₄²⁻ multi-ion shared-θ Bikerman closure,
Stern Robin BC at the electrode, parallel R2e + R4e log-rate BV. Two test
classes per the derivation §7:

- `TestMMSConvergence`: UnitSquareMesh N ∈ {8, 16, 32, 64}; assert L2 slope
  ≥ 1.8, H1 slope ≥ 0.8, R² > 0.99 per primary unknown
  (u_O2, u_H2O2, μ_H, φ).
- `TestMMSProductionGradedMesh`: single-solve recovery on (Nx=8, Ny=80, β=3).

Non-goals (deferred): Stern-off cross-check, K0_R4e_factor=1 secondary
sweep, clip-activation MMS, saturation-active MMS, time-dependent MMS,
adjoint Taylor-test, c_ref-anchored anodic branch coverage. See derivation
§8.

## 1. Files

```
scripts/verification/mms_pnpbv_muh_multi_ion_stern.py   NEW  (~700 LOC)
tests/test_mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern.py              NEW  (~250 LOC)
```

No edits to production code. Existing `conftest.py::skip_without_firedrake`
is reused.

## 2. Top-level constants and config

In `scripts/verification/mms_pnpbv_muh_multi_ion_stern.py`:

```python
V_RHE_TEST = 0.55                       # V vs RHE — demo anchor
DT_LARGE   = 1.0e15
T_END_LARGE = 1.0e15
K0_R4E_FACTOR_MMS = 1.0e-18             # derivation §5.5; bounded R4e/R2e
STERN_C_S_F_M2  = 0.20                  # production target; NO two-stage anchor
DELTA_PERTURB   = (0.30, 0.30, 0.30)    # (O2, H2O2, H+) — matches existing MMS
ALPHA0          = 0.5
ALPHA1          = 0.5
GAMMA           = 0.5
SRC_QUAD_DEGREE_INITIAL = 8             # pinned post-sweep
MESH_SIZES   = (8, 16, 32, 64)
```

Plus reaction configs (R2e + R4e) reused from the demo's `_make_sp`.

## 3. Implementation steps (dependency order)

### Step 1 — Scaffolding

Create the two new files with module-level imports, header docstrings,
and `setup_firedrake_env()` boilerplate matching the existing MMS pattern.

`tests/test_mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern.py` skeleton:

```python
@skip_without_firedrake
@pytest.mark.slow
class TestMMSConvergence: ...

@skip_without_firedrake
@pytest.mark.slow
class TestMMSProductionGradedMesh: ...
```

**Verification:** `pytest --collect-only tests/test_mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern.py`
discovers two classes, no collection errors.

### Step 2 — Factory `make_sp_production_muh`

Mirror `scripts/studies/solver_demo_slide15_no_speculative_cs.py:_make_sp`
with these MMS-specific differences:
- `eta_hat = V_RHE_TEST / V_T` (fixed; not sweep).
- `dt = DT_LARGE, t_end = T_END_LARGE` (time term negligible).
- `K0_R4e_factor = K0_R4E_FACTOR_MMS` (1e−18).
- `stern_capacitance_f_m2 = STERN_C_S_F_M2` direct (no two-stage anchor;
  source builder will provide the manufactured initial guess so anchor
  numerics aren't needed).
- SNES: `atol=1e-5, rtol=1e-8, stol=1e-12, max_it=80`,
  `snes_linesearch_type="l2"`, `snes_linesearch_maxlambda=0.3`. (Mirrors
  existing logc MMS at `mms_bv_3sp_logc_boltzmann.py:139–148`.)
- `formulation="logc_muh"`, `log_rate=True`, `initializer="debye_boltzmann"`
  (initializer choice irrelevant for MMS since we overwrite with U_manuf
  before solve, but the factory requires a valid value).
- `multi_ion_enabled=True`, `boltzmann_counterions=[Cs⁺, SO₄²⁻]` from
  `DEFAULT_CSPLUS_BOLTZMANN_COUNTERION_STERIC,
  DEFAULT_SULFATE_BOLTZMANN_COUNTERION_STERIC`.
- `species` = SpeciesConfig with physical hard-sphere a_nondim from the
  demo (`A_O2_PHYSICAL`, `A_H2O2_PHYSICAL`, `A_HP_PHYSICAL`).

Signature:
```python
def make_sp_production_muh(*, mesh_Nx: int | None = None) -> SolverParams:
    ...
```

**Verification:** smoke-call `make_sp_production_muh()`, inspect the
returned tuple — formulation key reads `"logc_muh"`, `bv_reactions` has
2 entries with the right E_eq and α, `bv_stern_capacitance_model > 0`
in the converted scaling.

### Step 3 — Manufactured field UFL builders

`_make_manufactured_fields(mesh: fd.Mesh, ctx: dict, sp) -> dict`

Returns:
```
{
  "c_ex":           [c_O2_ex,  c_H2O2_ex,  c_H_ex],         # UFL
  "u_ex":           [u_O2_ex,  u_H2O2_ex,  u_H_recon_ex],   # UFL; proton is recon = ln c_H
  "mu_H_ex":        mu_H_ex,                                # UFL
  "phi_ex":         phi_ex,                                 # UFL
  "phi_app_model":  float,                                  # for hand checks
}
```

Field shapes per derivation §3.1:

```python
x, y = fd.SpatialCoordinate(mesh)
c_ex = [c0_i * (1 + δ_i * fd.cos(π·x) * (1-y)²) for i in {O2, H2O2, H}]
phi_ex = (1-y)·[α0 + α1·cos(π·x)] + γ·y·(1-y)·cos(π·x)
mu_H_ex = fd.ln(c_H_ex) + Constant(em·z_H) · phi_ex
u_ex[h_idx] = mu_H_ex − Constant(em·z_H) · phi_ex     # = ln c_H_ex by construction
```

`c0_i, em, z_H` read off `ctx["nondim"]`.

### Step 4 — Independent shared-θ closure helper

`_build_shared_theta_closure_ex(*, counterions_cfg, a_dyn, c0_dyn,
phi_ex, c_dyn_ex) -> dict`

Composes its **own** UFL for the multi-ion closure, mirroring
`Forward/bv_solver/boltzmann.py:91–268` algebraically but **without
consuming the production-side `steric_boltz` bundle objects** (derivation
§7 Independence policy).

Returns:
```
{
  "q_k_ex":        [q_k_ex per ion],
  "D_ex":          D_ex,                       # shared denominator
  "c_steric_ex":   [c_k_steric_ex per ion],
  "P_k_ex":        [a_k · c_k_steric_ex per ion],
  "rho_k_ex":      [z_k · c_k_steric_ex per ion],
  "theta_b":       float (bulk packing constant),
  "A_dyn_ex":      Σ a_i · c_i_ex,
  "theta_inner_ex": 1 − A_dyn_ex − Σ P_k_ex,
  "mu_steric_ex":  -ln(theta_inner_ex),
}
```

Reads counterions from `_get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(sp[10])`.

**Verification:** sanity-print θ_b ≈ 0.991 against the derivation §5.4
hand-computed value; sanity-print c_Cs_steric_ex evaluated at a few mesh
points and confirm magnitude ~ c_Cs^bulk · q ~ O(100).

### Step 5 — muh-aware BV rate helper

`_build_bv_rates_ex(*, reactions_cfg, scaling, u_ex, phi_ex) ->
list[ufl.Expr]`

Builds one UFL R_j_ex per reaction following derivation §3.3:
- η_j_ex = bv_exp_scale · (φ_app_model − φ_ex − E_eq_j_model)
- log_cath: `ln(k0_j) + u_ex[cat_j] + Σ_f power·(u_ex[sp_f] − ln c_ref_f) − α·n_e·η`
- log_anod: by branch (reversible+anodic / reversible+c_ref / irreversible)
- R_j = exp(log_cath) − exp(log_anod)

`u_ex[h_idx]` is **already** the muh-reconstructed `μ_H − em·z_H·φ` per
step 3, so no extra substitution here.

**Verification:** evaluate R_R4e_ex and R_R2e_ex at (x=0.5, y=0)
assembled-norm in (10, 1e5) ratio (the §5.5 invariant). If outside,
flag and stop.

### Step 6 — Source-injection routine `_build_manufactured_source`

```python
def _build_manufactured_source(
    ctx: dict, sp,
    *,
    manuf: dict,           # output of _make_manufactured_fields
    closure: dict,         # output of _build_shared_theta_closure_ex
    rxn_rates: list,       # output of _build_bv_rates_ex
    quad_degree: int = SRC_QUAD_DEGREE_INITIAL,
) -> dict:
```

Mutates `ctx['F_res']` in place by appending the four sources per
derivation §4:

1. **NP interior** (per species i): `S_c_i = −∇·J_i_ex`;
   `F_res -= S_c_i · v_i · dx_q`.
   - For non-mu species: `J_i_ex = D_i · c_i_ex · ∇(u_i_ex + μ_steric_ex)`.
   - For proton: `J_H_ex = D_H · c_H_ex · ∇(μ_H_ex + μ_steric_ex)`.
2. **NP electrode boundary** (per species i):
   `g_i_elec = J_i_ex·n − Σ_j s_{ij}·R_j_ex`;
   `F_res -= g_i_elec · v_i · ds_q(elec)`.
   Use `fd.dot(J_i_ex, fd.FacetNormal(mesh))` for the normal projection.
3. **Poisson interior**:
   `S_phi = −ε_c·∇²φ_ex − ρ_c·z_H·c_H_ex − ρ_c·Σ_k z_k·c_k_steric_ex`;
   `F_res -= S_phi · w · dx_q`.
4. **Stern Robin boundary**:
   `g_S = ε_c·(∇φ_ex·n) − C_S_model·(φ_app_model − φ_ex)`;
   `F_res -= g_S · w · ds_q(elec)`.

All on `dx_q = fd.dx(domain=mesh, degree=quad_degree)` and
`ds_q = fd.ds(domain=mesh, degree=quad_degree)`.

Re-derive Jacobian: `ctx["J_form"] = fd.derivative(ctx["F_res"], U)`.

### Step 7 — Stack-invariant asserts + runtime invariants

Embed the §7 derivation asserts as a private `_assert_stack_invariants(
ctx, sp, closure, rxn_rates)` called at the top of step 6. Implements:
- `len(scaling['bv_reactions']) == 2`
- `conv_cfg['bv_log_rate'] is True`
- `scaling['bv_stern_capacitance_model'] > 0`
- `not nondim_cfg['suppress_poisson_source']`
- `not is_water_ionization_enabled(conv_cfg)`
- `not is_cation_hydrolysis_enabled(conv_cfg)`
- `ctx['n_species'] == 3`
- exactly 2 bikerman counterions
- `ctx['mixed_space_indices'].gamma_index is None`
- `scaling['dt_model'] >= 1e12`
- `snes_atol <= 1e-5, snes_rtol <= 1e-7`

Plus the **field-dependent runtime invariants** computed against
`manuf, closure, rxn_rates`:
- θ_inner_ex discrete-min indicator: `assemble(conditional(θ < 1e-7, 1, 0)*dx) < 1e-12 · vol`
- R_ratio in finite window: `10 < ||R_R4e_ex||_L2(ds_e) / ||R_R2e_ex||_L2(ds_e) < 1e5`

Failure raises `AssertionError` with the offending value in the message
(so a green-light run never needs human inspection, but a failure points
straight at the cause).

### Step 8 — Outer `run_mms` loop

```python
def run_mms(
    N_list: Sequence[int] = MESH_SIZES,
    *,
    quad_degree: int = SRC_QUAD_DEGREE_INITIAL,
    verbose: bool = True,
) -> dict:
```

Per mesh:
1. `mesh = fd.UnitSquareMesh(N, N)`.
2. `sp = make_sp_production_muh()`; ensure `sp.solver_options["bv_convergence"]["exponent_clip"]`
   is the canonical 100.0 (Hard Rule #2).
3. `ctx = build_context(sp, mesh=mesh); ctx = build_forms(ctx, sp)`.
4. `manuf = _make_manufactured_fields(mesh, ctx, sp)`.
5. `closure = _build_shared_theta_closure_ex(...)` reading counterions from sp.
6. `rxn_rates = _build_bv_rates_ex(...)`.
7. `ctx = _build_manufactured_source(ctx, sp, manuf=manuf, closure=closure,
   rxn_rates=rxn_rates, quad_degree=quad_degree)`.
8. Build `U_manuf`: interpolate `u_O2_ex, u_H2O2_ex, μ_H_ex, φ_ex` onto
   each `W.sub(...)`. **For the proton, interpolate μ_H_ex, NOT u_H_recon_ex.**
9. `U.assign(U_manuf); U_prev.assign(U_manuf)`.
10. Solve via `fd.NonlinearVariationalSolver` with `snes_params` from sp.
11. Compute L2 / H1 errors per primary unknown:
    - O2: `_ufl_l2_error(u_O2_ex, U.sub(O2_idx), mesh, degree=quad_degree)`
    - H2O2: same with u_H2O2_ex
    - **H+: `_ufl_l2_error(μ_H_ex, U.sub(h_idx), mesh, degree=quad_degree)`**
    - φ: same with phi_ex

Returns `{"N": [...], "h": [...], "u_O2_L2": [...], "u_O2_H1": [...], ...,
"mu_H_L2": [...], "mu_H_H1": [...], "phi_L2": [...], "phi_H1": [...]}`.

### Step 9 — `verify_on_graded_production_mesh` (single solve)

Mirrors the existing logc MMS's `verify_on_graded_production_mesh` but
for the new stack. Uses the graded rectangle Nx=8, Ny=80, β=3 from the
demo. Returns the same dict shape as `run_mms` for a single mesh.

**Newton-converged check** is the load-bearing one here; L2/H1
thresholds are 6× above the empirically-measured baseline.

### Step 10 — Pilot validation (BEFORE adding pytest assertions)

Run-once shake-out before the convergence tests can land:

1. **Quadrature sweep at N=32**: run `run_mms([32], quad_degree=d)` for
   `d ∈ {6, 8, 10, 12, 16}`. Tabulate per-field L2 errors. Pin
   `SRC_QUAD_DEGREE` to smallest `d` where each field's L2 is within
   1% of the `d=16` value. Document the table in the test file's
   class docstring.
2. **Newton-convergence sanity at N=8**: `run_mms([8])` must report
   `newton_converged=True`. If not, debug source-builder bug before
   widening.
3. **R_ratio check at N=32**: confirm `||R_R4e_ex||_L2 / ||R_R2e_ex||_L2`
   lies in `(10, 1e5)` at the chosen K0_R4e_factor; if not, retune
   K0_R4e_factor.
4. **θ_inner_ex discrete-min**: confirm
   `min over mesh nodes of theta_inner_ex > 1e-7` at the chosen envelope;
   if not, tighten (α0, α1, γ) — should pass at 0.5/0.5/0.5.

Save pilot artifacts to
`StudyResults/mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern/pilot/` (JSON + plots) and
reference them in the test file docstring.

### Step 11 — `TestMMSConvergence`

```python
class TestMMSConvergence:
    MESH_SIZES = (8, 16, 32, 64)
    EXPECTED_L2_RATE = 2.0
    EXPECTED_H1_RATE = 1.0
    RATE_TOL = 0.2          # accept slope >= 1.8 (L2) and >= 0.8 (H1)
    MIN_R_SQUARED = 0.99

    @pytest.fixture(scope="class")
    def mms_results(self):
        return run_mms(self.MESH_SIZES, verbose=True)

    def test_newton_converges_on_all_meshes(self, mms_results): ...
    def test_l2_convergence_rates(self, mms_results): ...   # 4 fields × scipy.linregress
    def test_h1_convergence_rates(self, mms_results): ...
    def test_gci_output(self, mms_results): ...             # Roache, Fs=1.25
    def test_save_convergence_artifacts(self, mms_results): ...  # JSON + PNG
```

`test_l2_convergence_rates` iterates over fields
`["u_O2", "u_H2O2", "mu_H", "phi"]` using `assert_convergence_rate`
imported from the existing `tests/test_mms_convergence.py` (already
written; reuse).

Artifacts land at
`StudyResults/mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern/convergence_data.json` and
`mms_convergence.png`.

## 4. Dependency graph

```
Step 1 (scaffolding)
  └─→ Step 2 (factory)
        └─→ Step 3 (manuf fields)
              ├─→ Step 4 (closure helper)
              │     └─→ Step 6 (source injection)
              └─→ Step 5 (BV rates helper)
                    └─→ Step 6 (source injection)
                          └─→ Step 7 (asserts/invariants — embedded in step 6)
                                └─→ Step 8 (run_mms loop)
                                      ├─→ Step 9 (graded mesh)
                                      └─→ Step 10 (pilot validation)
                                            ├─→ Step 11 (TestMMSConvergence)
                                            └─→ Step 12 (TestMMSProductionGradedMesh)
                                                  └─→ Step 13 (CI integration)
```

## 5. Risks and unknowns

| Risk | Mitigation | Pre-pilot evidence required |
|---|---|---|
| Newton fails to converge at N=8 because manufactured source overwhelms RHS | Pilot step 10.2 must pass before proceeding | Newton convergence + `||F_res||_final < snes_atol` |
| Convergence rate falls below 1.8 (L2) because quadrature error dominates | Quadrature sweep (step 10.1) pins degree where error plateaus | Rate stable across degree 8 → 12 → 16 |
| R4e/R2e outside (10, 1e5) at chosen K0_R4e_factor | Step 10.3 retunes factor; alternatives 1e-16 or 1e-20 | Single L2-norm computation per ds_e |
| θ_inner_ex hits packing_floor on some mesh | Step 10.4; tighten envelope if needed | Discrete-min via indicator |
| Stern setter or runtime mutation accidentally fires between source build and solve | `_assert_stack_invariants` checks; no setters called in `run_mms` body | Code review of the new module |
| Existing `_ufl_l2_error` / `_ufl_h1_error` quadrature degree is too low for μ_H_ex (because of em·z_H·φ_ex coupling) | Pass `degree=quad_degree` explicitly per call site | Step 10.1 catches if quadrature is the bottleneck |
| Production residual changes between MMS authoring and merge (Phase 6β churn) | Tie MMS to specific Forward/bv_solver commit; rerun pilot on update | git pin in test file docstring |
| Test wall time blows up | Mark slow; cap N≤64 for convergence sweep | Empirical timing in pilot |

## 6. Empirical pilot artifacts to produce

Output to `StudyResults/mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern/pilot/`:

- `quadrature_sweep.json`: per-degree L2 / H1 / Newton-iteration counts.
- `quadrature_sweep.png`: log-log L2 vs degree per field.
- `n8_newton_convergence.json`: Newton history, residual norm trace.
- `r_ratio_check.json`: R_R4e_norm, R_R2e_norm, ratio.
- `theta_min_check.json`: discrete min, indicator-measure, sample plot
  of θ_inner_ex on N=32 mesh.

These set the per-field thresholds in step 12 and feed into the
convergence-test docstring.

## 7. Acceptance criteria

The implementation is complete when:

1. `pytest tests/test_mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern.py -m slow` passes end
   to end on the venv-firedrake environment.
2. All four primary unknowns achieve L2 slope ≥ 1.8 and H1 slope ≥ 0.8
   with R² > 0.99 in the N ∈ {8, 16, 32, 64} sweep.
3. `verify_on_graded_production_mesh` converges Newton in fewer than 30
   iterations on the production graded rectangle and meets the
   empirically-pinned thresholds.
4. JSON + PNG artifacts land in
   `StudyResults/mms_logc_muh_multi_ion_stern/`.
5. Source builder asserts catch all the §7 invariants on a deliberately
   broken config (sanity test, optional but recommended).
6. Test class docstrings reference the quadrature sweep and pilot results.
7. The derivation doc
   `docs/solver/mms_pnpbv_muh_multi_ion_stern_derivation.md` and the
   handoff `docs/handoffs/CHATGPT_HANDOFF_38_.../FINAL_REVISION.md` are
   linked from the test file.

## 8. Estimated effort

- Steps 1–2: 1 h.
- Steps 3–5: 4 h (manufactured fields + closure helper + BV helper).
- Step 6: 4 h (term-by-term source injection, careful with `fd.dot` /
  `fd.FacetNormal` / quadrature).
- Step 7: 2 h (asserts + runtime invariants).
- Steps 8–9: 3 h (run_mms loop + graded-mesh single solve).
- Step 10 (pilot, includes debugging): 4–8 h.
- Steps 11–13: 3 h.

Total: 21–25 hours of focused work. Half-budget for the pilot is
deliberate — that's where unknown unknowns surface.

## 9. Open questions to resolve during implementation

1. Should the source builder accept `quad_degree` as a per-mesh argument
   (to support the quadrature sweep) or as a module-level constant?
   Recommendation: kwarg with sensible default, so the sweep is a clean
   call.
2. For the graded mesh in step 9, does the manufactured solution need
   re-design (the existing logc MMS reuses the `(x,y) ∈ [0,1]²` shape
   on a graded rectangle)? Expected answer: same shape works because
   the rectangle is mapped 1-to-1 to the unit square. Verify in pilot.
3. Should we emit per-mesh Newton-iteration plots to catch
   non-monotonic convergence? Yes if pilot shows N=64 hits the iteration
   cap.
4. Is `boltzmann.py:91-268` stable enough that mirroring its algebra in
   step 4 is safe? Pin the test to a specific commit via
   git-log-reference in the test docstring; revisit if `boltzmann.py`
   undergoes a structural change.

This plan is ready for adversarial GPT review. Loop will pressure-test
dependency ordering, factory misconfiguration risk, source-builder
correctness, pilot design, threshold choices, and any missing setup
steps.

## Section 3: Critique prompt

You are an adversarial reviewer. Be critical. Be argumentative.
Find every hole: missing steps, wrong algebra, untested assumptions,
edge cases not addressed, implicit dependencies, claims without
evidence, off-by-one errors, sign errors, dimensional errors. Don't
be polite — if something is wrong, say so. Concision over hedging.

For each issue, state:
  - WHAT is wrong (specific, not vague — name the line or symbol)
  - WHY it matters (what breaks downstream if uncorrected)
  - WHAT to do (concrete fix, or what evidence would close the gap)

Number your issues. After all issues, end your response with exactly
one of these lines, no other text after it:

  VERDICT: APPROVED
  VERDICT: ISSUES_REMAIN

Use APPROVED only when there are no issues you would block on.
Minor nitpicks alone do not justify ISSUES_REMAIN — call them out
but still verdict APPROVED. Use ISSUES_REMAIN whenever any of your
issues are genuinely blocking.

     1	"""Production-faithful MMS convergence test for the production PNP-BV solver.
     2	
     3	Verifies the *exact* production stack used by ``scripts/plot_iv_curve_unified.py``:
     4	
     5	  - 3 dynamic species (O2, H2O2, H+) + analytic Boltzmann ClO4-
     6	  - log-concentration primary variables ``u_i = ln(c_i)``
     7	  - log-rate Butler-Volmer evaluation (``bv_log_rate=True``)
     8	  - Physical E_eq (R1 = 0.68 V, R2 = 1.78 V vs RHE)
     9	  - Real D, k0, alpha, c0 from ``scripts/_bv_common.py`` (Mangan2025, pH 4)
    10	  - Steric (Bikerman) with a_vals = [0.01]*3 (production default)
    11	  - eta-clip (+/-50) and u-clamp (100, production-widened) left active --
    12	    inactive *by manufactured-solution design* so MMS verifies the smooth
    13	    operator without crossing a non-smooth threshold.
    14	
    15	The factory call mirrors the production driver
    16	``scripts/plot_iv_curve_unified.py:139`` exactly.
    17	
    18	Manufactured solution (in nondim units)::
    19	
    20	    c_i^ex(x, y) = c0_HAT[i] * (1 + delta_i * cos(pi x) * (1 - y)^2)
    21	    phi^ex(x, y) = eta_hat * (1 - y) + B_phi * cos(pi x) * y * (1 - y)
    22	
    23	These exactly satisfy production Dirichlet BCs::
    24	
    25	    u_i(x, 1) = ln(c0_HAT[i])    <- production concentration BC
    26	    phi(x, 1) = 0                 <- production ground BC
    27	    phi(x, 0) = eta_hat           <- production electrode BC
    28	
    29	so no BC overrides are needed.
    30	
    31	V_RHE = +0.55 V chosen so:
    32	
    33	  - eta_R1 = (V - 0.68) / V_T = -5.06   (clip inactive, |eta| << 50)
    34	  - eta_R2 = (V - 1.78) / V_T = -47.87  (clip inactive, |eta| < 50)
    35	  - Inside production warm-walk regime (V_RHE in [+0.50, +1.20] V).
    36	
    37	Source generation (term-by-term continuum residual at u_exact):
    38	
    39	  Standard MMS pattern: compute the *continuum* residual of each
    40	  production weak-form term at U=u_exact, inject as forcing on F_res.
    41	  At u_exact in continuum the residual vanishes; the discrete operator
    42	  has O(h^p) error vs continuum, so the discrete solution u_h satisfies
    43	  ||u_h - u_exact||_L2 = O(h^(k+1)) and ||u_h - u_exact||_H1 = O(h^k).
    44	
    45	  Important: we deliberately do NOT use ``ufl.replace`` to mirror the
    46	  discrete F_res at U_manuf -- that would make U_manuf an exact discrete
    47	  solution by construction, hiding any wiring bug that's symmetric on
    48	  both sides of the subtraction.  By writing the source against an
    49	  independent continuum statement of the PDE, any inconsistency in
    50	  F_res's discrete implementation shows up as a convergence-rate violation.
    51	
    52	Mesh: ``UnitSquareMesh(N, N)``.  Departure from production's graded
    53	rectangle (Nx=8, Ny=200, beta=3): graded refinement breaks h^p
    54	convergence.  The operator under test is mesh-topology independent.
    55	
    56	Expected: L2 rate ~ 2.0, H1 rate ~ 1.0 (CG1) for u_i and phi.

   118	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   119	# SolverParams factory call (mirrors ``plot_iv_curve_unified.py:139``)
   120	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   121	def make_sp_production(eta_hat: float, *, counterion_entry=None):
   122	    """Build SolverParams matching the production driver, with two changes:
   123	
   124	    (1) ``eta_hat`` is fixed at the test voltage.
   125	    (2) ``dt`` is large to neutralize the time term -- we initialise
   126	        ``U_prev = U_manuf`` so ``(c - c_old)/dt`` is exactly zero.
   127	    """
   128	    # Tolerances are looser than the production driver (atol=1e-7) because
   129	    # the manufactured-solution test problem has large absolute source
   130	    # magnitude at V_RHE = +0.55 V -- the Boltzmann counterion contributes
   131	    # ~1e8 to F_res near the electrode (Σz·c_bulk·exp(-z·η) at η ~ 21).
   132	    # The FP-noise floor on source evaluation is therefore ~1e-8 absolute,
   133	    # below which Newton spins.  Relative tolerance (rtol=1e-8) is what
   134	    # actually drives Newton to the discretization-error floor; that's
   135	    # what verifies the operator.  Initial residual norm reaches O(1e9)
   136	    # at U_manuf, so rtol=1e-8 means Newton drives residual to O(1e1),
   137	    # which is below the smallest discretization error of interest at
   138	    # N=128 (O(h^2) ~ 6e-5).
   139	    snes_opts = {
   140	        **SNES_OPTS_CHARGED,
   141	        "snes_max_it":               60,
   142	        "snes_atol":                 1e-5,
   143	        "snes_rtol":                 1e-8,
   144	        "snes_stol":                 1e-12,
   145	        "snes_linesearch_type":      "l2",   # production setting
   146	        "snes_linesearch_maxlambda": 0.3,    # production setting
   147	        "snes_divergence_tolerance": 1e10,
   148	    }
   149	    return make_bv_solver_params(
   150	        eta_hat=eta_hat,
   151	        dt=1e15, t_end=1e15,
   152	        species=THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN,
   153	        snes_opts=snes_opts,
   154	        formulation="logc",
   155	        log_rate=True,
   156	        u_clamp=100.0,
   157	        boltzmann_counterions=(

   159	            else [DEFAULT_CLO4_BOLTZMANN_COUNTERION]
   160	        ),
   161	        k0_hat_r1=K0_HAT_R1, k0_hat_r2=K0_HAT_R2,
   162	        alpha_r1=ALPHA_R1,   alpha_r2=ALPHA_R2,
   163	        E_eq_r1=E_EQ_R1,     E_eq_r2=E_EQ_R2,
   164	    )

   167	def _extract_solver_parameters(sp):
   168	    """Pull the SNES/KSP/PC/MUMPS options from the SolverParams 11-tuple."""
   169	    params = sp[10]

   187	    """Inject the continuum residual of every production weak-form term at
   188	    U=u_exact into ``ctx['F_res']`` as a forcing.
   189	
   190	    The PDE we mirror in continuum (matching forms_logc.py + boltzmann.py):
   191	
   192	      Per species i:
   193	        d c_i / dt + nabla . J_i  =  0  (interior)
   194	        J_i . n  =  sum_j s_ij R_j      (electrode)
   195	        J_i  =  -D_i * c_i * (grad u_i + em*z_i*grad phi + grad mu_steric)
   196	        mu_steric  =  ln(1 - sum_i a_i * c_i)
   197	        R_j = exp(log_cathodic_j) - exp(log_anodic_j)  (log-rate form)
   198	
   199	      Poisson:
   200	        -eps * laplacian(phi)  -  charge_rhs * sum_i z_i * c_i
   201	                                -  z_scale * charge_rhs * sum_k z_k * c_bulk_k * exp(-z_k * phi)
   202	        =  0
   203	
   204	    The corresponding discrete weak form (production):
   205	        sum_i [ ((c_i - c_old_i)/dt) v_i dx + J_i . grad(v_i) dx
   206	                - sum_j s_ij R_j v_i ds(electrode) ]
   207	        + eps * grad(phi) . grad(w) dx
   208	        - charge_rhs * sum_i z_i c_i w dx
   209	        - sum_k z_scale * charge_rhs * z_k * c_bulk_k * exp(-z_k phi_clamped) w dx
   210	        =  0
   211	
   212	    Adding the continuum source (subtracting from F_res) makes u_exact a
   213	    continuum solution; the discrete solver finds u_h that approximates
   214	    u_exact at the predicted h^(k+1) / h^k rate.
   215	    """
   216	    n = ctx["n_species"]
   217	    mesh = ctx["mesh"]
   218	    W = ctx["W"]
   219	
   220	    # --- Pull production scaling (so D, k0, alpha, em, eps, charge_rhs all
   221	    # match the dispatched production residual) ---
   222	    scaling = ctx["nondim"]
   223	    em = float(scaling["electromigration_prefactor"])
   224	    eps = float(scaling["poisson_coefficient"])
   225	    charge_rhs = float(scaling["charge_rhs_prefactor"])
   226	    D_model = [float(scaling["D_model_vals"][i]) for i in range(n)]
   227	    z_vals_float = [float(z) for z in THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.z_vals]
   228	    phi_app_model = float(scaling["phi_applied_model"])  # nondim eta_hat
   229	    bv_exp_scale = float(scaling["bv_exponent_scale"])
   230	
   231	    # Steric (Bikerman) coefficients.  Production a_vals_hat is
   232	    # [A_DEFAULT]*3 = [0.01]*3.  packing_floor only fires near
   233	    # close-packing -- our manufactured c_i is well below that.
   234	    a_vals_float = [float(A_DEFAULT)] * n
   235	
   236	    # Steric-aware Boltzmann counterion (bikerman closure) — when
   237	    # supplied, the manufactured Poisson source uses ``c_steric_manuf``
   238	    # in place of ideal ``c_b * exp(-z*phi)``, AND the dynamic species'
   239	    # packing fraction includes the counterion's contribution
   240	    # (mirroring forms_logc.py's wiring).
   241	    if bikerman_counterion is not None:
   242	        z_b_steric = float(bikerman_counterion["z"])
   243	        c_b_steric = float(bikerman_counterion["c_bulk_nondim"])
   244	        a_b_steric = float(bikerman_counterion["a_nondim"])
   245	        # Bulk packing fraction (the helper in boltzmann.py validates this).
   246	        c0_dyn_bulk = list(scaling.get("c0_model_vals", []))[:n]
   247	        A_dyn_bulk = sum(a_vals_float[i] * float(c0_dyn_bulk[i])
   248	                         for i in range(min(n, len(c0_dyn_bulk))))
   249	        theta_b_steric = 1.0 - A_dyn_bulk - a_b_steric * c_b_steric
   250	        # Closure expression at the manufactured fields.  The phi clamp
   251	        # is irrelevant on our smooth manufactured solution (well below
   252	        # the ±50 limit), so we omit the clamp here.
   253	        q_manuf = fd.exp(-fd.Constant(z_b_steric) * phi_exact)
   254	        A_dyn_manuf = sum(
   255	            fd.Constant(a_vals_float[i]) * c_exact[i] for i in range(n)
   256	        )
   257	        c_steric_manuf = (
   258	            fd.Constant(c_b_steric) * q_manuf
   259	            * (fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn_manuf)
   260	            / (fd.Constant(theta_b_steric)

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""Solver demo — Cs+/SO4(2-) baseline I-V curves over slide-15 V_RHE band.
     2	
     3	Purpose
     4	-------
     5	Demonstrate that the production PNP+BV forward stack produces sensible

     9	
    10	What is OFF
    11	-----------
    12	* ``enable_water_ionization = False``       (no Kw split / proton-condition residual)
    13	* ``enable_cation_hydrolysis`` not enabled  (no Singh cation hydrolysis source)
    14	* ``lambda_hydrolysis = 0.0``               (no Singh sigma-pKa ramp)
    15	
    16	What is ON (production defaults)
    17	--------------------------------
    18	* THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN (O2, H2O2, H+) with PHYSICAL hard-sphere
    19	  ``a_vals_hat`` for the dynamic species — replaces A_DEFAULT=0.01 with
    20	  Marcus/Stokes radii (O2 r=1.70 A, H2O2 r=2.00 A, H+ r=2.80 A as H3O+).
    21	  Counterions Cs+ and SO4(2-) keep their existing A_*_HAT entries.
    22	* Parallel-2e/4e Butler-Volmer (Ruggiero 2022): E0_R2e = 0.695 V,

    26	  "suppressed 18 orders of magnitude").

   105	# Physical hard-sphere a_nondim for dynamic species O2/H2O2/H+.
   106	# a_phys = (4/3) pi r^3 N_A m^3/mol; a_nondim = a_phys * C_SCALE.

   111	def _a_nondim_from_radius_m(r_m: float) -> float:
   112	    a_phys = (4.0 / 3.0) * math.pi * r_m ** 3 * _N_A
   113	    return a_phys * _C_SCALE

   152	def build_context_logc_muh(solver_params: Any, *, mesh: Any = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
   153	    """Build mesh and function spaces for muh BV PNP solver.
   154	
   155	    Identical mixed-space layout to ``build_context_logc`` -- the muh
   156	    transform changes only the *interpretation* of ``U.sub(mu_h_idx)``, not
   157	    the function space.  Marks the context with ``logc_muh_transform=True``
   158	    so downstream diagnostics know to read concentrations through
   159	    ``ctx['ci_exprs']`` rather than ``np.exp(U.sub(i).dat...)``.
   160	    """
   161	    ctx = build_context_logc(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
   162	    ctx["logc_muh_transform"] = True
   163	    return ctx
   164	
   165	
   166	def build_forms_logc_muh(ctx: dict[str, Any], solver_params: Any) -> dict[str, Any]:
   167	    """Assemble weak forms with the proton electrochemical-potential transform.
   168	
   169	    Primary unknowns: ``u_i = log(c_i)`` for non-mu species, ``mu_H =
   170	    u_H + em*z_H*phi`` for the proton, plus ``phi``.  Concentrations
   171	    reconstructed pointwise as
   172	
   173	        c_H    = exp(min/max(mu_H - em*z_H*phi,    +/- u_clamp))
   174	        c_H,old= exp(min/max(mu_H_old - em*z_H*phi_old, +/- u_clamp))   <- phi_prev!
   175	
   176	    The clamp is applied to reconstructed ``log(c_H)`` (not raw ``mu_H``);
   177	    see module docstring.
   178	    """
   179	    try:
   180	        n_species, order, dt, t_end, z_vals, D_vals, a_vals, phi_applied, c0, phi0, params = solver_params
   181	    except Exception as exc:
   182	        raise ValueError("bv_solver expects a list of 11 solver parameters") from exc
   183	
   184	    c0_raw = [float(v) for v in (
   185	        [c0] * n_species if np.isscalar(c0) else list(c0)
   186	    )][:n_species]
   187	
   188	    mesh = ctx["mesh"]
   189	    W = ctx["W"]
   190	    n = ctx["n_species"]
   191	
   192	    # Parse BV config and convergence options.
   193	    bv_cfg = _get_bv_cfg(params, n)
   194	    conv_cfg = _get_bv_convergence_cfg(params)
   195	    reactions_cfg = _get_bv_reactions_cfg(params, n)
   196	    use_reactions = reactions_cfg is not None
   197	
   198	    # Nondimensionalization (same as forms_logc.py).
   199	    dummy_robin = {
   200	        "kappa_vals": [1.0] * n,
   201	        "c_inf_vals": bv_cfg["c_ref_vals"],
   202	        "electrode_marker": bv_cfg["electrode_marker"],
   203	        "concentration_marker": bv_cfg["concentration_marker"],
   204	        "ground_marker": bv_cfg["ground_marker"],
   205	    }
   206	    base_scaling = build_model_scaling(
   207	        params=params,
   208	        n_species=n,
   209	        dt=dt,
   210	        t_end=t_end,
   211	        D_vals=D_vals,
   212	        c0_vals=c0_raw,
   213	        phi_applied=phi_applied,
   214	        phi0=phi0,
   215	        robin=dummy_robin,
   216	    )
   217	
   218	    nondim_cfg = _get_nondim_cfg(params)
   219	    nondim_enabled = _bool(nondim_cfg.get("enabled", False))
   220	    kappa_inputs_dimless = _bool(nondim_cfg.get("kappa_inputs_are_dimensionless", True))
   221	    concentration_inputs_dimless = _bool(
   222	        nondim_cfg.get("concentration_inputs_are_dimensionless", False)
   223	    )
   224	
   225	    if use_reactions:
   226	        E_eq_v = float(bv_cfg.get("E_eq_v", 0.0))
   227	        scaling = _add_bv_reactions_scaling_to_transform(
   228	            base_scaling, reactions_cfg,
   229	            nondim_enabled=nondim_enabled,
   230	            kappa_inputs_dimless=kappa_inputs_dimless,
   231	            concentration_inputs_dimless=concentration_inputs_dimless,
   232	            E_eq_v=E_eq_v,
   233	        )
   234	        # Stern layer capacitance (same as forms_logc.py).  Phase 6β v9
   235	        # Gate 2: also store the phys→nondim conversion factor so the
   236	        # C_S continuation orchestrator can reassign the live Constant
   237	        # given a physical F/m² target.
   238	        stern_raw = bv_cfg.get("stern_capacitance_f_m2")
   239	        if stern_raw is not None and float(stern_raw) > 0:
   240	            if not nondim_enabled:
   241	                scaling["bv_stern_capacitance_model"] = float(stern_raw)
   242	                scaling["bv_stern_phys_to_nondim_factor"] = 1.0
   243	            else:
   244	                from Nondim.constants import FARADAY_CONSTANT as _F
   245	                length_scale = scaling.get("length_scale_m", 1.0)
   246	                potential_scale_v = scaling.get("potential_scale_v", 1.0)
   247	                concentration_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
   248	                conv_factor = potential_scale_v / (
   249	                    _F * concentration_scale * length_scale
   250	                )
   251	                scaling["bv_stern_capacitance_model"] = (
   252	                    float(stern_raw) * conv_factor
   253	                )
   254	                scaling["bv_stern_phys_to_nondim_factor"] = float(conv_factor)
   255	        else:
   256	            scaling.setdefault("bv_stern_capacitance_model", None)
   257	            scaling.setdefault("bv_stern_phys_to_nondim_factor", 1.0)
   258	    else:
   259	        scaling = _add_bv_scaling_to_transform(
   260	            base_scaling, bv_cfg,
   261	            n_species=n,
   262	            nondim_enabled=nondim_enabled,
   263	            kappa_inputs_dimless=kappa_inputs_dimless,
   264	            concentration_inputs_dimless=concentration_inputs_dimless,
   265	        )
   266	
   267	    electrode_marker = bv_cfg["electrode_marker"]
   268	    concentration_marker = bv_cfg["concentration_marker"]
   269	    ground_marker = bv_cfg["ground_marker"]
   270	
   271	    dx = fd.Measure("dx", domain=mesh)
   272	    ds = fd.Measure("ds", domain=mesh)
   273	    R_space = fd.FunctionSpace(mesh, "R", 0)
   274	
   275	    # Log-diffusivity controls (same as forms_logc.py).
   276	    m = [fd.Function(R_space, name=f"logD{i}") for i in range(n)]
   277	    for i in range(n):
   278	        m[i].assign(np.log(float(scaling["D_model_vals"][i])))
   279	    D = [fd.exp(m[i]) for i in range(n)]
   280	
   281	    z = [fd.Constant(float(z_vals[i])) for i in range(n)]
   282	
   283	    U = ctx["U"]
   284	    U_prev = ctx["U_prev"]
   285	
   286	    # Resolve mu species (Phase 2: H+ only).  Phase 6β v9 Gate 1: thread
   287	    # ``species_roles`` so K2SO4-style stacks with two z=+1 species (H⁺
   288	    # + K⁺) can disambiguate via explicit role labels.
   289	    species_roles = _get_species_roles(params, n)
   290	    mu_h_idx = _resolve_mu_h_index(list(z_vals), roles=species_roles)
   291	    mu_species = [mu_h_idx]
   292	
   293	    # Split mixed function: u_i (non-mu) or mu_H (mu_h_idx) for species,
   294	    # phi for potential.  Note: ui[mu_h_idx] is mu_H, NOT u_H.
   295	    # Phase 6β v9 Gate 3A: use the layout-aware index helper so the
   296	    # mixed-space slicing works for both the legacy ``species + phi``
   297	    # layout and the Γ-augmented ``species + phi + Γ`` layout.  The
   298	    # indices object lives on ctx (set by ``build_context_logc``).
   299	    indices = ctx.get("mixed_space_indices") or unpack_dof_indices(
   300	        has_gamma=False
   301	    )
   302	    ui = fd.split(U)[indices.species_slice]
   303	    phi = fd.split(U)[indices.phi_index]
   304	    ui_prev = fd.split(U_prev)[indices.species_slice]
   305	    phi_prev = fd.split(U_prev)[indices.phi_index]   # NEW for muh: c_H_old reconstruction
   306	    v_tests = fd.TestFunctions(W)
   307	    v_list = v_tests[indices.species_slice]
   308	    w = v_tests[indices.phi_index]
   309	
   310	    # Electromigration prefactor and dt -- moved up from forms_logc.py
   311	    # (line 214) so we can reference em when reconstructing log(c_H) for
   312	    # the mu-species.
   313	    em = float(scaling["electromigration_prefactor"])
   314	    dt_const = fd.Constant(float(scaling["dt_model"]))
   315	
   316	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   317	    # Reconstruct log-concentrations and concentrations
   318	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   319	    # For non-mu species:    u_expr(i)      = ui[i]
   320	    # For mu species (H+):   u_expr(i)      = mu_H - em*z_H*phi              <- recover log(c_H)
   321	    #                        u_expr_prev(i) = mu_H_prev - em*z_H*phi_prev    <- USE phi_prev
   322	    #
   323	    # The clamp is applied to the reconstructed log(c_H), not raw mu_H,
   324	    # so the floating-point overflow protection on c_H = exp(...) is
   325	    # preserved for the muh formulation.
   326	    _U_CLAMP = float(conv_cfg.get("u_clamp", 30.0))
   327	    _U_CLAMP_C = fd.Constant(_U_CLAMP)
   328	    _NEG_U_CLAMP_C = fd.Constant(-_U_CLAMP)
   329	
   330	    def _u_expr(i: int, ui_split, phi_var):
   331	        if i in mu_species:
   332	            return ui_split[i] - fd.Constant(em) * z[i] * phi_var
   333	        return ui_split[i]
   334	
   335	    u_exprs      = [_u_expr(i, ui,      phi)      for i in range(n)]
   336	    u_prev_exprs = [_u_expr(i, ui_prev, phi_prev) for i in range(n)]
   337	
   338	    ci      = [fd.exp(fd.min_value(fd.max_value(u_exprs[i],      _NEG_U_CLAMP_C), _U_CLAMP_C))
   339	               for i in range(n)]
   340	    ci_prev = [fd.exp(fd.min_value(fd.max_value(u_prev_exprs[i], _NEG_U_CLAMP_C), _U_CLAMP_C))
   341	               for i in range(n)]
   342	
   343	    # Phase 6α — water self-ionization closure for the muh backend.
   344	    # ``u_exprs[h_idx_water]`` is the muh-reconstructed log(c_H) =
   345	    # μ_H − em·z_H·φ; pass the unclamped reconstruction to the helper so
   346	    # the symmetric clamp on c_OH = Kw_eff·exp(-u_H) lines up with the
   347	    # symmetric clamp on c_H = exp(u_H).
   348	    water_ion_enabled = is_water_ionization_enabled(conv_cfg)
   349	    if water_ion_enabled:
   350	        h_idx_water = resolve_h_index(list(z_vals), roles=species_roles)
   351	        if h_idx_water != mu_h_idx:
   352	            raise ValueError(
   353	                "enable_water_ionization=True requires the water-ionization "
   354	                "H+ index to match the muh formulation's mu species index "
   355	                f"(h_idx_water={h_idx_water}, mu_h_idx={mu_h_idx}); the "
   356	                "muh stack only supports H+ as the proton-condition variable."
   357	            )
   358	        water_bundle = build_water_ionization_terms(
   359	            ctx=ctx,
   360	            conv_cfg=conv_cfg,
   361	            z_vals=z_vals,
   362	            u_h_unclamped=u_exprs[h_idx_water],
   363	            u_h_unclamped_prev=u_prev_exprs[h_idx_water],
   364	            ci_h_clamped=ci[h_idx_water],
   365	            ci_h_prev_clamped=ci_prev[h_idx_water],
   366	            R_space=R_space,
   367	            u_clamp=_U_CLAMP,
   368	            roles=species_roles,
   369	        )
   370	    else:
   371	        h_idx_water = None
   372	        water_bundle = None
   373	
   374	    # Electrode potential constant.
   375	    phi_applied_func = fd.Function(R_space, name="phi_applied")
   376	    phi_applied_func.assign(float(scaling["phi_applied_model"]))
   377	    phi0_func = fd.Function(R_space, name="phi0")
   378	    phi0_func.assign(float(scaling["phi0_model"]))
   379	
   380	    # Global E_eq.
   381	    E_eq_model_global = fd.Constant(float(scaling["bv_E_eq_model"]))
   382	    bv_exp_scale = fd.Constant(float(scaling["bv_exponent_scale"]))
   383	
   384	    # Stern layer flag.
   385	    stern_capacitance_model = scaling.get("bv_stern_capacitance_model")
   386	    use_stern = stern_capacitance_model is not None and float(stern_capacitance_model) > 0
   387	
   388	    def _build_eta_clipped(E_eq_const):
   389	        """Build clipped overpotential expression for a given E_eq.
   390	
   391	        See ``forms_logc.py`` for the full semantics of the clip.
   392	        """
   393	        if use_stern:
   394	            eta_raw = phi_applied_func - phi - E_eq_const
   395	        elif conv_cfg["use_eta_in_bv"]:
   396	            eta_raw = phi_applied_func - E_eq_const
   397	        else:
   398	            eta_raw = phi - E_eq_const
   399	        eta_scaled = bv_exp_scale * eta_raw
   400	        if conv_cfg["clip_exponent"]:
   401	            clip_val = fd.Constant(float(conv_cfg["exponent_clip"]))
   402	            return fd.min_value(fd.max_value(eta_scaled, -clip_val), clip_val)
   403	        return eta_scaled
   404	
   405	    eta_clipped = _build_eta_clipped(E_eq_model_global)
   406	
   407	    # Steric chemical potential (Bikerman model) -- ci[mu_h_idx] is the
   408	    # muh-reconstructed c_H, so packing automatically uses the right c_H.
   409	    a_vals_list = [float(v) for v in a_vals]
   410	    steric_a_funcs = [fd.Function(R_space, name=f"steric_a_{i}") for i in range(n)]
   411	    for i in range(n):
   412	        steric_a_funcs[i].assign(float(a_vals_list[i]))
   413	
   414	    # Steric-aware analytic Boltzmann counterion(s) — same Option 2
   415	    # wiring as forms_logc.py: closure expression must enter BOTH
   416	    # Poisson AND the dynamic species' total packing fraction.
   417	    c0_model_for_steric = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)
   418	    steric_boltz = build_steric_boltzmann_expressions(
   419	        ctx=ctx,
   420	        params=params,
   421	        ci=ci,
   422	        a_dyn_funcs=steric_a_funcs,
   423	        a_dyn_floats=a_vals_list,
   424	        c0_dyn=[float(v) for v in c0_model_for_steric[:n]],
   425	        z_dyn=[int(v) for v in z_vals[:n]],
   426	        phi=phi,
   427	        R_space=R_space,
   428	    )
   429	
   430	    steric_active = (
   431	        any(v != 0.0 for v in a_vals_list)
   432	        or bool(steric_boltz)
   433	        or (water_ion_enabled and float(water_bundle.a_oh_const) != 0.0)
   434	    )
   435	    if steric_active:
   436	        packing_floor = float(conv_cfg.get("packing_floor", 1e-8))
   437	        A_dyn = sum(steric_a_funcs[j] * ci[j] for j in range(n))
   438	        if water_ion_enabled and float(water_bundle.a_oh_const) != 0.0:
   439	            # OH⁻ Bikerman packing contribution (shadow species).
   440	            A_dyn = A_dyn + water_bundle.a_oh_const * water_bundle.c_oh_expr
   441	        if steric_boltz:
   442	            # Multi-counterion: shared z_scale, sum packing_contribution
   443	            # over every bikerman bundle.  Single-counterion case (the
   444	            # legacy path) reduces to the same UFL algebra.
   445	            z_scale_shared = steric_boltz[0].z_scale
   446	            packing_total = sum(b.packing_contribution for b in steric_boltz)
   447	            theta_inner = (
   448	                fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn - z_scale_shared * packing_total
   449	            )
   450	        else:
   451	            theta_inner = fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn
   452	        packing = fd.max_value(theta_inner, fd.Constant(packing_floor))
   453	        mu_steric = -fd.ln(packing)
   454	
   455	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   456	    # Residual: Nernst-Planck with muh transform
   457	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   458	    # For non-mu species (u_i = log(c_i)):
   459	    #   J_i = -D_i * c_i * (grad(u_i) + em*z_i*grad(phi))
   460	    # For mu species (mu_H = u_H + em*z_H*phi):
   461	    #   J_H = -D_H * c_H * grad(mu_H)
   462	    # because grad(u_H) + em*z_H*grad(phi) = grad(mu_H) by definition.
   463	    F_res = 0
   464	
   465	    for i in range(n):
   466	        c_i = ci[i]
   467	        c_old = ci_prev[i]
   468	        v = v_list[i]
   469	
   470	        if i in mu_species:
   471	            # mu-species flux: D*c*grad(mu) (+ steric activity).  In muh,
   472	            # the proton's μ_H is the primary, so ∇μ_H_ideal = ∇ui[i].
   473	            ideal_grad = fd.grad(ui[i])
   474	        else:
   475	            # log-c flux: D*c*(grad(u) + em*z*grad(phi))
   476	            drift = fd.Constant(em) * z[i] * phi
   477	            ideal_grad = fd.grad(u_exprs[i]) + fd.grad(drift)
   478	
   479	        if water_ion_enabled and i == h_idx_water:
   480	            # Phase 6α — proton-condition residual on E = c_H − c_OH for
   481	            # the muh backend.  ``ideal_grad`` here is ∇μ_H (the primary).
   482	            mu_steric_grad = fd.grad(mu_steric) if steric_active else None
   483	            Jflux = build_proton_condition_flux(
   484	                bundle=water_bundle,
   485	                D_h=D[i],
   486	                c_h=c_i,
   487	                ideal_grad_h=ideal_grad,
   488	                mu_steric_grad=mu_steric_grad,
   489	                steric_active=steric_active,
   490	            )
   491	            F_res += (
   492	                (water_bundle.e_var_expr - water_bundle.e_var_prev_expr)
   493	                / dt_const
   494	            ) * v * dx
   495	            F_res += fd.dot(Jflux, fd.grad(v)) * dx
   496	            continue
   497	
   498	        if steric_active:
   499	            Jflux = D[i] * c_i * (ideal_grad + fd.grad(mu_steric))
   500	        else:
   501	            Jflux = D[i] * c_i * ideal_grad
   502	
   503	        # Time-stepping residual: (c - c_old)/dt
   504	        F_res += ((c_i - c_old) / dt_const) * v * dx
   505	        F_res += fd.dot(Jflux, fd.grad(v)) * dx
   506	
   507	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   508	    # Butler-Volmer boundary flux
   509	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   510	    # Surface concentrations are c_surf[i] = ci[i] -- already muh-aware
   511	    # because ci[mu_h_idx] is the reconstruction.
   512	    c_surf = ci
   513	
   514	    bv_log_rate = bool(conv_cfg.get("bv_log_rate", False))
   515	
   516	    bv_k0_funcs = []
   517	    bv_alpha_funcs = []
   518	    if use_reactions:
   519	        bv_rate_exprs = []
   520	        rxns_scaled = scaling["bv_reactions"]
   521	        for j, rxn in enumerate(rxns_scaled):
   522	            k0_j = fd.Function(R_space, name=f"bv_k0_rxn{j}")
   523	            k0_j.assign(float(rxn["k0_model"]))
   524	            bv_k0_funcs.append(k0_j)
   525	            alpha_j = fd.Function(R_space, name=f"bv_alpha_rxn{j}")
   526	            alpha_j.assign(float(rxn["alpha"]))
   527	            bv_alpha_funcs.append(alpha_j)
   528	
   529	            # k0 <= 0 OR enabled=False means disabled; skip to avoid fd.ln(0)
   530	            # in log-rate branch. bv_k0_funcs/bv_alpha_funcs are populated
   531	            # above so Stage-4 k0-continuation can still .assign(...) them.
   532	            if float(rxn["k0_model"]) <= 0.0 or bool(rxn.get("enabled", True)) is False:
   533	                R_j = fd.Constant(0.0)
   534	                bv_rate_exprs.append(R_j)
   535	                continue
   536	
   537	            n_e_j = fd.Constant(float(rxn["n_electrons"]))
   538	            cat_idx = rxn["cathodic_species"]
   539	
   540	            # Per-reaction E_eq
   541	            E_eq_j_val = rxn.get("E_eq_model", None)
   542	            if E_eq_j_val is not None and E_eq_j_val != 0.0:
   543	                E_eq_j = fd.Constant(float(E_eq_j_val))
   544	                eta_j = _build_eta_clipped(E_eq_j)
   545	            else:
   546	                eta_j = eta_clipped
   547	
   548	            if bv_log_rate:
   549	                # Cathodic: log_r = ln(k0) + u_cat + sum power*(u_sp - ln c_ref)
   550	                #                   - alpha * n_e * eta_clipped
   551	                # MUH: u_exprs[i] is log(c_i) for both branches (recovered
   552	                # from mu for the proton).
   553	                log_cathodic = (
   554	                    fd.ln(k0_j) + u_exprs[cat_idx]
   555	                    - alpha_j * n_e_j * eta_j
   556	                )
   557	                for factor in rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", []):
   558	                    sp_idx = factor["species"]
   559	                    power = fd.Constant(float(factor["power"]))
   560	                    c_ref_log = fd.ln(fd.Constant(
   561	                        max(float(factor["c_ref_nondim"]), 1e-12)
   562	                    ))
   563	                    log_cathodic = log_cathodic + power * (u_exprs[sp_idx] - c_ref_log)
   564	                cathodic = fd.exp(log_cathodic)
   565	
   566	                # Anodic: log_r = ln(k0) + u_anod + (1-alpha) * n_e * eta_clipped
   567	                if rxn["reversible"] and rxn["anodic_species"] is not None:
   568	                    anod_idx = rxn["anodic_species"]
   569	                    log_anodic = (
   570	                        fd.ln(k0_j) + u_exprs[anod_idx]
   571	                        + (fd.Constant(1.0) - alpha_j) * n_e_j * eta_j
   572	                    )
   573	                    anodic = fd.exp(log_anodic)
   574	                elif rxn["reversible"] and float(rxn["c_ref_model"]) > 1e-30:
   575	                    c_ref_j_log = fd.ln(fd.Constant(float(rxn["c_ref_model"])))
   576	                    log_anodic = (
   577	                        fd.ln(k0_j) + c_ref_j_log
   578	                        + (fd.Constant(1.0) - alpha_j) * n_e_j * eta_j
   579	                    )
   580	                    anodic = fd.exp(log_anodic)
   581	                else:
   582	                    anodic = fd.Constant(0.0)
   583	            else:
   584	                # Cathodic term: k0 * c_cat * exp(-alpha * n_e * eta)
   585	                # c_surf[mu_h_idx] is muh-reconstructed; transparent here.
   586	                cathodic = k0_j * c_surf[cat_idx] * fd.exp(-alpha_j * n_e_j * eta_j)
   587	
   588	                # Cathodic concentration factors
   589	                for factor in rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", []):
   590	                    sp_idx = factor["species"]
   591	                    power = factor["power"]
   592	                    c_ref_f = fd.Constant(max(float(factor["c_ref_nondim"]), 1e-12))
   593	                    cathodic = cathodic * (c_surf[sp_idx] / c_ref_f) ** power
   594	
   595	                # Anodic term (if reversible)
   596	                if rxn["reversible"] and rxn["anodic_species"] is not None:
   597	                    anod_idx = rxn["anodic_species"]
   598	                    anodic = k0_j * c_surf[anod_idx] * fd.exp(
   599	                        (fd.Constant(1.0) - alpha_j) * n_e_j * eta_j
   600	                    )
   601	                elif rxn["reversible"]:
   602	                    c_ref_j = fd.Constant(float(rxn["c_ref_model"]))
   603	                    anodic = k0_j * c_ref_j * fd.exp(
   604	                        (fd.Constant(1.0) - alpha_j) * n_e_j * eta_j
   605	                    )
   606	                else:
   607	                    anodic = fd.Constant(0.0)
   608	
   609	            R_j = cathodic - anodic
   610	            bv_rate_exprs.append(R_j)
   611	
   612	            stoi = rxn["stoichiometry"]
   613	            for i in range(n):
   614	                if stoi[i] != 0:
   615	                    F_res -= fd.Constant(float(stoi[i])) * R_j * v_list[i] * ds(electrode_marker)
   616	
   617	    else:
   618	        # Legacy per-species path (concentration-form BV).  Surface c is
   619	        # via c_surf[i] = ci[i] which is muh-aware.
   620	        bv_rate_exprs = []
   621	        for i in range(n):
   622	            alpha_i = fd.Function(R_space, name=f"bv_alpha_sp{i}")
   623	            alpha_i.assign(float(scaling["bv_alpha_vals"][i]))
   624	            bv_alpha_funcs.append(alpha_i)
   625	            stoi_i = int(scaling["bv_stoichiometry"][i])
   626	            k0_i = fd.Function(R_space, name=f"bv_k0_sp{i}")
   627	            k0_i.assign(float(scaling["bv_k0_model_vals"][i]))
   628	            bv_k0_funcs.append(k0_i)
   629	            c_ref_i = fd.Constant(float(scaling["bv_c_ref_model_vals"][i]))
   630	
   631	            bv_flux_i = k0_i * (
   632	                c_surf[i] * fd.exp(-alpha_i * eta_clipped)
   633	                - c_ref_i * fd.exp((fd.Constant(1.0) - alpha_i) * eta_clipped)
   634	            )
   635	            bv_rate_exprs.append(bv_flux_i)
   636	            F_res -= fd.Constant(float(stoi_i)) * bv_flux_i * v_list[i] * ds(electrode_marker)
   637	
   638	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   639	    # Poisson equation (uses c_i = exp(...) -- ci[mu_h_idx] is muh-reconstructed)
   640	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   641	    suppress_poisson_source = _bool(nondim_cfg.get("suppress_poisson_source", False))
   642	    eps_coeff = fd.Constant(float(scaling["poisson_coefficient"]))
   643	    charge_rhs = fd.Constant(float(scaling["charge_rhs_prefactor"]))
   644	    F_res += eps_coeff * fd.dot(fd.grad(phi), fd.grad(w)) * dx
   645	    if not suppress_poisson_source:
   646	        F_res -= charge_rhs * sum(z[i] * ci[i] * w for i in range(n)) * dx
   647	        if water_ion_enabled:
   648	            # OH⁻ Poisson contribution (z = −1).
   649	            F_res -= charge_rhs * (
   650	                fd.Constant(-1.0) * water_bundle.c_oh_expr
   651	            ) * w * dx
   652	        if steric_boltz:
   653	            # Bikerman counterion charge density: shared z_scale, sum
   654	            # charge_density across every bundle.  Single-counterion
   655	            # case reduces to the same UFL algebra as the legacy path.
   656	            z_scale_shared = steric_boltz[0].z_scale
   657	            charge_density_total = sum(b.charge_density for b in steric_boltz)
   658	            F_res -= (
   659	                z_scale_shared * charge_rhs * charge_density_total * w * dx
   660	            )
   661	
   662	    # Stern layer Robin BC.  Phase 6β v9 Gate 2: ``stern_coeff`` is
   663	    # promoted to the ctx so the C_S continuation ladder in
   664	    # ``solve_anchor_with_continuation`` can reassign it via
   665	    # ``set_stern_capacitance_model``.
   666	    if use_stern:
   667	        stern_coeff = fd.Constant(float(stern_capacitance_model))
   668	        F_res -= stern_coeff * (phi_applied_func - phi) * w * ds(electrode_marker)
   669	    else:
   670	        stern_coeff = None
   671	
   672	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   673	    # Phase 6β v9 Gate 3 — cation hydrolysis (Γ as external coefficient)
   674	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   675	    cation_hydrolysis_bundle = None
   676	    if is_cation_hydrolysis_enabled(conv_cfg):
   677	        h_idx_for_cation = (
   678	            h_idx_water
   679	            if water_ion_enabled
   680	            else resolve_h_index(list(z_vals), roles=species_roles)
   681	        )
   682	        cation_hydrolysis_bundle = build_cation_hydrolysis_terms(
   683	            ctx=ctx,
   684	            conv_cfg=conv_cfg,
   685	            z_vals=z_vals,
   686	            roles=species_roles,
   687	            h_idx=h_idx_for_cation,
   688	            R_space=R_space,
   689	        )
   690	
   691	        # σ_S for the Singh formula — bare Stern surface charge per R4#5
   692	        # in **physical** C/m² (Singh's Eq. (4) is unit-specific).
   693	        if stern_coeff is not None:
   694	            from Nondim.constants import FARADAY_CONSTANT as _F
   695	            length_scale = float(scaling.get("length_scale_m", 1.0))
   696	            concentration_scale = float(
   697	                scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
   698	            )
   699	            sigma_phys_per_nondim = float(_F) * concentration_scale * length_scale
   700	            sigma_S_expr = (
   701	                stern_coeff
   702	                * (phi_applied_func - phi)
   703	                * fd.Constant(sigma_phys_per_nondim)
   704	            )
   705	        else:
   706	            sigma_S_expr = fd.Constant(0.0)
   707	        ctx["_cation_hydrolysis_sigma_S_expr"] = sigma_S_expr
   708	
   709	        # On the muh backend the proton primary is mu_H, but the
   710	        # boundary concentration we want is c_H = exp(u_exprs[mu_h_idx])
   711	        # which is ci[mu_h_idx] — same convention as Phase 6α.
   712	        c_M_bdy_expr = ci[cation_hydrolysis_bundle.counterion_idx]
   713	        c_H_bdy_expr = ci[h_idx_for_cation]
   714	
   715	        # Phase 6β step 6 plumbing-ablation flags — see
   716	        # Forward/bv_solver/config.py for cross-validation rules
   717	        # (manufactured_R_inj required when half-physical;
   718	        # override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2 mutually exclusive with
   719	        # manufactured_R_inj).
   720	        manufactured_R_inj = conv_cfg.get("manufactured_R_inj", None)
   721	        apply_h_source = bool(conv_cfg.get("apply_h_source", True))
   722	        apply_k_sink = bool(conv_cfg.get("apply_k_sink", True))
   723	        sigma_singh_override = conv_cfg.get(
   724	            "override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2", None
   725	        )
   726	
   727	        if sigma_singh_override is not None:
   728	            # σ_singh_post_clamp = max(0, -σ_S_signed) · 6.2415e-6.
   729	            # To force σ_singh_post_clamp = override (counts/pm²),
   730	            # pass σ_S_signed = -override / 6.2415e-6 (C/m², negative
   731	            # ⇒ cathodic) so the existing anode clamp + conversion
   732	            # in build_pka_shift collapse to the override.
   733	            inv_factor_C_m2_per_count_pm2 = 1.602176634e-19 / 1.0e-24
   734	            fake_signed_sigma_S = fd.Constant(
   735	                -float(sigma_singh_override) * inv_factor_C_m2_per_count_pm2
   736	            )
   737	            pka_shift_expr = build_pka_shift(
   738	                cation_params=cation_hydrolysis_bundle.cation_params,
   739	                sigma_S=fake_signed_sigma_S,
   740	                r_H_El_func=cation_hydrolysis_bundle.r_H_El_pm_func,
