     1	"""Analytic Boltzmann counterion contribution to Poisson's equation.
     2	
     3	When a supporting electrolyte ion is inert (does not participate in any
     4	electrode reaction) it can be removed from the dynamic Nernst--Planck
     5	system and replaced by an analytic Boltzmann profile in equilibrium with
     6	the electrostatic potential.
     7	
     8	Two variants are supported per-counterion via ``steric_mode``:
     9	
    10	    "ideal" (default, legacy):
    11	        c(x) = c_bulk * exp(-z * phi(x))   — unbounded.
    12	
    13	    "bikerman":
    14	        c(x) = c_b * exp(-z * phi)
    15	               * (1 - A_dyn(x)) / (theta_b + a_b * c_b * exp(-z * phi))
    16	
    17	        where A_dyn(x) = sum_j a_j * c_j(x) over dynamic species, and
    18	        theta_b = 1 - sum_j a_j * c_b_j - a_b * c_b is the bulk packing
    19	        fraction.  This is the steady-state algebraic reduction of the
    20	        4sp dynamic Bikerman problem for an inert counterion under the
    21	        sign-corrected Bikerman chemical potential
    22	        ``mu_i = ln(c_i) + z_i*phi - ln(theta)``.  See
    23	        ``docs/steric_analytic_clo4_reduction_handoff.md`` for the full
    24	        derivation.
    25	
    26	This module provides:
    27	    - ``add_boltzmann_counterion_residual`` for the legacy ideal path
    28	      (mutates Poisson residual after ``build_forms_logc`` returns).
    29	    - ``build_steric_boltzmann_expressions`` for the bikerman path
    30	      (returns UFL expressions called from inside ``build_forms_logc``
    31	      so the closure enters BOTH the dynamic-species packing and the
    32	      Poisson source).
    33	
    34	The sign convention matches the Poisson residual built by the forms
    35	modules:
    36	
    37	    F_poisson  =  eps * grad(phi) . grad(w) * dx
    38	                  - charge_rhs * sum_i z_i * c_i * w * dx
    39	                  - charge_rhs * sum_k z_k * c_steric_k * w * dx
    40	                                                  (analytic counterions)
    41	"""
    42	
    43	from __future__ import annotations
    44	
    45	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    46	from typing import Any
    47	
    48	import firedrake as fd
    49	
    50	from .config import _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg
    51	from .forms_indexing import unpack_dof_indices
    52	
    53	
    54	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    55	class StericBoltzmannBundle:
    56	    """UFL expressions and metadata for one steric-aware Boltzmann counterion.
    57	
    58	    Attributes
    59	    ----------
    60	    c_steric_expr
    61	        UFL expression for the steric-aware analytic concentration
    62	        ``c_b * q * (1 - A_dyn) / (theta_b + a_b * c_b * q)`` where
    63	        ``q = exp(-z * phi_clamped)``.  Caller can extract surface
    64	        values for diagnostics.
    65	    packing_contribution
    66	        UFL expression for ``a_b * c_steric``.  Caller adds this to
    67	        ``theta = 1 - A_dyn - packing_contribution`` so the dynamic
    68	        species' steric chemical potential includes the counterion.
    69	    charge_density
    70	        UFL expression for ``z * c_steric`` (NOT yet multiplied by
    71	        ``charge_rhs`` or ``z_scale``).  Caller adds
    72	        ``-charge_rhs * z_scale * charge_density * w * dx`` to the
    73	        Poisson residual.
    74	    z_scale
    75	        R-space ``Function`` shared with any ideal-mode counterions on
    76	        the same ``ctx`` (key ``'boltzmann_z_scale'``).  Default 1.0;
    77	        Strategy-B orchestrators ramp this alongside the dynamic
    78	        species' z-ramp (see ``add_boltzmann_counterion_residual``
    79	        docstring).
    80	    metadata
    81	        Diagnostic info (z, c_bulk_nondim, a_nondim, phi_clamp,
    82	        theta_b, config_index) used by the diagnostics layer.
    83	    """
    84	    c_steric_expr: Any
    85	    packing_contribution: Any
    86	    charge_density: Any
    87	    z_scale: Any
    88	    metadata: dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    89	
    90	
    91	def build_steric_boltzmann_expressions(
    92	    *,
    93	    ctx: dict[str, Any],
    94	    params: Any,
    95	    ci: list,
    96	    a_dyn_funcs: list,
    97	    a_dyn_floats: list[float],
    98	    c0_dyn: list[float],
    99	    z_dyn: list[int],
   100	    phi: Any,
   101	    R_space: Any,
   102	) -> list[StericBoltzmannBundle]:
   103	    """Build UFL closure expressions for steric-aware Boltzmann counterions.
   104	
   105	    Returns an empty list when no entries have ``steric_mode='bikerman'``.
   106	    The legacy single-counterion case (len == 1) reduces to the same
   107	    UFL algebra it always built; the bundle list contains exactly one
   108	    element. The multi-counterion shared-theta closure (plan §2.1)
   109	    extends this:
   110	
   111	    .. code-block:: text
   112	
   113	        For each analytic ion k (steric):
   114	          c_k(φ) = c_b_k · exp(-z_k·φ) · (1 - A_dyn(φ))
   115	                       / (θ_b + Σ_k' a_k' · c_b_k' · exp(-z_k'·φ))
   116	
   117	        with A_dyn(φ) = Σ_dyn a_i · c_i_dyn(φ)
   118	             θ_b      = 1 - A_dyn_bulk - Σ_k a_k · c_b_k
   119	
   120	    The denominator is the same for every steric ion (shared theta);
   121	    no coupled local NL solve needed.
   122	
   123	    Validates:
   124	        - ``θ_b > 0`` for the bulk (sum over ALL bikerman entries);
   125	          raises ``ValueError`` with a descriptive message otherwise.
   126	        - No double-counting: no bikerman entry's (z, c_bulk) may
   127	          duplicate any dynamic species' (z, c_bulk) within ``1e-9``
   128	          relative tolerance.
   129	
   130	    The (re)used ``ctx['boltzmann_z_scale']`` Function is the same
   131	    R-space scaling used by the legacy ideal path; both ideal and
   132	    bikerman counterions share it on the same ctx, so a single
   133	    ``_set_z_factor`` call ramps every contribution.
   134	
   135	    Returns
   136	    -------
   137	    list[StericBoltzmannBundle]
   138	        Empty list when no bikerman entries.  Otherwise one bundle per
   139	        bikerman counterion.  All bundles share the same z_scale.
   140	    """
   141	    counterions = _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params)
   142	    bikerman = [(j, e) for j, e in enumerate(counterions)
   143	                if e.get("steric_mode", "ideal") == "bikerman"]
   144	    if not bikerman:
   145	        return []
   146	
   147	    if not (len(a_dyn_floats) == len(c0_dyn) == len(z_dyn) == len(ci) == len(a_dyn_funcs)):
   148	        raise ValueError(
   149	            "build_steric_boltzmann_expressions: dynamic-species inputs misaligned "
   150	            f"(a_dyn_floats={len(a_dyn_floats)}, c0_dyn={len(c0_dyn)}, "
   151	            f"z_dyn={len(z_dyn)}, ci={len(ci)}, a_dyn_funcs={len(a_dyn_funcs)})"
   152	        )
   153	
   154	    # ----- bulk-side validation across ALL bikerman entries -----
   155	    A_dyn_bulk = sum(a * c for a, c in zip(a_dyn_floats, c0_dyn))
   156	    A_an_bulk = sum(
   157	        float(e["a_nondim"]) * float(e["c_bulk_nondim"]) for _, e in bikerman
   158	    )
   159	    theta_b = 1.0 - A_dyn_bulk - A_an_bulk
   160	    if theta_b <= 0.0:
   161	        bm_str = ", ".join(
   162	            f"a={float(e['a_nondim']):.4g}*c_b={float(e['c_bulk_nondim']):.4g}"
   163	            for _, e in bikerman
   164	        )
   165	        raise ValueError(
   166	            f"bikerman multi-counterion closure requires theta_b > 0, but got "
   167	            f"theta_b = 1 - A_dyn_bulk - sum(a_k*c_b_k) "
   168	            f"= 1 - {A_dyn_bulk:.6g} - {A_an_bulk:.6g} = {theta_b:.6g}; "
   169	            f"bikerman entries: [{bm_str}]; reduce dynamic-species packing, "
   170	            f"per-ion a_nondim, or per-ion c_bulk_nondim."
   171	        )
   172	
   173	    # Double-counting guard against EVERY dynamic species AND
   174	    # within-bikerman duplication (e.g. user lists Cs+ twice).
   175	    rel_tol = 1e-9
   176	    for k_idx, (j, entry) in enumerate(bikerman):
   177	        z_k = int(entry["z"])
   178	        c_k = float(entry["c_bulk_nondim"])
   179	        for i in range(len(c0_dyn)):
   180	            same_z = z_dyn[i] == z_k
   181	            denom = max(abs(c0_dyn[i]), abs(c_k), 1e-300)
   182	            same_c = abs(c0_dyn[i] - c_k) <= rel_tol * denom
   183	            if same_z and same_c:
   184	                raise ValueError(
   185	                    f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}] (z={z_k}, c_bulk={c_k}) "
   186	                    f"duplicates dynamic species[{i}] (z={z_dyn[i]}, "
   187	                    f"c_bulk={c0_dyn[i]}); remove from one or the other to "
   188	                    f"avoid double-counting in Poisson and steric packing."
   189	                )
   190	        for k2_idx, (j2, entry2) in enumerate(bikerman):
   191	            if k2_idx <= k_idx:
   192	                continue
   193	            z_k2 = int(entry2["z"])
   194	            c_k2 = float(entry2["c_bulk_nondim"])
   195	            denom = max(abs(c_k), abs(c_k2), 1e-300)
   196	            if z_k == z_k2 and abs(c_k - c_k2) <= rel_tol * denom:
   197	                raise ValueError(
   198	                    f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}] and [{j2}] duplicate "
   199	                    f"(z={z_k}, c_bulk={c_k}); remove one to avoid "
   200	                    f"double-counting."
   201	                )
   202	
   203	    # ----- shared UFL pieces (denominator + dynamic packing factor) -----
   204	    A_dyn_local = sum(a_dyn_funcs[i] * ci[i] for i in range(len(ci)))
   205	    free_dyn_floor = fd.Constant(1e-10)   # FE-interpolation safety on coarse meshes
   206	    free_dyn = fd.max_value(fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn_local, free_dyn_floor)
   207	    theta_b_const = fd.Constant(theta_b)
   208	
   209	    # Per-bikerman exponent uses each ion's OWN phi_clamp (each entry
   210	    # may set its own conservative clamp).  The SHARED denominator sums
   211	    # a_k * c_b_k * exp(-z_k * phi_clamped_k) — using each ion's clamp
   212	    # for its own term inside the sum is consistent with the closure
   213	    # derivation (the clamp only ever appears multiplied by that ion's
   214	    # z_k anyway, so the per-ion clamp is the right cap).
   215	    per_ion_q = []
   216	    for k_idx, (j, entry) in enumerate(bikerman):
   217	        z_k = int(entry["z"])
   218	        c_k = float(entry["c_bulk_nondim"])
   219	        a_k = float(entry["a_nondim"])
   220	        phi_clamp_k = float(entry["phi_clamp"])
   221	        z_k_const = fd.Constant(float(z_k))
   222	        c_k_const = fd.Constant(c_k)
   223	        a_k_const = fd.Constant(a_k)
   224	        phi_clamped_k = fd.min_value(
   225	            fd.max_value(phi, fd.Constant(-phi_clamp_k)),
   226	            fd.Constant(phi_clamp_k),
   227	        )
   228	        q_k = fd.exp(-z_k_const * phi_clamped_k)
   229	        per_ion_q.append({
   230	            "z_const": z_k_const,
   231	            "c_const": c_k_const,
   232	            "a_const": a_k_const,
   233	            "q": q_k,
   234	            "z": z_k,
   235	            "c_bulk": c_k,
   236	            "a_nondim": a_k,
   237	            "phi_clamp": phi_clamp_k,
   238	            "config_index": j,
   239	        })
   240	
   241	    denom = theta_b_const + sum(p["a_const"] * p["c_const"] * p["q"]
   242	                                for p in per_ion_q)
   243	
   244	    # Shared z_scale Function — single producer / single consumer.
   245	    if "boltzmann_z_scale" in ctx:
   246	        z_scale = ctx["boltzmann_z_scale"]
   247	    else:
   248	        z_scale = fd.Function(R_space, name="boltzmann_z_scale")
   249	        z_scale.assign(1.0)
   250	        ctx["boltzmann_z_scale"] = z_scale
   251	
   252	    bundles: list[StericBoltzmannBundle] = []
   253	    for p in per_ion_q:
   254	        c_steric_k = p["c_const"] * p["q"] * free_dyn / denom
   255	        bundles.append(StericBoltzmannBundle(
   256	            c_steric_expr=c_steric_k,
   257	            packing_contribution=p["a_const"] * c_steric_k,
   258	            charge_density=p["z_const"] * c_steric_k,
   259	            z_scale=z_scale,
   260	            metadata={
   261	                "config_index": p["config_index"],
   262	                "z": p["z"],
   263	                "c_bulk_nondim": p["c_bulk"],
   264	                "a_nondim": p["a_nondim"],
   265	                "phi_clamp": p["phi_clamp"],
   266	                "theta_b": theta_b,
   267	            },
   268	        ))
   269	    return bundles
   270	
   271	
   272	def add_boltzmann_counterion_residual(
   273	    ctx: dict[str, Any],
   274	    params: Any,
   275	    *,
   276	    skip_bikerman: bool = False,
   277	) -> int:
   278	    """Append analytic-Boltzmann counterion residuals to ``ctx['F_res']``.
   279	
   280	    Looks up ``params['bv_bc']['boltzmann_counterions']`` (parsed via
   281	    :func:`_get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg`).  When non-empty, mutates
   282	    ``ctx`` in place by:
   283	
   284	        - extending ``F_res`` with one Poisson source term per counterion
   285	          (sign and prefactor matching the existing Poisson residual);
   286	        - re-deriving ``J_form`` from the updated residual;
   287	        - storing the parsed config under ``ctx['boltzmann_counterions']``;
   288	        - storing a mutable scaling Constant under
   289	          ``ctx['boltzmann_z_scale']``.
   290	
   291	    The ``boltzmann_z_scale`` is an R-space Function (default ``1.0`` so
   292	    standalone usage is unchanged) that orchestrators use to *ramp the
   293	    counterion's contribution alongside* the dynamic-species z-ramp.
   294	    Without this scale, when ``solve_grid_with_charge_continuation``
   295	    Phase 1 sets the dynamic species' ``z_consts`` to zero to compute a
   296	    voltage-only neutral sweep, the analytic counterion would still
   297	    contribute its full ``z = -1`` charge to Poisson, leaving the bulk
   298	    non-electroneutral and breaking the V-sweep bisection.  Setting
   299	    ``boltzmann_z_scale = 0`` during Phase 1 (then ramping to 1 in
   300	    Phase 2 alongside ``z_consts``) keeps Phase 1 truly neutral.
   301	
   302	    Parameters
   303	    ----------
   304	    ctx : dict
   305	        Context produced by ``build_forms`` / ``build_forms_logc``.  Must
   306	        contain ``F_res``, ``U``, ``W``, ``mesh``, and ``nondim``.
   307	    params : dict
   308	        The 11-tuple's params dict (``solver_params[10]``).
   309	
   310	    Returns
   311	    -------
   312	    int
   313	        Number of Boltzmann counterion entries added.  ``0`` is a no-op.
   314	    """
   315	    counterions = _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params)
   316	    if not counterions:
   317	        return 0
   318	
   319	    if "F_res" not in ctx or "U" not in ctx or "W" not in ctx:
   320	        raise ValueError(

exec

   740	                r_H_El_func=cation_hydrolysis_bundle.r_H_El_pm_func,
   741	                beta_offset_pm2_func=cation_hydrolysis_bundle.beta_offset_pm2_func,
   742	            )
   743	            pka_sigma_S_for_storage = fake_signed_sigma_S
   744	        else:

   746	                cation_params=cation_hydrolysis_bundle.cation_params,
   747	                sigma_S=sigma_S_expr,

   753	        if manufactured_R_inj is not None:

   766	        # λ=0 this restores the disabled-feature baseline up to

   768	        # so they can be stored on ctx for diagnostic / consistency

   771	        lam_func = cation_hydrolysis_bundle.lambda_hydrolysis_func

   777	        K_residual_term = (

   782	        R_net_scalar_form = lam_func * R_net * ds(electrode_marker)
   783	        H_flux_scalar_form = R_net_scalar_form
   784	        K_flux_scalar_form = lam_func * (-R_net) * ds(electrode_marker)
   785	
   786	        if apply_h_source:
   787	            F_res -= H_residual_term
   788	        if apply_k_sink:
   789	            F_res -= K_residual_term
   790	
   791	        # Step 6 canonical artifacts — single source of truth for
   792	        # diagnostics, Picard, and slow slot-wiring tests.  Inserted
   793	        # into ctx via the ctx.update block below.
   794	        _step6_cation_hydrolysis_artifacts = {
   795	            "_cation_hydrolysis_R_net_expr": R_net,
   796	            "_cation_hydrolysis_pka_shift_expr": pka_shift_expr,
   797	            "_cation_hydrolysis_pka_sigma_S_expr": pka_sigma_S_for_storage,
   798	            "_cation_hydrolysis_H_residual_term": H_residual_term,
   799	            "_cation_hydrolysis_K_residual_term": K_residual_term,
   800	            "_cation_hydrolysis_R_net_scalar_form": R_net_scalar_form,
   801	            "_cation_hydrolysis_H_flux_scalar_form": H_flux_scalar_form,
   802	            "_cation_hydrolysis_K_flux_scalar_form": K_flux_scalar_form,
   803	        }
   804	    else:
   805	        _step6_cation_hydrolysis_artifacts = {}
   806	
   807	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   808	    # Boundary conditions
   809	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   810	    # Concentration BCs:
   811	    #   non-mu species:  u_i        = ln(c0_i)
   812	    #   mu species:      mu_H_bulk  = ln(c0_H) + em*z_H*phi_bulk
   813	    #

   815	    # the bulk for Stern) is where phi = 0 by construction, so the muh BC
   816	    # value is numerically identical to ln(c0_H).  The explicit em*z*0
   817	    # term is kept for documentation -- a future Robin or non-zero bulk
   818	    # phi would activate it.
   819	    c0_model = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)
   820	    _C_FLOOR = 1e-20
   821	    bc_phi_ground = fd.DirichletBC(W.sub(n), fd.Constant(0.0), ground_marker)
   822	    bc_ui = []
   823	    phi_bulk_at_ground = 0.0  # by Dirichlet at ground_marker
   824	    for i in range(n):
   825	        c0_i = max(float(c0_model[i]), _C_FLOOR)
   826	        if i in mu_species:
   827	            bc_val = fd.Constant(
   828	                np.log(c0_i) + em * float(z_vals[i]) * phi_bulk_at_ground
   829	            )
   830	        else:
   831	            bc_val = fd.Constant(np.log(c0_i))
   832	        bc_ui.append(fd.DirichletBC(W.sub(i), bc_val, concentration_marker))
   833	    if use_stern:
   834	        bcs = bc_ui + [bc_phi_ground]
   835	    else:
   836	        bc_phi_electrode = fd.DirichletBC(W.sub(n), phi_applied_func, electrode_marker)
   837	        bcs = bc_ui + [bc_phi_electrode, bc_phi_ground]
   838	
   839	    J_form = fd.derivative(F_res, U)
   840	
   841	    ctx.update({
   842	        "F_res": F_res,
   843	        "J_form": J_form,
   844	        "bcs": bcs,
   845	        "logD_funcs": m,
   846	        "D_consts": D,
   847	        "z_consts": z,
   848	        "dt_const": dt_const,
   849	        "phi_applied_func": phi_applied_func,
   850	        "phi0_func": phi0_func,
   851	        "bv_settings": bv_cfg,
   852	        "bv_convergence": conv_cfg,
   853	        "bv_rate_exprs": bv_rate_exprs,
   854	        "bv_k0_funcs": bv_k0_funcs,
   855	        "bv_alpha_funcs": bv_alpha_funcs,
   856	        "steric_a_funcs": steric_a_funcs,
   857	        "nondim": scaling,
   858	        "use_stern": use_stern,
   859	        # Phase 6β v9 Gate 2: live FE Constant for the Stern capacitance
   860	        # in nondim units.  None when use_stern is False.  Allows
   861	        # set_stern_capacitance_model() to update the residual without a
   862	        # form rebuild.
   863	        "stern_coeff_const": stern_coeff,
   864	        "ci_exprs": ci,
   865	        "u_exprs": u_exprs,           # NEW: log(c_i) for diagnostics in muh runs
   866	        "mu_species": list(mu_species),  # NEW: which raw U.sub(i) is mu, not u
   867	        "logc_transform": True,        # downstream code may key off this
   868	        "logc_muh_transform": True,    # NEW: muh-specific code path flag
   869	        # Diagnostic metadata mirroring forms_logc.py.
   870	        "_diag_bv_exp_scale": float(bv_exp_scale),
   871	        "_diag_exponent_clip": float(conv_cfg["exponent_clip"]),
   872	        "_diag_eps_c": float(conv_cfg.get("conc_floor", 1e-8)),
   873	        "steric_boltzmann": steric_boltz,
   874	        "water_ionization": water_bundle,  # None when feature disabled
   875	        "cation_hydrolysis": cation_hydrolysis_bundle,  # None when feature disabled
   876	    })
   877	    # Phase 6β step 6 — canonical cation-hydrolysis artifacts.
   878	    ctx.update(_step6_cation_hydrolysis_artifacts)
   879	    # Ideal-path Boltzmann counterions (bikerman entries handled above
   880	    # by build_steric_boltzmann_expressions).
   881	    add_boltzmann_counterion_residual(ctx, params, skip_bikerman=True)
   882	    return ctx
   883	
   884	
   885	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   886	# Initial conditions
   887	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   888	
   889	def set_initial_conditions_logc_muh(ctx: dict[str, Any], solver_params: Any) -> None:
   890	    """Linear-phi IC for the muh formulation.
   891	
   892	    Sets:
   893	
   894	      non-mu species:   u_i(y) = ln(c0_i)              (constant, same as logc)
   895	      mu species:       mu_H(y) = ln(c0_H) + em*z_H*phi_init(y)
   896	      phi:              phi_init(y) = phi_surface * (1 - y)
   897	
   898	    Pointwise reconstruction of c_H from these IC fields recovers
   899	    c_H_bulk exactly when phi_o_bulk = 0:
   900	
   901	      exp(mu_H(y) - em*z_H*phi(y)) = c_H_bulk * exp(-em*z_H*(phi(y) - phi_init(y)))
   902	
   903	    For Stern-aware configs, ``phi_surface = phi_applied - psi_S``
   904	    instead of ``phi_applied`` (Phase F fix; see forms_logc.py
   905	    counterpart for full rationale).
   906	    """
   907	    from .picard_ic import solve_stern_split
   908	
   909	    try:
   910	        n_species, order, dt, t_end, z_vals, D_vals, a_vals, phi_applied, c0, phi0, params = solver_params
   911	    except Exception as exc:
   912	        raise ValueError("bv_solver expects a list of 11 solver parameters") from exc
   913	
   914	    mesh = ctx["mesh"]
   915	    U_prev = ctx["U_prev"]
   916	    n = ctx["n_species"]
   917	    scaling = ctx.get("nondim", {})
   918	
   919	    c0_raw = [float(v) for v in ([c0] * n if np.isscalar(c0) else list(c0))][:n]
   920	    c0_model = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)

exec
/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba scripts/verification/mms_bv_3sp_logc_boltzmann.py | sed -n '260,620p'" in /Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse
 succeeded in 0ms:
   260	            / (fd.Constant(theta_b_steric)
   261	               + fd.Constant(a_b_steric * c_b_steric) * q_manuf)
   262	        )
   263	        packing_manuf = (
   264	            fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn_manuf
   265	            - fd.Constant(a_b_steric) * c_steric_manuf
   266	        )
   267	    else:
   268	        c_steric_manuf = None
   269	        packing_manuf = fd.Constant(1.0) - sum(
   270	            fd.Constant(a_vals_float[i]) * c_exact[i] for i in range(n)
   271	        )
   272	    mu_steric_manuf = -fd.ln(packing_manuf)
   273	
   274	    # --- Manufactured fluxes J_i = D_i * c_i * (grad u + em z grad phi + grad mu_steric) ---
   275	    # NOTE: forms_logc.py line 287-291 uses the log-c-friendly form
   276	    #   Jflux = D[i] * c_i * (grad(u_i) + grad(em*z_i*phi) + grad(mu_steric))
   277	    # mathematically equivalent to D*(grad(c) + em*z*c*grad(phi) + c*grad(mu_steric))
   278	    # since c*grad(u) = grad(c) and c*grad(em*z*phi) = em*z*c*grad(phi).
   279	    # Wrap em*z_i as fd.Constant so z_i = 0 species keep mesh-aware UFL terms
   280	    # (a Python float 0.0 multiplied into a UFL expression simplifies to scalar 0
   281	    # and fd.grad(0) fails to find the geometric dimension).
   282	    em_z_const = [fd.Constant(em * z_vals_float[i]) for i in range(n)]
   283	    J_manuf = [
   284	        D_model[i] * c_exact[i] * (
   285	            fd.grad(u_exact[i])
   286	            + em_z_const[i] * fd.grad(phi_exact)
   287	            + fd.grad(mu_steric_manuf)
   288	        )
   289	        for i in range(n)
   290	    ]
   291	
   292	    # --- Manufactured BV rates (log-rate form, mirror of forms_logc.py:334-366) ---
   293	    rxns = scaling["bv_reactions"]
   294	    R_manuf = []
   295	    for j_idx, rxn in enumerate(rxns):
   296	        k0 = float(rxn["k0_model"])
   297	        alpha = float(rxn["alpha"])
   298	        n_e = float(rxn["n_electrons"])
   299	        cat_idx = rxn["cathodic_species"]
   300	        E_eq_j_model = float(rxn.get("E_eq_model", 0.0))
   301	        # eta is *spatially constant* on the electrode (depends only on
   302	        # phi_applied_func, not phi).  forms_logc.py line 235-241 uses
   303	        # use_eta_in_bv=True path: eta_raw = phi_applied_func - E_eq.
   304	        eta_j = bv_exp_scale * (phi_app_model - E_eq_j_model)
   305	        if clip_source:
   306	            # Mirror the production eta-clip so the source assumes the same
   307	            # numeric eta as the discrete operator -- isolates discrete
   308	            # truncation error from clip-induced model error.
   309	            eta_j = max(min(eta_j, 50.0), -50.0)
   310	
   311	        log_cath = log(k0) + u_exact[cat_idx] - alpha * n_e * eta_j
   312	        for f in rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", []):
   313	            sp_idx = f["species"]
   314	            power = float(f["power"])
   315	            c_ref_f = max(float(f["c_ref_nondim"]), 1e-12)
   316	            log_cath = log_cath + power * (u_exact[sp_idx] - log(c_ref_f))
   317	        cathodic = fd.exp(log_cath)
   318	
   319	        if rxn["reversible"] and rxn["anodic_species"] is not None:
   320	            anod_idx = rxn["anodic_species"]
   321	            log_anod = log(k0) + u_exact[anod_idx] + (1.0 - alpha) * n_e * eta_j
   322	            anodic = fd.exp(log_anod)
   323	        elif rxn["reversible"] and float(rxn.get("c_ref_model", 0.0)) > 1e-30:
   324	            c_ref_j = float(rxn["c_ref_model"])
   325	            log_anod = log(k0) + log(c_ref_j) + (1.0 - alpha) * n_e * eta_j
   326	            anodic = fd.exp(log_anod)
   327	        else:
   328	            anodic = fd.Constant(0.0)
   329	
   330	        R_manuf.append(cathodic - anodic)
   331	
   332	    # --- Test functions and measures (high quadrature for non-polynomial integrands) ---
   333	    v_tests = fd.TestFunctions(W)
   334	    v_list = v_tests[:-1]
   335	    w_test = v_tests[-1]
   336	    n_vec = fd.FacetNormal(mesh)
   337	    dx_q = fd.dx(domain=mesh, degree=SRC_QUAD_DEGREE)
   338	    ds_q = fd.ds(domain=mesh, degree=SRC_QUAD_DEGREE)
   339	
   340	    bv_settings = ctx["bv_settings"]
   341	    electrode_marker = bv_settings["electrode_marker"]
   342	
   343	    # --- Inject sources into F_res ---
   344	    # Pattern: production residual term ``+ ∫ X · v · dx`` requires source
   345	    # ``- ∫ X_continuum_at_u_exact · v · dx`` to make u_exact a continuum
   346	    # solution.  We use the divergence theorem to write everything in
   347	    # divergence form on dx + boundary on ds.
   348	    F_res = ctx["F_res"]
   349	
   350	    for i in range(n):
   351	        # NP interior source.  Production: +∫ J_i · ∇v_i · dx
   352	        # IBP:  +∫ J_i · ∇v_i dx  =  -∫ div(J_i) v_i dx + ∫ J_i·n v_i ds_boundary
   353	        # Continuum residual at u_exact: -div(J_manuf_i) on interior,
   354	        # J_manuf_i·n - sum_j s_ij R_manuf_j on electrode, J_manuf_i·n on bulk side.
   355	        # The bulk side has Dirichlet BC so v_i = 0 there; only electrode + bulk
   356	        # natural-BC sides contribute.  All sides except electrode have zero
   357	        # natural BC in production (no flux on x-walls; concentration BC on bulk).
   358	        # Inject sources for interior and electrode only.
   359	        S_c_i = -fd.div(J_manuf[i])
   360	        F_res -= S_c_i * v_list[i] * dx_q
   361	
   362	        # Electrode boundary correction:
   363	        #   ∫ J_i·n v_i ds_elec - ∫ Σ s_ij R_j v_i ds_elec  ===> needs
   364	        # source g_i = J_manuf_i·n - Σ s_ij R_manuf_j on electrode.
   365	        flux_outward = fd.dot(J_manuf[i], n_vec)
   366	        bv_sum = sum(
   367	            float(rxns[j_idx]["stoichiometry"][i]) * R_manuf[j_idx]
   368	            for j_idx in range(len(rxns))
   369	            if rxns[j_idx]["stoichiometry"][i] != 0
   370	        )
   371	        # If no reaction touches species i, bv_sum is 0; flux_outward source still applies.
   372	        if isinstance(bv_sum, int) and bv_sum == 0:
   373	            bv_sum = fd.Constant(0.0)
   374	        g_i = flux_outward - bv_sum
   375	        F_res -= g_i * v_list[i] * ds_q(electrode_marker)
   376	
   377	    # --- Poisson source ---
   378	    # Production residual (signs match forms_logc.py + boltzmann.py):
   379	    #   F_res += eps * grad(phi) . grad(w) * dx
   380	    #   F_res -= charge_rhs * sum_i z_i * c_i * w * dx
   381	    #   F_res -= z_scale * charge_rhs * z_C * c_bulk * exp(-z_C * phi_clamped) * w * dx
   382	    #
   383	    # IBP first: eps * grad(phi) . grad(w) dx = -eps * lap(phi) * w dx + boundary.
   384	    # On Dirichlet boundaries (electrode + bulk for phi) w=0; on x-walls natural
   385	    # BC has grad(phi).n = 0 for our manufactured phi (cos(pi x) vanishes derivatively).
   386	    # So F_res_phi at u_manuf integrates to:
   387	    #   ∫ [ -eps*lap(phi_manuf) - charge_rhs*Σ z_i c_i_manuf
   388	    #       - charge_rhs * Σ_k z_k c_bulk_k * exp(-z_k phi_manuf) ] * w * dx
   389	    # which we want to make zero by subtracting that integrand as a source.
   390	    S_phi = (
   391	        -eps * fd.div(fd.grad(phi_exact))
   392	        - charge_rhs * sum(z_vals_float[i] * c_exact[i] for i in range(n))
   393	    )
   394	    if bikerman_counterion is not None:
   395	        # Bikerman closure replaces the ideal Boltzmann source.
   396	        S_phi = S_phi - charge_rhs * fd.Constant(z_b_steric) * c_steric_manuf
   397	    else:
   398	        # Ideal Boltzmann counterions (z_scale defaults to 1.0; clamp inactive at our phi).
   399	        for entry in [DEFAULT_CLO4_BOLTZMANN_COUNTERION]:
   400	            z_c = float(entry["z"])
   401	            c_bulk_c = float(entry["c_bulk_nondim"])
   402	            S_phi = S_phi - charge_rhs * z_c * c_bulk_c * fd.exp(-z_c * phi_exact)
   403	    F_res -= S_phi * w_test * dx_q
   404	
   405	    ctx["F_res"] = F_res
   406	    return ctx
   407

   409	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   410	# Reporting helpers
   411	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   412	SPECIES_NAMES = ["O2", "H2O2", "H+"]
   413	
   414	
   415	def compute_rates(h_list, err_list):
   416	    rates = [None]
   417	    for k in range(1, len(h_list)):
   418	        if err_list[k] > 0 and err_list[k - 1] > 0:
   419	            rates.append(log(err_list[k - 1] / err_list[k]) / log(h_list[k - 1] / h_list[k]))
   420	        else:
   421	            rates.append(None)
   422	    return rates

   424	
   425	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   426	# MMS convergence study
   427	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   428	def _ufl_l2_error(u_ufl, u_h, mesh, degree=SRC_QUAD_DEGREE):
   429	    """L2 error of u_h vs UFL expression u_ufl, using high-degree quadrature."""
   430	    dx_q = fd.dx(domain=mesh, degree=degree)
   431	    return float(fd.sqrt(fd.assemble((u_ufl - u_h) ** 2 * dx_q)))
   432	
   433	
   434	def _ufl_h1_error(u_ufl, u_h, mesh, degree=SRC_QUAD_DEGREE):
   435	    """H1 error of u_h vs UFL expression u_ufl, using high-degree quadrature."""
   436	    dx_q = fd.dx(domain=mesh, degree=degree)
   437	    diff = u_ufl - u_h
   438	    grad_diff = fd.grad(u_ufl) - fd.grad(u_h)
   439	    integrand = diff ** 2 + fd.inner(grad_diff, grad_diff)
   440	    return float(fd.sqrt(fd.assemble(integrand * dx_q)))
   441	
   442	
   443	def _solve_mms_on_mesh(
   444	    mesh,
   445	    sp,
   446	    snes_params,
   447	    *,
   448	    eta_hat: float = ETA_HAT_TEST,
   449	    clip_source: bool = False,
   450	    bikerman_counterion=None,
   451	) -> dict:
   452	    """Set up the MMS problem on a given mesh, solve, and return error dict.
   453	
   454	    Returns a dict with per-field L2/H1 errors against the continuum
   455	    manufactured solution (UFL-based, high quadrature)::
   456	
   457	        {"u0_L2", "u0_H1", "u1_L2", ..., "phi_L2", "phi_H1",
   458	         "c0_L2", "c1_L2", "c2_L2",
   459	         "newton_converged": bool, "newton_iterations": int}
   460	
   461	    Caller is responsible for printing diagnostics; this helper only
   462	    raises on Newton divergence (sets newton_converged=False and returns
   463	    NaN errors so the caller can still report).
   464	    """
   465	    n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   466	    c0_HAT = list(THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.c0_vals_hat)
   467	
   468	    x, y = fd.SpatialCoordinate(mesh)
   469	
   470	    # ---- Build the production residual via the dispatcher ----
   471	    ctx = build_context(sp, mesh=mesh)
   472	    ctx = build_forms(ctx, sp)
   473	
   474	    # ---- Manufactured solution as UFL expressions in (x, y) ----
   475	    c_exact = [
   476	        c0_HAT[i] * (
   477	            fd.Constant(1.0)
   478	            + fd.Constant(DELTA_PERTURB[i]) * fd.cos(pi * x) * (1.0 - y) ** 2
   479	        )
   480	        for i in range(n)
   481	    ]
   482	    u_exact = [fd.ln(c_exact[i]) for i in range(n)]
   483	    phi_exact = (
   484	        fd.Constant(eta_hat) * (1.0 - y)
   485	        + fd.Constant(B_PHI) * fd.cos(pi * x) * y * (1.0 - y)
   486	    )
   487	
   488	    # ---- Inject continuum source into F_res (term-by-term mirror) ----
   489	    ctx = _build_manufactured_source(
   490	        ctx, c_exact, u_exact, phi_exact,
   491	        clip_source=clip_source,
   492	        bikerman_counterion=bikerman_counterion,
   493	    )
   494	
   495	    W = ctx["W"]; U = ctx["U"]; U_prev = ctx["U_prev"]
   496	    F_res = ctx["F_res"]; bcs = ctx["bcs"]
   497	
   498	    # ---- Build U_manuf for initial guess ----
   499	    U_manuf = fd.Function(W)
   500	    for i in range(n):
   501	        U_manuf.sub(i).interpolate(u_exact[i])
   502	    U_manuf.sub(n).interpolate(phi_exact)
   503	
   504	    # Production BCs already match U_manuf by manufactured-shape design.
   505	    U.assign(U_manuf)
   506	    U_prev.assign(U_manuf)
   507	
   508	    # ---- Solve ----
   509	    J_form  = fd.derivative(F_res, U)
   510	    problem = fd.NonlinearVariationalProblem(F_res, U, bcs=bcs, J=J_form)
   511	    solver  = fd.NonlinearVariationalSolver(
   512	        problem, solver_parameters=snes_params,
   513	    )
   514	    out: dict = {"newton_converged": False, "newton_iterations": -1}
   515	    try:
   516	        solver.solve()
   517	        out["newton_converged"] = True
   518	        out["newton_iterations"] = int(solver.snes.getIterationNumber())
   519	    except fd.ConvergenceError as exc:
   520	        out["newton_error"] = str(exc)
   521	        for i in range(n):
   522	            out[f"u{i}_L2"] = float("nan")
   523	            out[f"u{i}_H1"] = float("nan")
   524	            out[f"c{i}_L2"] = float("nan")
   525	        out["phi_L2"] = float("nan")
   526	        out["phi_H1"] = float("nan")
   527	        return out
   528	
   529	    # ---- Errors (UFL-based, high quadrature against continuum manuf) ----
   530	    for i in range(n):
   531	        out[f"u{i}_L2"] = _ufl_l2_error(u_exact[i], U.sub(i), mesh)
   532	        out[f"u{i}_H1"] = _ufl_h1_error(u_exact[i], U.sub(i), mesh)
   533	        out[f"c{i}_L2"] = _ufl_l2_error(c_exact[i], fd.exp(U.sub(i)), mesh)
   534	    out["phi_L2"] = _ufl_l2_error(phi_exact, U.sub(n), mesh)
   535	    out["phi_H1"] = _ufl_h1_error(phi_exact, U.sub(n), mesh)
   536	    return out
   537	
   538	
   539	def _print_config_banner(
   540	    *,
   541	    mesh_sizes_str: str,
   542	    v_rhe: float = V_RHE_TEST,
   543	    eta_hat: float = ETA_HAT_TEST,
   544	    clip_source: bool = False,
   545	) -> None:
   546	    n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   547	    c0_HAT = list(THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.c0_vals_hat)
   548	    eta_R1 = (v_rhe - E_EQ_R1) / V_T
   549	    eta_R2 = (v_rhe - E_EQ_R2) / V_T
   550	    R1_status = "CLIPPED" if abs(eta_R1) > 50.0 else "unclipped"
   551	    R2_status = "CLIPPED" if abs(eta_R2) > 50.0 else "unclipped"
   552	    print("=" * 80)
   553	    print("  Production-Faithful MMS: 3sp + Boltzmann + log-c + log-rate BV")
   554	    print("=" * 80)
   555	    print(f"  V_RHE          = {v_rhe} V vs RHE")
   556	    print(f"  eta_hat        = {eta_hat:.4f} (nondim)")
   557	    print(f"  E_eq R1/R2     = {E_EQ_R1}/{E_EQ_R2} V")
   558	    print(f"  c0_HAT         = {c0_HAT}")
   559	    print(f"  delta_i        = {DELTA_PERTURB}")
   560	    print(f"  B_phi          = {B_PHI}")
   561	    print(f"  log-rate BV    = ON (bv_log_rate=True)")
   562	    cl04 = DEFAULT_CLO4_BOLTZMANN_COUNTERION
   563	    print(f"  Boltzmann ClO4-= z={cl04['z']}, c_bulk_hat={cl04['c_bulk_nondim']}")
   564	    print(f"  steric a_vals  = {[A_DEFAULT]*n}")

   576	
   577	def run_mms(
   578	    N_vals: list[int],
   579	    verbose: bool = True,
   580	    *,
   581	    eta_hat: float = ETA_HAT_TEST,
   582	    v_rhe: float = V_RHE_TEST,
   583	    clip_source: bool = False,
   584	    bikerman_counterion=None,
   585	) -> dict:
   586	    """Run the production-faithful MMS convergence study on a chain of
   587	    UnitSquareMesh(N, N) meshes for h^p rate verification.
   588	
   589	    Parameters
   590	    ----------
   591	    eta_hat, v_rhe : float
   592	        Voltage to test (nondim eta and physical V_RHE; should satisfy
   593	        ``eta_hat = v_rhe / V_T``). Defaults preserve the legacy
   594	        V_RHE = +0.55 V test point.
   595	    clip_source : bool
   596	        If True, the manufactured BV source applies the same eta-clip
   597	        (+/-50) as the discrete operator. Useful for isolating discrete
   598	        truncation error from clip-induced model error when ``v_rhe``
   599	        falls in the production clipped regime (R2 below +0.495 V).
   600	
   601	    For single-mesh recovery on the production graded mesh, see
   602	    :func:`verify_on_graded_production_mesh`.
   603	    """
   604	    n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   605	
   606	    if verbose:
   607	        _print_config_banner(
   608	            mesh_sizes_str=f"UnitSquareMesh sweep N={N_vals}",
   609	            v_rhe=v_rhe,
   610	            eta_hat=eta_hat,

   618	    for i in range(n):
   619	        results[f"u{i}_L2"] = []
   620	        results[f"u{i}_H1"] = []

   398	            )

     1	"""3-species + Boltzmann ClO4- log-c MMS convergence test.

     3	Publication-grade convergence proof for the production forward PDE

     7	
     8	Convergence is verified via log-log linear regression (scipy.stats.linregress):
     9	  - L2 error rate ~ O(h^2) for CG1 elements
    10	  - H1 error rate ~ O(h^1) for CG1 elements
    11	  - R-squared > 0.99 for all fits (asymptotic regime check)
    12	
    13	GCI (Grid Convergence Index) is computed using the Roache 3-grid formula
    14	with safety factor Fs=1.25, providing uncertainty quantification for the
    15	finest-grid solution.
    16	
    17	Artifacts (JSON + PNG) are saved to StudyResults/mms_convergence/.
    18	"""
    19	
    20	from __future__ import annotations
    21	
    22	import json
    23	import math
    24	import os
    25	import sys
    26	from datetime import datetime, timezone
    27	
    28	import numpy as np
    29	import pytest
    30	
    31	# Ensure the PNPInverse root is importable
    32	_THIS_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
    33	_ROOT = os.path.dirname(_THIS_DIR)
    34	if _ROOT not in sys.path:
    35	    sys.path.insert(0, _ROOT)
    36	
    37	from conftest import skip_without_firedrake
    38

    40	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    41	# Lazy import of MMS functions (Firedrake must be available at import time)
    42	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    43	
    44	def _import_mms_run():
    45	    """Import run_mms lazily to avoid Firedrake import errors at collection."""
    46	    from scripts.verification.mms_bv_3sp_logc_boltzmann import run_mms
    47	    return run_mms
    48	
    49	
    50	def _import_graded_verifier():
    51	    """Import the graded-mesh verifier lazily."""
    52	    from scripts.verification.mms_bv_3sp_logc_boltzmann import (
    53	        verify_on_graded_production_mesh,
    54	    )
    55	    return verify_on_graded_production_mesh
    56	
    57	
    58	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    59	# Field iteration constants
    60	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    61	
    62	# u_i = ln(c_i) primary variables for 3 dynamic species + phi.  ClO4- is
    63	# the analytic Boltzmann background, not a primary unknown.
    64	FIELD_NAMES = ["u0", "u1", "u2", "phi"]
    65	SPECIES_LABELS = ["O2 (u)", "H2O2 (u)", "H+ (u)", "phi"]
    66	
    67	
    68	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    69	# Helper: convergence rate assertion via log-log regression
    70	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    71	
    72	def assert_convergence_rate(
    73	    h_vals,
    74	    err_vals,
    75	    expected_rate: float,
    76	    rate_tol: float = 0.2,
    77	    min_r_squared: float = 0.99,
    78	    label: str = "",
    79	) -> tuple[float, float]:
    80	    """Assert log-log convergence rate and R-squared, return (slope, r_squared).
    81	
    82	    Parameters
    83	    ----------
    84	    h_vals : array-like
    85	        Mesh sizes (h = 1/N).
    86	    err_vals : array-like
    87	        Error norms corresponding to each mesh size.
    88	    expected_rate : float
    89	        Expected convergence rate (slope in log-log space).
    90	    rate_tol : float
    91	        Acceptable deviation from expected_rate (both sides).
    92	    min_r_squared : float
    93	        Minimum R-squared for the log-log linear fit.
    94	    label : str
    95	        Label for error messages.
    96	
    97	    Returns
    98	    -------
    99	    tuple[float, float]
   100	        (slope, r_squared) from the log-log regression.
   101	    """
   102	    from scipy.stats import linregress
   103	
   104	    log_h = np.log(np.array(h_vals, dtype=float))
   105	    log_err = np.log(np.array(err_vals, dtype=float))
   106	
   107	    slope, _intercept, r_value, _p_value, std_err = linregress(log_h, log_err)
   108	    r_squared = r_value ** 2
   109	
   110	    assert r_squared > min_r_squared, (
   111	        f"{label}: R^2 = {r_squared:.6f} < {min_r_squared} "
   112	        f"(slope={slope:.4f}, std_err={std_err:.4f}). "
   113	        f"Log-log fit is not sufficiently linear -- may not be in asymptotic regime."
   114	    )
   115	    assert slope >= expected_rate - rate_tol, (
   116	        f"{label}: slope = {slope:.4f}, expected >= {expected_rate:.1f} - {rate_tol} "
   117	        f"(R^2={r_squared:.6f}, std_err={std_err:.4f}). "
   118	        f"Convergence rate is worse than theoretical minimum."
   119	    )
   120	
   121	    return slope, r_squared
   122	
   123	
   124	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   125	# Helper: GCI (Grid Convergence Index) via Roache 3-grid formula
   126	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   127	
   128	def compute_gci(
   129	    errors: list[float],
   130	    h_vals: list[float],
   131	    observed_order: float,
   132	    Fs: float = 1.25,
   133	) -> list[dict]:
   134	    """Compute GCI for each consecutive mesh pair using the Roache formula.
   135	
   136	    Parameters
   137	    ----------
   138	    errors : list[float]
   139	        Error norms from coarsest to finest mesh.
   140	    h_vals : list[float]
   141	        Mesh sizes from coarsest to finest.
   142	    observed_order : float
   143	        Observed convergence order (log-log slope).
   144	    Fs : float
   145	        Safety factor (1.25 for >= 3 grids per Roache).
   146	
   147	    Returns
   148	    -------
   149	    list[dict]
   150	        One dict per consecutive pair with keys: h_fine, h_coarse,
   151	        refinement_ratio, error_fine, error_coarse, gci.
   152	    """
   153	    gci_results = []
   154	    for i in range(1, len(errors)):
   155	        e_coarse = errors[i - 1]
   156	        e_fine = errors[i]
   157	        h_coarse = h_vals[i - 1]
   158	        h_fine = h_vals[i]
   159	        r = h_coarse / h_fine  # refinement ratio
   160	
   161	        if e_fine == 0.0:
   162	            gci_val = float("nan")
   163	        else:
   164	            relative_error = abs(e_coarse - e_fine) / e_fine
   165	            denom = r ** observed_order - 1.0
   166	            gci_val = Fs * relative_error / denom if denom != 0.0 else float("nan")
   167	
   168	        gci_results.append({
   169	            "h_fine": h_fine,
   170	            "h_coarse": h_coarse,
   171	            "refinement_ratio": r,
   172	            "error_fine": e_fine,
   173	            "error_coarse": e_coarse,
   174	            "gci": gci_val,
   175	        })
   176	
   177	    return gci_results
   178	
   179	
   180	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   181	# Custom JSON encoder for numpy types
   182	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   183	
   184	class _NumpyEncoder(json.JSONEncoder):
   185	    """JSON encoder that handles numpy scalar types."""
   186	
   187	    def default(self, obj):
   188	        if isinstance(obj, (np.integer,)):
   189	            return int(obj)
   190	        if isinstance(obj, (np.floating,)):
   191	            return float(obj)
   192	        if isinstance(obj, np.ndarray):
   193	            return obj.tolist()
   194	        return super().default(obj)
   195

   204	    """3-species + Boltzmann log-c MMS convergence tests."""

   206	    MESH_SIZES = [8, 16, 32, 64]
   207	    OUTPUT_DIR = os.path.join(_ROOT, "StudyResults", "mms_convergence")
   208	
   209	    @pytest.fixture(scope="class")
   210	    def mms_results(self):
   211	        """Run the 3sp+Boltzmann log-c MMS convergence study once for the class."""

   213	        results = run_mms(self.MESH_SIZES, verbose=True)
   214	
   215	        # Sanity: all mesh sizes should have produced results
   216	        assert len(results["N"]) == len(self.MESH_SIZES), (
   217	            f"Expected {len(self.MESH_SIZES)} mesh results, "
   218	            f"got {len(results['N'])} (some solves may have failed)"
   219	        )
   220	        return results
   221	
   222	    # ---- L2 convergence ----
   223	
   224	    def test_l2_convergence_rates(self, mms_results):
   225	        """Assert L2 convergence rate ~ 2.0 for all 5 fields (CG1)."""
   226	        results_l2 = {}
   227	        for field, label in zip(FIELD_NAMES, SPECIES_LABELS):
   228	            slope, r_squared = assert_convergence_rate(
   229	                mms_results["h"],
   230	                mms_results[f"{field}_L2"],
   231	                expected_rate=2.0,
   232	                rate_tol=0.2,
   233	                min_r_squared=0.99,
   234	                label=f"{label} L2",
   235	            )
   236	            results_l2[field] = {"slope": slope, "r_squared": r_squared}
   237	
   238	        # Store on class for artifact generation
   239	        TestMMSConvergence._l2_results = results_l2
   240	
   241	    # ---- H1 convergence ----
   242	
   243	    def test_h1_convergence_rates(self, mms_results):
   244	        """Assert H1 convergence rate ~ 1.0 for all 5 fields (CG1)."""
   245	        results_h1 = {}
   246	        for field, label in zip(FIELD_NAMES, SPECIES_LABELS):
   247	            slope, r_squared = assert_convergence_rate(
   248	                mms_results["h"],
   249	                mms_results[f"{field}_H1"],
   250	                expected_rate=1.0,
   251	                rate_tol=0.2,
   252	                min_r_squared=0.99,
   253	                label=f"{label} H1",
   254	            )
   255	            results_h1[field] = {"slope": slope, "r_squared": r_squared}
   256	
   257	        TestMMSConvergence._h1_results = results_h1
   258	
   259	    # ---- GCI output ----
   260

   659	
   660	def verify_on_graded_production_mesh(verbose: bool = True) -> dict:
   661	    """Single-mesh MMS recovery test on the production graded rectangle.
   662	
   663	    Mirrors ``scripts/plot_iv_curve_unified.py:118``: ``Nx=8``, ``Ny=200``,
   664	    ``beta=3.0`` -- exactly the mesh production solves use.  Sanity check
   665	    that the solver recovers the manufactured solution to within the
   666	    expected discretization error of the *production* mesh (not the
   667	    asymptotic regime).
   668	
   669	    The dominant error here is ``h_x = 1/8 = 0.125``: our manufactured
   670	    solution has cos(pi x) variation in x, and Nx=8 is coarse for it.
   671	    Expected L2 errors for u_i and phi: O(h_x^2) ~ O(1.6e-2).  Newton
   672	    should still converge cleanly from the U_manuf initial guess.
   673	
   674	    Returns the error dict from :func:`_solve_mms_on_mesh` plus a
   675	    ``mesh_label`` field.
   676	    """
   677	    Nx, Ny, beta = 8, 200, 3.0
   678	    if verbose:
   679	        _print_config_banner(
   680	            mesh_sizes_str=f"graded rectangle Nx={Nx}, Ny={Ny}, beta={beta} (production)"
   681	        )
   682	
   683	    sp = make_sp_production(ETA_HAT_TEST)
   684	    snes_params = _extract_solver_parameters(sp)
   685	
   686	    t0 = time.time()
   687	    mesh = make_graded_rectangle_mesh(Nx=Nx, Ny=Ny, beta=beta)
   688	    errs = _solve_mms_on_mesh(mesh, sp, snes_params)
   689	    elapsed = time.time() - t0
   690	    errs["mesh_label"] = f"graded Nx={Nx}, Ny={Ny}, beta={beta}"
   691	    errs["elapsed_seconds"] = float(elapsed)
   692	
   693	    if verbose:
   694	        if errs.get("newton_converged", False):
   695	            print(
   696	                f"  [graded {Nx}x{Ny}, beta={beta}]  "
   697	                f"Newton iterations: {errs['newton_iterations']}  "
   698	                f"({elapsed:.1f}s)"
   699	            )
   700	            n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   701	            for i in range(n):
   702	                print(
   703	                    f"    {SPECIES_NAMES[i]:>5s} u{i}: "
   704	                    f"L2={errs[f'u{i}_L2']:.3e}  H1={errs[f'u{i}_H1']:.3e}"
   705	                )
   706	            print(
   707	                f"    {'phi':>5s}   : "
   708	                f"L2={errs['phi_L2']:.3e}  H1={errs['phi_H1']:.3e}"
   709	            )
   710	        else:
   711	            print(f"  [graded {Nx}x{Ny}] Newton FAILED: {errs.get('newton_error', '?')}")
   712	
   713	    return errs
   714	
   715	
   716	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   717	# Reporting (pretty-print + plot)
   718	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   719	def format_summary(results: dict) -> str:
   720	    lines = [""]
   721	    lines.append("=" * 80)
   722	    lines.append("  Production-Faithful MMS: Convergence Rate Summary")
   723	    lines.append("=" * 80)
   724	
   725	    h_list = results["h"]
   726	    n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   727	    all_pass = True
   728	
   729	    for i in range(n):
   730	        for norm in ("L2", "H1"):
   731	            key = f"u{i}_{norm}"
   732	            rates = compute_rates(h_list, results[key])
   733	            final = rates[-1] if rates[-1] is not None else 0.0
   734	            expected = 2.0 if norm == "L2" else 1.0
   735	            lo = 1.85 if norm == "L2" else 0.85
   736	            hi = 2.15 if norm == "L2" else 999.0
   737	            status = "PASS" if lo <= final <= hi else "FAIL"
   738	            if status == "FAIL":
   739	                all_pass = False
   740	            lines.append(
   741	                f"  {SPECIES_NAMES[i]:>5s} u{i} {norm}: rate = {final:.4f}  "
   742	                f"(expected ~{expected:.1f})  [{status}]"
   743	            )
   744	        rates = compute_rates(h_list, results[f"c{i}_L2"])
   745	        final = rates[-1] if rates[-1] is not None else 0.0
   746	        lines.append(
   747	            f"  {SPECIES_NAMES[i]:>5s} c{i} L2 (=exp(u)): rate = {final:.4f}"
   748	        )
   749	
   750	    for norm in ("L2", "H1"):
   751	        key = f"phi_{norm}"
   752	        rates = compute_rates(h_list, results[key])
   753	        final = rates[-1] if rates[-1] is not None else 0.0
   754	        expected = 2.0 if norm == "L2" else 1.0
   755	        lo = 1.85 if norm == "L2" else 0.85
   756	        hi = 2.15 if norm == "L2" else 999.0
   757	        status = "PASS" if lo <= final <= hi else "FAIL"
   758	        if status == "FAIL":
   759	            all_pass = False
   760	        lines.append(
   761	            f"  {'phi':>5s}    {norm}: rate = {final:.4f}  "
   762	            f"(expected ~{expected:.1f})  [{status}]"
   763	        )
   764	
   765	    lines.append("-" * 80)
   766	    lines.append(f"  Overall: {'ALL PASS' if all_pass else 'SOME FAILURES'}")
   767	    lines.append("=" * 80)
   768	    return "\n".join(lines)
   769	
   770	
   771	def format_table(results: dict) -> str:
   772	    lines = ["", "=" * 100]
   773	    lines.append("  Full Error Table (u_i = ln(c_i) primary unknown)")
   774	    lines.append("=" * 100)
   775	    h_list = results["h"]
   776	    n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   777	
   778	    fields: list[str] = []
   779	    for i in range(n):
   780	        fields.append(f"u{i}_L2")
   781	        fields.append(f"u{i}_H1")
   782	    fields.append("phi_L2")
   783	    fields.append("phi_H1")
   784	
   785	    header = f"  {'N':>4} {'h':>8}  "
   786	    for fn in fields:
   787	        header += f"{fn:>10}  {'rate':>5}  "
   788	    lines.append(header)
   789	    lines.append("-" * 100)
   790	
   791	    rates = {fn: compute_rates(h_list, results[fn]) for fn in fields}
   792	    for k in range(len(results["N"])):
   793	        row = f"  {results['N'][k]:>4} {results['h'][k]:>8.4f}  "
   794	        for fn in fields:
   795	            r = rates[fn][k]
   796	            r_str = f"{r:.2f}" if r is not None else "---"
   797	            row += f"{results[fn][k]:>10.3e}  {r_str:>5}  "
   798	        lines.append(row)
   799	    lines.append("=" * 100)
   800	    return "\n".join(lines)
   801	
   802	
   803	def plot_convergence(results: dict, out_dir: str) -> str:
   804	    fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(14, 5))
   805	    h = np.array(results["h"])
   806	    n = THREE_SPECIES_LOGC_BOLTZMANN.n_species
   807	    colors = ["#1f77b4", "#ff7f0e", "#2ca02c", "#9467bd"]
   808	
   809	    ax = axes[0]
   810	    for i in range(n):
   811	        ax.loglog(h, results[f"u{i}_L2"], "o-", color=colors[i], linewidth=1.5,
   812	                  markersize=5, label=f"{SPECIES_NAMES[i]} $u_{i}$ $L^2$")
   813	    ax.loglog(h, results["phi_L2"], "s-", color=colors[3], linewidth=1.5,
   814	              markersize=5, label=r"$\phi$ $L^2$")
   815	    h_ref = np.array([h[0], h[-1]])
   816	    scale = results["u0_L2"][0] / h[0] ** 2
   817	    ax.loglog(h_ref, scale * h_ref ** 2, "k:", linewidth=0.8, label=r"$O(h^2)$")
   818	    ax.set_xlabel("$h$"); ax.set_ylabel("$L^2$ error")
   819	    ax.set_title("$L^2$ Convergence (production-faithful)")
   820	    ax.legend(fontsize=8); ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, which="both")
   821	
   822	    ax = axes[1]
   823	    for i in range(n):
   824	        ax.loglog(h, results[f"u{i}_H1"], "o-", color=colors[i], linewidth=1.5,
   825	                  markersize=5, label=f"{SPECIES_NAMES[i]} $u_{i}$ $H^1$")
   826	    ax.loglog(h, results["phi_H1"], "s-", color=colors[3], linewidth=1.5,
   827	              markersize=5, label=r"$\phi$ $H^1$")
   828	    scale = results["u0_H1"][0] / h[0] ** 1
   829	    ax.loglog(h_ref, scale * h_ref ** 1, "k-.", linewidth=0.8, label=r"$O(h^1)$")
   830	    ax.set_xlabel("$h$"); ax.set_ylabel("$H^1$ error")
   831	    ax.set_title("$H^1$ Convergence (production-faithful)")
   832	    ax.legend(fontsize=8); ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, which="both")
   833	
   834	    fig.suptitle(
   835	        f"MMS: 3sp + Boltzmann + log-c + log-rate BV   "
   836	        f"(V_RHE = {V_RHE_TEST} V, production stack)",
   837	        fontsize=11,
   838	    )
   839	    plt.tight_layout()
   840	    png = os.path.join(out_dir, "mms_3sp_logc_boltzmann.png")
   841	    fig.savefig(png, dpi=170, bbox_inches="tight")
   842	    plt.close(fig)
   843	    return png
   844	
   845	
   846	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   847	# Main
   848	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   849	def main():
   850	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
   851	    parser.add_argument("--Nvals", type=int, nargs="+",
   852	                        default=[8, 16, 32, 64, 128])
   853	    parser.add_argument("--out-dir", default="StudyResults/mms_3sp_logc_boltzmann")
   854	    args = parser.parse_args()
   855	
   856	    os.makedirs(args.out_dir, exist_ok=True)
   857	
   858	    results = run_mms(args.Nvals)
   859	    if len(results["N"]) < 2:
   860	        print("\n[ERROR] Not enough successful solves for convergence analysis.")
   861	        sys.exit(1)
   862	
   863	    print(format_table(results))
   864	    print(format_summary(results))
   865	
   866	    summary_path = os.path.join(args.out_dir, "mms_3sp_logc_summary.txt")
   867	    with open(summary_path, "w") as f:
   868	        f.write("Production-faithful MMS study\n")
   869	        f.write(f"Date: {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n\n")
   870	        f.write(format_table(results) + "\n\n")
   871	        f.write(format_summary(results) + "\n")

     1	"""Formulation dispatcher for the BV-PNP forward solver.
     2	
     3	The production stack uses the log-concentration backend (``forms_logc``).
     4	An experimental proton-electrochemical-potential variant
     5	(``forms_logc_muh``) is available for ``formulation="logc_muh"``; the muh
     6	backend stores the proton primary variable as ``mu_H = u_H + em*z_H*phi``
     7	to give Newton a smoother variable in Debye-layer regions where ``u_H``
     8	and ``phi`` separately vary by tens of log-units.  See
     9	``Forward/bv_solver/forms_logc_muh.py`` for the math and
    10	``docs/electrochemical_potential_solver_plan.md`` for the landing plan.
    11	
    12	``build_context`` / ``build_forms`` / ``set_initial_conditions`` dispatch on:
    13	
    14	  - ``params['bv_convergence']['formulation']``  -- selects backend module
    15	    (``"logc"`` or ``"logc_muh"``).
    16	  - ``params['bv_convergence']['initializer']``  -- selects IC routine
    17	    within the chosen backend (``"linear_phi"`` or ``"debye_boltzmann"``).
    18	
    19	The ``*_logc`` and ``*_logc_muh`` names are re-exported for scripts that
    20	want to be explicit about the backend they target.
    21	"""
    22	
    23	from __future__ import annotations
    24	
    25	from typing import Any
    26	
    27	from .forms_logc import (
    28	    build_context_logc,
    29	    build_forms_logc,
    30	    set_initial_conditions_logc,
    31	    set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc,
    32	)
    33	from .forms_logc_muh import (
    34	    build_context_logc_muh,
    35	    build_forms_logc_muh,
    36	    set_initial_conditions_logc_muh,
    37	    set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh,
    38	)
    39	
    40	
    41	def _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params: Any, key: str, default: str) -> str:
    42	    """Read ``bv_convergence[key]`` with a graceful default.
    43	
    44	    Robust to ``SolverParams`` (via ``__getitem__``), legacy 11-tuples,
    45	    and malformed test inputs.  Falls back to ``default`` whenever the
    46	    config block is missing or non-dict.
    47	    """
    48	    try:
    49	        params_dict = solver_params[10] if hasattr(solver_params, "__getitem__") else None
    50	    except Exception:
    51	        params_dict = None
    52	    if not isinstance(params_dict, dict):
    53	        return default
    54	    bv_conv = params_dict.get("bv_convergence", {})
    55	    if not isinstance(bv_conv, dict):
    56	        return default
    57	    return str(bv_conv.get(key, default)).strip().lower()
    58	
    59	
    60	def _read_formulation(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    61	    return _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params, "formulation", "logc")
    62	
    63	
    64	def _read_initializer(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    65	    return _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params, "initializer", "linear_phi")
    66	
    67	
    68	def _resolve_backend(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    69	    """Pick a backend module name based on ``formulation``.
    70	
    71	    Returns one of ``"logc"`` or ``"logc_muh"``.  Unknown formulations
    72	    fall through to ``"logc"`` (the production default) -- the config
    73	    layer (``Forward/bv_solver/config.py:_validate_formulation``) already
    74	    rejects unknown names at parse time, so this is defensive only.
    75	    """
    76	    formulation = _read_formulation(solver_params)
    77	    if formulation == "logc_muh":
    78	        return "logc_muh"
    79	    return "logc"
    80	
    81	
    82	def build_context(solver_params: Any, *, mesh: Any = None) -> dict:
    83	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
    84	    if backend == "logc_muh":
    85	        return build_context_logc_muh(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
    86	    return build_context_logc(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
    87	
    88	
    89	def build_forms(ctx: dict, solver_params: Any) -> dict:
    90	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
    91	    if backend == "logc_muh":
    92	        return build_forms_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
    93	    return build_forms_logc(ctx, solver_params)
    94	
    95	
    96	def set_initial_conditions(
    97	    ctx: dict, solver_params: Any, *, blob: bool = False
    98	) -> None:
    99	    """Set initial conditions for the dispatched backend.
   100	
   101	    Dispatches on ``params['bv_convergence']['formulation']`` to pick the
   102	    backend, then on ``params['bv_convergence']['initializer']`` to pick
   103	    the IC routine within that backend:
   104	
   105	      - ``"linear_phi"``     -> ``set_initial_conditions_*``
   106	      - ``"debye_boltzmann"`` -> ``set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_*``
   107	
   108	    ``blob`` is accepted for backward-compatible kwargs and silently
   109	    ignored -- blob ICs were a concentration-formulation feature removed
   110	    with that backend.
   111	    """
   112	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
   113	    initializer = _read_initializer(solver_params)
   114	    if backend == "logc_muh":
   115	        if initializer == "debye_boltzmann":
   116	            return set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   117	        return set_initial_conditions_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   118	    if initializer == "debye_boltzmann":
   119	        return set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   120	    return set_initial_conditions_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   121	
   122	
   123	__all__ = [
   124	    "build_context",
   125	    "build_forms",
   126	    "set_initial_conditions",
   127	    # logc backend (production)
   128	    "build_context_logc",
   129	    "build_forms_logc",
   130	    "set_initial_conditions_logc",
   131	    "set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc",
   132	    # logc_muh backend (experimental)
   133	    "build_context_logc_muh",
   134	    "build_forms_logc_muh",
   135	    "set_initial_conditions_logc_muh",
   136	    "set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh",
   137	]

   381	@skip_without_firedrake
   382	@pytest.mark.slow
   383	class TestMMSProductionGradedMesh:
   384	    """Single-mesh MMS recovery on the production graded rectangle.
   385	
   386	    Verifies the solver produces the manufactured solution within the
   387	    expected discretization error of the actual production mesh
   388	    (Nx=8, Ny=200, beta=3 -- mirrors plot_iv_curve_unified.py).  This is
   389	    not an asymptotic convergence test; the thresholds are sized to the
   390	    Nx=8-dominated x-direction discretization error (h_x^2 = 1/64) with
   391	    safety margin.  Intended to fail loudly on any wiring bug that
   392	    causes O(1) rather than O(h_x^2) errors.
   393	    """
   394	
   395	    # Empirically observed errors (May 2026 baseline):
   396	    #   u0 (O2):   L2 = 1.6e-3,  H1 = 5.4e-2
   397	    #   u1 (H2O2): L2 = 6.5e-4,  H1 = 5.5e-2
   398	    #   u2 (H+):   L2 = 7.2e-4,  H1 = 5.5e-2
   399	    #   phi:       L2 = 3.8e-4,  H1 = 4.0e-2
   400	    # Thresholds set ~6x above observed to stay robust to compiler /
   401	    # solver-version drift, while still ~100x below the O(1) errors a
   402	    # wiring bug would produce.
   403	    L2_THRESHOLD = 1e-2

     1	"""Mixed-function-space DOF indexing helper (Phase 6β v9 Gate 3A).
     2	
     3	The bv_solver mixed space normally has shape ``[V_scalar]*n_species +
     4	[V_scalar (phi)]``.  Phase 6β v9 Gate 3A extends it conditionally with an
     5	R-space global scalar for the surface coverage ``Γ_MOH`` of the
     6	cation-hydrolysis residual::
     7	
     8	    legacy   :   [V_scalar]*n_species + [V_scalar (phi)]
     9	    +Γ slot  :   [V_scalar]*n_species + [V_scalar (phi)] + [R_space (Γ)]
    10	
    11	Form-build call-sites used to slice the mixed components with the
    12	hard-coded patterns ``fd.split(U)[:-1]`` / ``fd.split(U)[-1]``.  Those
    13	break silently when ``has_gamma=True`` because ``[-1]`` then points at
    14	``Γ`` rather than ``φ``.
    15	
    16	This helper centralises the slice / index logic so every call-site can
    17	stay agnostic of the layout.  When ``has_gamma=False`` the indices match
    18	the legacy patterns byte-for-byte; when ``has_gamma=True`` ``φ`` shifts
    19	to position ``-2`` and ``Γ`` lands at ``-1``.
    20	
    21	Pure-Python; no Firedrake import.  Lets the fast unit suite verify the
    22	indexing without spinning up FE infrastructure.
    23	"""
    24	from __future__ import annotations
    25	
    26	from dataclasses import dataclass
    27	from typing import Optional
    28	
    29	
    30	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    31	class SpeciesPhiGammaIndices:
    32	    """DOF-position indices for the species + φ (+ Γ) mixed space.
    33	
    34	    Attributes
    35	    ----------
    36	    species_slice
    37	        Python ``slice`` covering all dynamic-species components.  For
    38	        both legacy and Γ-augmented layouts the species occupy indices
    39	        ``0..n_species-1``; the slice expresses that via negative
    40	        right-bound (``-1`` legacy, ``-2`` Γ-augmented) so it does not
    41	        need to know ``n_species``.
    42	    phi_index
    43	        Position of the ``φ`` component using negative indexing
    44	        (``-1`` legacy, ``-2`` Γ-augmented).  Negative form chosen so
    45	        the same index works on both ``fd.split(U)`` (a tuple) and
    46	        ``fd.TestFunctions(W)`` (also a tuple).
    47	    gamma_index
    48	        Position of the ``Γ_MOH`` R-space component (always ``-1`` when
    49	        present).  ``None`` in legacy layout — callers should short-
    50	        circuit on ``is None`` rather than catch IndexError.
    51	    has_gamma
    52	        Convenience flag mirroring the constructor argument.
    53	    """
    54	
    55	    species_slice: slice
    56	    phi_index: int
    57	    gamma_index: Optional[int]
    58	    has_gamma: bool
    59	
    60	
    61	def unpack_dof_indices(*, has_gamma: bool) -> SpeciesPhiGammaIndices:
    62	    """Return DOF-position indices for the current mixed-space layout.
    63	
    64	    Parameters
    65	    ----------
    66	    has_gamma
    67	        ``True`` iff the form was built with
    68	        ``enable_cation_hydrolysis=True`` (mixed space includes one
    69	        extra R-space slot at the end for Γ_MOH).  ``False`` for the
    70	        legacy layout.
    71	
    72	    Returns
    73	    -------
    74	    SpeciesPhiGammaIndices
    75	        Indices that bridge legacy and Γ-augmented layouts uniformly.
    76	        Caller can use ``species_slice`` against ``fd.split(U)`` /
    77	        ``fd.TestFunctions(W)`` for the species block, ``phi_index``
    78	        for the potential, and ``gamma_index`` for ``Γ`` (when present).
    79	    """
    80	    if has_gamma:
    81	        return SpeciesPhiGammaIndices(
    82	            species_slice=slice(0, -2),
    83	            phi_index=-2,
    84	            gamma_index=-1,
    85	            has_gamma=True,
    86	        )
    87	    return SpeciesPhiGammaIndices(
    88	        species_slice=slice(0, -1),
    89	        phi_index=-1,
    90	        gamma_index=None,
    91	        has_gamma=False,
    92	    )
    93	
    94	
    95	__all__ = [
    96	    "SpeciesPhiGammaIndices",
    97	    "unpack_dof_indices",
    98	]

     1	"""Graded mesh utilities for the Butler-Volmer PNP solver."""
     2	
     3	from __future__ import annotations
     4	
     5	import firedrake as fd
     6	
     7	
     8	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
     9	# Domain-height bounds
    10	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    11	#
    12	# ``domain_height_hat`` decouples the mesh y-extent from L_REF so the
    13	# transport-domain physical height L_eff_m can be swept independently of
    14	# the global nondim scale.  See ``.claude/plans/l-eff-transport-sweep.md``
    15	# for the L_eff sweep design and ``Forward/bv_solver/forms_logc.py`` for
    16	# how the IC routines normalize their outer linear interpolations by
    17	# this factor.
    18	
    19	_DOMAIN_HEIGHT_HAT_MIN = 1e-3   # 0.1 µm at L_REF = 100 µm
    20	_DOMAIN_HEIGHT_HAT_MAX = 10.0   # 1 mm at L_REF = 100 µm
    21	
    22	
    23	def _validate_domain_height_hat(domain_height_hat: float) -> float:
    24	    """Validate ``domain_height_hat`` is positive and within sanity bounds."""
    25	    val = float(domain_height_hat)
    26	    if val <= 0.0:
    27	        raise ValueError(
    28	            f"domain_height_hat must be positive; got {val}."
    29	        )
    30	    if val < _DOMAIN_HEIGHT_HAT_MIN or val > _DOMAIN_HEIGHT_HAT_MAX:
    31	        raise ValueError(
    32	            f"domain_height_hat={val} out of sanity range "
    33	            f"[{_DOMAIN_HEIGHT_HAT_MIN}, {_DOMAIN_HEIGHT_HAT_MAX}]; "
    34	            f"if intentional, raise the bounds in mesh.py."
    35	        )
    36	    return val
    37	
    38	
    39	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    40	# Graded mesh utilities
    41	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    42	
    43	def make_graded_interval_mesh(N: int = 300, beta: float = 2.0) -> fd.Mesh:
    44	    """Create a 1D interval mesh on [0, 1] with power-law grading.
    45	
    46	    Points are placed at ``x_i = (i/N)^beta`` for ``i = 0, ..., N``.
    47	    ``beta > 1`` clusters nodes near ``x = 0`` (electrode).
    48	
    49	    Boundary markers:
    50	        1 = left  (x=0, electrode)
    51	        2 = right (x=1, bulk)
    52	
    53	    Parameters
    54	    ----------
    55	    N : int
    56	        Number of cells (elements).
    57	    beta : float
    58	        Grading exponent.  beta=1 gives uniform spacing; beta=2 gives
    59	        quadratic clustering near x=0.
    60	    """
    61	    mesh = fd.IntervalMesh(N, 1.0)
    62	    coords = mesh.coordinates.dat.data
    63	    # Apply power-law stretching: x -> x^beta
    64	    coords[:] = coords[:] ** beta
    65	    return mesh
    66	
    67	
    68	def make_graded_rectangle_mesh(
    69	    Nx: int = 8,
    70	    Ny: int = 300,
    71	    beta: float = 2.0,
    72	    domain_height_hat: float = 1.0,
    73	) -> fd.Mesh:
    74	    """Create a 2D rectangle mesh on [0, 1] x [0, domain_height_hat].
    75	
    76	    The y-coordinate is stretched: ``y -> y^beta`` (in unit-cube space) and
    77	    then scaled by ``domain_height_hat``.  ``beta > 1`` clusters nodes near
    78	    ``y = 0`` (electrode / bottom).  The x-direction is uniform.  When
    79	    ``domain_height_hat == 1.0`` the mesh is byte-identical to the legacy
    80	    ``[0, 1]^2`` graded rectangle.
    81	
    82	    Boundary markers (firedrake ``RectangleMesh`` convention):
    83	        1 = left   (x=0, zero-flux)
    84	        2 = right  (x=1, zero-flux)
    85	        3 = bottom (y=0, electrode)
    86	        4 = top    (y=domain_height_hat, bulk)
    87	
    88	    Parameters
    89	    ----------
    90	    Nx : int
    91	        Number of cells in x (tangential, uniform).
    92	    Ny : int
    93	        Number of cells in y (normal to electrode, graded).
    94	    beta : float
    95	        Grading exponent for the y-direction.
    96	    domain_height_hat : float
    97	        Mesh y-extent in nondim coords (= ``L_eff_m / L_REF``).  Default
    98	        ``1.0`` reproduces the legacy ``[0, 1]^2`` rectangle.  Used by the
    99	        L_eff transport sweep to vary the proton-transport ceiling without
   100	        rescaling the global L_REF.
   101	    """
   102	    domain_height_hat = _validate_domain_height_hat(domain_height_hat)
   103	    mesh = fd.RectangleMesh(Nx, Ny, 1.0, 1.0)
   104	    coords = mesh.coordinates.dat.data
   105	    # Stretch y in unit-cube coords first so the relative clustering near
   106	    # y=0 is preserved, then scale to the requested physical extent.
   107	    coords[:, 1] = (coords[:, 1] ** beta) * domain_height_hat
   108	    return mesh
