     1	"""BV configuration helpers for parsing solver_params."""
     2	
     3	from __future__ import annotations
     4	
     5	import warnings
     6	from typing import Any, List, Optional
     7	
     8	from Nondim.transform import _as_list, _bool
     9	
    10	
    11	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    12	# BV config helpers
    13	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    14	
    15	def _get_bv_cfg(params: Any, n_species: int) -> dict:
    16	    """Parse and validate the ``bv_bc`` block from solver_params[10]."""
    17	    if not isinstance(params, dict):
    18	        raise ValueError("solver_params[10] must be a dict containing 'bv_bc'.")
    19	    raw = params.get("bv_bc", {})
    20	    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
    21	        raise ValueError("solver_params[10]['bv_bc'] must be a dict.")
    22	
    23	    k0 = raw.get("k0", 1e-5)
    24	    alpha = raw.get("alpha", 0.5)
    25	    alpha_val = float(alpha) if not isinstance(alpha, (list, tuple)) else None
    26	    if alpha_val is not None and not (0.0 < alpha_val <= 1.0):
    27	        raise ValueError(f"alpha must be in (0, 1]; got {alpha_val}")
    28	    if alpha_val is None:
    29	        for k, a in enumerate(alpha):
    30	            try:
    31	                a_f = float(a)
    32	            except (TypeError, ValueError) as exc:
    33	                raise ValueError(
    34	                    f"bv_bc.alpha[{k}] must be a float; got {a!r}"
    35	                ) from exc
    36	            if not (0.0 < a_f <= 1.0):
    37	                raise ValueError(
    38	                    f"bv_bc.alpha[{k}] must be in (0, 1]; got {a_f}"
    39	                )
    40	    stoichiometry = raw.get("stoichiometry", [-1] * n_species)
    41	    c_ref = raw.get("c_ref", raw.get("c_inf", 1.0))
    42	    E_eq_v = float(raw.get("E_eq_v", 0.0))
    43	    # Defaults match RectangleMesh convention: 3=bottom (electrode), 4=top (bulk).
    44	    # For IntervalMesh, override to electrode_marker=1, concentration_marker=2, ground_marker=2.
    45	    electrode_marker = int(raw.get("electrode_marker", 3))
    46	    concentration_marker = int(raw.get("concentration_marker", 4))
    47	    ground_marker = int(raw.get("ground_marker", 4))
    48	    # Stern layer capacitance [F/m²].  When set (> 0), enables the Frumkin-
    49	    # corrected overpotential model:
    50	    #   eta = phi_m - phi_s - E_eq     (matches LaTeX formulation)
    51	    # where phi_m = phi_applied (metal potential) and phi_s = solution potential
    52	    # at the electrode surface (free to float, determined by the Poisson
    53	    # equation + Stern layer Robin BC).  The Dirichlet BC for phi at the
    54	    # electrode is replaced with:
    55	    #   epsilon * grad(phi) . n = C_stern * (phi_m - phi)
    56	    # When None or 0 (default), the classical model is used:
    57	    #   eta = phi_applied - E_eq       (phi_s = phi_applied via Dirichlet BC)
    58	    stern_raw = raw.get("stern_capacitance_f_m2", None)
    59	    stern_capacitance = float(stern_raw) if stern_raw is not None else None
    60	    if stern_capacitance is not None and stern_capacitance < 0:
    61	        raise ValueError(
    62	            f"stern_capacitance_f_m2 must be non-negative; got {stern_capacitance}"
    63	        )
    64	
    65	    return {
    66	        "k0_vals":            _as_list(k0, n_species, "bv_bc.k0"),
    67	        "alpha_vals":         _as_list(alpha, n_species, "bv_bc.alpha"),
    68	        "stoichiometry":      [int(s) for s in _as_list(stoichiometry, n_species, "bv_bc.stoichiometry")],
    69	        "c_ref_vals":         _as_list(c_ref, n_species, "bv_bc.c_ref"),
    70	        "E_eq_v":             E_eq_v,
    71	        "electrode_marker":   electrode_marker,
    72	        "concentration_marker": concentration_marker,
    73	        "ground_marker":      ground_marker,
    74	        "stern_capacitance_f_m2": stern_capacitance,
    75	    }
    76	
    77	
    78	_VALID_FORMULATIONS = ("concentration", "logc", "logc_muh")
    79	_VALID_INITIALIZERS = ("linear_phi", "debye_boltzmann")
    80	
    81	
    82	def _validate_formulation(value: Any) -> str:
    83	    """Coerce/validate the formulation config field.
    84	
    85	    The ``"concentration"`` backend was removed in the May 2026 cleanup;
    86	    the dispatcher silently falls through to ``"logc"`` for that value to
    87	    keep old configs parseable.  Emit a deprecation warning so callers
    88	    know they are getting the log-c backend rather than the named one.
    89	    """
    90	    if value is None:
    91	        return "logc"
    92	    s = str(value).strip().lower()
    93	    if s not in _VALID_FORMULATIONS:
    94	        raise ValueError(
    95	            f"bv_convergence.formulation must be one of {_VALID_FORMULATIONS}; got {value!r}"
    96	        )
    97	    if s == "concentration":
    98	        warnings.warn(
    99	            "bv_convergence.formulation='concentration' refers to a backend "
   100	            "removed in the May 2026 cleanup; the dispatcher will use 'logc' "
   101	            "instead.  Update the config to 'logc' or 'logc_muh' explicitly.",
   102	            DeprecationWarning,
   103	            stacklevel=2,
   104	        )
   105	    return s
   106	
   107	
   108	def _validate_initializer(value: Any) -> str:
   109	    """Coerce/validate the initializer config field."""
   110	    if value is None:
   111	        return "linear_phi"
   112	    s = str(value).strip().lower()
   113	    if s not in _VALID_INITIALIZERS:
   114	        raise ValueError(
   115	            f"bv_convergence.initializer must be one of {_VALID_INITIALIZERS}; got {value!r}"
   116	        )
   117	    return s
   118	
   119	
   120	def _default_bv_convergence_cfg() -> dict:
   121	    """Default BV convergence config (used when params is missing the block).
   122	
   123	    ``exponent_clip = 100.0`` is the only PC-trustworthy default.  At
   124	    clip=50 (production until 2026-05-04) the peroxide-current observable
   125	    is fictitious below V_RHE = -0.1 V (sign-flipped, 3-4 OOM off; CD is
   126	    approximately correct).  At clip=100 the production V grid
   127	    V_RHE in [-0.5, +1.0] V is unclipped for both reactions, exposing
   128	    true mass-transport-limited PC.  Do not lower this below 100 for
   129	    forward runs whose PC will be compared against experiment or used
   130	    for inverse fitting.  Trade-off: cold-start Newton basin shrinks
   131	    (10/13 -> 3/13 voltages on a typical sweep), but C+D warm-walk
   132	    continuation rescues every voltage.  See
   133	    ``docs/clip_observable_investigation.md`` §5.2 and
   134	    ``docs/clipping_conventions.md`` for the operational rule.
   135	    """
   136	    return {
   137	        "clip_exponent":            True,
   138	        "exponent_clip":            100.0,
   139	        "regularize_concentration": True,
   140	        "conc_floor":               1e-8,
   141	        "use_eta_in_bv":            True,
   142	        "packing_floor":            1e-8,
   143	        "softplus_regularization":  False,
   144	        "bv_log_rate":              False,
   145	        "u_clamp":                  100.0,
   146	        "formulation":              "logc",
   147	        "initializer":              "linear_phi",
   148	        # Phase 6β step 6 plumbing-ablation defaults (preserve
   149	        # byte-equivalence with v9/v10a/v10a'/A.2).
   150	        "apply_h_source":           True,
   151	        "apply_k_sink":             True,
   152	        "override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2": None,
   153	    }
   154	
   155	
   156	def _get_bv_convergence_cfg(params: Any) -> dict:
   157	    """Parse optional BV convergence-strategy settings."""
   158	    if not isinstance(params, dict):
   159	        return _default_bv_convergence_cfg()
   160	    raw = params.get("bv_convergence", {})
   161	    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
   162	        return _default_bv_convergence_cfg()
   163	    exponent_clip = float(raw.get("exponent_clip", 100.0))
   164	    conc_floor = float(raw.get("conc_floor", 1e-8))
   165	    packing_floor = float(raw.get("packing_floor", 1e-8))
   166	    u_clamp = float(raw.get("u_clamp", 100.0))
   167	    formulation = _validate_formulation(raw.get("formulation", "logc"))
   168	    initializer = _validate_initializer(raw.get("initializer", "linear_phi"))
   169	    if exponent_clip <= 0:
   170	        raise ValueError(f"exponent_clip must be positive; got {exponent_clip}")
   171	    if conc_floor <= 0:
   172	        raise ValueError(f"conc_floor must be positive; got {conc_floor}")
   173	    if packing_floor <= 0:
   174	        raise ValueError(f"packing_floor must be positive; got {packing_floor}")
   175	    if u_clamp <= 0:
   176	        raise ValueError(f"u_clamp must be positive; got {u_clamp}")
   177	
   178	    # Phase 6α — water self-ionization keys.  Default to a disabled
   179	    # configuration (enable_water_ionization=False, zero kw/d_oh/a_oh)
   180	    # so callers that never set these keys are byte-equivalent to the
   181	    # pre-Phase-6α stack.  Validated when enable_water_ionization is on.
   182	    enable_water_ionization = _bool(raw.get("enable_water_ionization", False))
   183	    kw_eff_hat = float(raw.get("kw_eff_hat", 0.0))
   184	    d_oh_hat = float(raw.get("d_oh_hat", 0.0))
   185	    a_oh_hat = float(raw.get("a_oh_hat", 0.0))
   186	    if enable_water_ionization:
   187	        if kw_eff_hat < 0.0:
   188	            raise ValueError(
   189	                "kw_eff_hat must be non-negative when "
   190	                f"enable_water_ionization=True; got {kw_eff_hat}"
   191	            )
   192	        if d_oh_hat <= 0.0:
   193	            raise ValueError(
   194	                "d_oh_hat must be positive when "
   195	                f"enable_water_ionization=True; got {d_oh_hat}"
   196	            )
   197	        if a_oh_hat < 0.0:
   198	            raise ValueError(
   199	                "a_oh_hat must be non-negative when "
   200	                f"enable_water_ionization=True; got {a_oh_hat}"
   201	            )
   202	
   203	    # Phase 6β v9 Gate 3 — cation hydrolysis keys.  The flag gates the
   204	    # mixed-space Γ slot (Gate 3A) and the cation_hydrolysis bundle
   205	    # (Gate 3B).  ``cation_hydrolysis_config`` carries the per-cation
   206	    # Singh parameters + finite-rate kinetics (filled in by Gate 4A);
   207	    # at Gate 3 the flag is enough to extend the mixed space.
   208	    enable_cation_hydrolysis = _bool(raw.get("enable_cation_hydrolysis", False))
   209	    cation_hydrolysis_config = raw.get("cation_hydrolysis_config", None)
   210	    if enable_cation_hydrolysis:
   211	        if cation_hydrolysis_config is not None and not isinstance(
   212	            cation_hydrolysis_config, dict
   213	        ):
   214	            raise ValueError(
   215	                "cation_hydrolysis_config must be a dict (or None) when "
   216	                f"enable_cation_hydrolysis=True; got "
   217	                f"{type(cation_hydrolysis_config).__name__}"
   218	            )
   219	    # Manufactured-source override for Gate 3D unit tests: when set,
   220	    # the form replaces R_net with this Constant value.  ``None`` (the
   221	    # default) leaves the production R_net wired up.  Surfaced via the
   222	    # parser so the form-build code can read it from conv_cfg.
   223	    manufactured_R_inj_raw = raw.get("manufactured_R_inj", None)
   224	    manufactured_R_inj = (
   225	        None if manufactured_R_inj_raw is None
   226	        else float(manufactured_R_inj_raw)
   227	    )
   228	
   229	    # Phase 6β step 6 — plumbing-ablation flags.  Defaults preserve
   230	    # byte-equivalence with v9/v10a/v10a'/A.2.
   231	    #
   232	    #   apply_h_source : gates the cation-hydrolysis proton residual
   233	    #       term.  Valid only with manufactured_R_inj is not None.
   234	    #   apply_k_sink : gates the cation-hydrolysis K+ residual term.
   235	    #       Valid only with manufactured_R_inj is not None.
   236	    #   override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2 : when set (non-negative finite
   237	    #       scalar in Singh counts/pm² units), replaces σ_S in
   238	    #       build_pka_shift with a fake-signed σ that, after the
   239	    #       existing anode clamp + 6.2415e-6 conversion, equals the
   240	    #       override.  Valid only with manufactured_R_inj is None.
   241	    apply_h_source = _bool(raw.get("apply_h_source", True))
   242	    apply_k_sink = _bool(raw.get("apply_k_sink", True))
   243	    override_raw = raw.get("override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2", None)
   244	    if override_raw is None:
   245	        override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2 = None
   246	    else:
   247	        override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2 = float(override_raw)
   248	        import math
   249	        if (
   250	            not math.isfinite(override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2)
   251	            or override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2 < 0.0
   252	        ):
   253	            raise ValueError(
   254	                "override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2 must be a finite "
   255	                "non-negative scalar (post-clamp σ_singh is "
   256	                f"non-negative by convention); got {override_raw!r}"
   257	            )
   258	    half_physical = (not apply_h_source) or (not apply_k_sink)
   259	    if half_physical and manufactured_R_inj is None:
   260	        raise ValueError(

    99	ALPHA_R2 = 0.5
   100	
   101	# Parallel 2e/4e ORR kinetics (Ruggiero 2022, M3a.2 — 2026-05-07).
   102	# R_2e: O₂ + 2H⁺ + 2e⁻ → H₂O₂ (peroxide-producing 2e channel).
   103	# R_4e: O₂ + 4H⁺ + 4e⁻ → 2H₂O (direct 4e-to-water channel).  Both
   104	# pathways consume O₂ and H⁺ but only R_2e produces free H₂O₂; the 4e
   105	# channel proceeds via adsorbed *-OOH → *-OH → H₂O without releasing
   106	# free peroxide (Ruggiero §1).
   107	K0_PHYS_R2E = K0_PHYS_R1     # same rate as legacy R_1 (the 2e channel)

   114	                              # M3a.2 if magnitude is far off experimental.
   115	ALPHA_R4E = 0.5              # default placeholder; revisit in M4 with Tafel.

   119	E_EQ_R1_V = 0.68

   122	# Refines the legacy E_EQ_R1_V = 0.68 V to 0.695 V for the 2e channel.
   123	E_EQ_R2E_V = 0.695   # V vs RHE, Ruggiero 2022 §1 (2e: O₂ + 2H⁺ + 2e⁻ → H₂O₂)
   124	E_EQ_R4E_V = 1.23    # V vs RHE, Ruggiero 2022 §1 (4e: O₂ + 4H⁺ + 4e⁻ → 2H₂O)

   132	D_REF = D_O2                # m²/s (O₂ diffusivity as reference)
   133	C_SCALE = C_O2              # mol/m³ (O₂ bulk concentration as reference)
   134	K_SCALE = D_REF / L_REF     # m/s (velocity scale for k0 nondimensionalization)
   135

   157	# Steric (Bikerman) parameters
   158	A_DEFAULT = 0.01
   159	
   160	
   161	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   162	# Water self-ionization constants (Phase 6α — proton-condition variable)
   163	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   164	#
   165	# Homogeneous water self-ionization:  H₂O ⇌ H⁺ + OH⁻,
   166	# fast-equilibrium closure  c_H · c_OH = K_w  (concentration-Kw model).
   167	#
   168	# Phase 6α replaces the H⁺ NP residual with the proton-condition residual
   169	# for E = c_H − c_OH; the closure c_OH = K_w / c_H sources fresh H⁺ as
   170	# ORR consumes it, capping local pH around the experimental 4-9 range.
   171	# OH⁻ enters Poisson (z = −1) and Bikerman packing (a_OH · c_OH) but is
   172	# NOT a separate dynamic NP species.  See
   173	# docs/PHASE_6A_OH_WATER_IONIZATION_PLAN.md and
   174	# docs/CHATGPT_HANDOFF_25_phase-6a-water-ionization/FINAL_REVISION.md.
   175	#
   176	# Scaling chain:
   177	#   KW_MOLAR_SQUARED  : 1e-14   (mol/L)²   [textbook value at 25 °C]
   178	#   KW_PHYS           : 1e-8    (mol/m³)²  [× (1000 mol/m³ per mol/L)²]
   179	#   KW_HAT            : KW_PHYS / C_SCALE² ≈ 6.944e-9
   180	#
   181	# At pH 4 (C_HP_HAT ≈ 0.0833):  KW_HAT == C_HP_HAT · C_OH_BULK_HAT
   182	# ⇒ C_OH_BULK_HAT = KW_HAT / C_HP_HAT ≈ 8.333e-8
   183	# ⇔ c_OH_phys = 1e-7 mol/m³ (i.e. 1e-10 mol/L) — matches Kw at pH 4 ✓
   184	#
   185	# Diffusivity (Atkins / CRC 25 °C):  D_OH⁻ = 5.273e-9 m²/s.
   186	# Hard-sphere radius (Marcus):  r_OH = 1.76 Å.
   187	KW_MOLAR_SQUARED = 1.0e-14   # (mol/L)²
   188	KW_PHYS = KW_MOLAR_SQUARED * (1000.0 ** 2)  # (mol/m³)² = 1.0e-8
   189	D_OH = 5.273e-9              # m²/s
   190	
   191	# C_SCALE / D_REF / L_REF are defined above; KW_HAT / D_OH_HAT / A_OH_HAT
   192	# are derived from them.
   193	KW_HAT = KW_PHYS / (C_SCALE ** 2)
   194	D_OH_HAT = D_OH / D_REF
   195	
   196	# A_OH hard-sphere nondim:  a_phys = (4/3) π r³ N_A  in m³/mol;
   197	# a_nondim = a_phys · C_SCALE.   (Linsey ACS-CATL 2025 deck slide 13
   198	# convention; Marcus radius for OH⁻ = 1.76 Å.)
   199	import math as _math
   200	_AVOGADRO = 6.02214076e23                                       # /mol (CODATA)
   201	_A_OH_PHYS = (4.0 / 3.0) * _math.pi * (1.76e-10) ** 3 * _AVOGADRO  # m³/mol
   202	A_OH_HAT = _A_OH_PHYS * C_SCALE
   203	del _math, _AVOGADRO, _A_OH_PHYS
   204	
   205	# Bulk OH⁻ at pH 4 (derived; useful for IC / diagnostics).
   206	C_OH_BULK_HAT = KW_HAT / C_HP_HAT
   207	
   208	
   209	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   210	# Current density scale
   211	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   212	
   213	def compute_i_scale(
   214	    n_electrons: int = N_ELECTRONS,
   215	    d_ref: float = D_REF,
   216	    c_scale: float = C_SCALE,
   217	    l_ref: float = L_REF,
   218	) -> float:
   219	    """Compute current density conversion: dimensionless rate → mA/cm².
   220	
   221	    ``I_SCALE = n_e × F × D_ref × c_scale / L_ref × 0.1``
   222	    """
   223	    return n_electrons * F_CONST * d_ref * c_scale / l_ref * 0.1
   224	
   225	
   226	I_SCALE = compute_i_scale()

   279	        "exponent_clip":              exponent_clip,

   287	        "formulation":                formulation,
   288	        "initializer":                initializer,
   289	        "enable_water_ionization":    enable_water_ionization,
   290	        "kw_eff_hat":                 kw_eff_hat,
   291	        "d_oh_hat":                   d_oh_hat,
   292	        "a_oh_hat":                   a_oh_hat,
   293	        "enable_cation_hydrolysis":   enable_cation_hydrolysis,
   294	        "cation_hydrolysis_config":   cation_hydrolysis_config,
   295	        # Phase 6β v9 Gate 3C — λ continuation knob; ramps cation
   296	        # hydrolysis source from 0 → 1.  Default 0.0 so a freshly-
   297	        # built form with the Γ slot but no λ override is the same
   298	        # as the disabled-feature baseline (Γ pinned to 0).
   299	        "lambda_hydrolysis":          float(raw.get("lambda_hydrolysis", 0.0)),
   300	        # Phase 6β v9 Gate 3D — manufactured-source override for
   301	        # unit tests.  ``None`` (default) leaves the production
   302	        # R_net wired up.
   303	        "manufactured_R_inj":         manufactured_R_inj,
   304	        # Phase 6β step 6 plumbing-ablation flags (see prose above).
   305	        "apply_h_source":             apply_h_source,
   306	        "apply_k_sink":               apply_k_sink,
   307	        "override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2": override_sigma_singh_counts_pm2,
   308	    }
   309	
   310	
   311	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   312	# Phase 6β v9 Gate 1 — role-aware species lookup
   313	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   314	
   315	def _get_species_roles(params: Any, n_species: int) -> Optional[List[str]]:
   316	    """Read optional per-species role labels from ``bv_bc.species_roles``.
   317	
   318	    Phase 6β v9 Gate 1.  Returns the explicit roles list when set on the
   319	    config, or ``None`` to signal callers should fall back to legacy
   320	    z-inference.  Validates length matches ``n_species`` so a stale config
   321	    fails LOUDLY at form-build rather than silently mis-wiring the proton
   322	    index.
   323	    """
   324	    if not isinstance(params, dict):
   325	        return None
   326	    bv_raw = params.get("bv_bc", {})
   327	    if not isinstance(bv_raw, dict):
   328	        return None
   329	    roles_raw = bv_raw.get("species_roles", None)
   330	    if roles_raw is None:
   331	        return None
   332	    if not isinstance(roles_raw, (list, tuple)):
   333	        raise ValueError(
   334	            "bv_bc.species_roles must be a list of strings or None; "
   335	            f"got {type(roles_raw).__name__}"
   336	        )
   337	    roles = [str(r) for r in roles_raw]
   338	    if len(roles) != n_species:
   339	        raise ValueError(
   340	            f"bv_bc.species_roles length {len(roles)} does not match "
   341	            f"n_species {n_species}"
   342	        )
   343	    return roles
   344	
   345	
   346	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   347	# Multi-reaction BV config helpers
   348	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   349	
   350	def _get_bv_boltzmann_counterions_cfg(params: Any) -> list[dict]:
   351	    """Parse ``bv_bc.boltzmann_counterions`` — analytic Boltzmann ions in Poisson.
   352	
   353	    Each entry represents an inert ion that is treated as locally
   354	    equilibrated with the electrostatic potential (Poisson--Boltzmann
   355	    reduction) instead of being solved as a dynamic Nernst--Planck
   356	    unknown.  The ion contributes an additional charge density term
   357	    ``z * c_bulk * exp(-z * phi)`` (in nondimensional units, sign
   358	    consistent with the Poisson convention used by the forms modules)
   359	    to the right-hand side of Poisson's equation.
   360	
   361	    The exponent is symmetrically clamped at ``|phi| <= phi_clamp`` to
   362	    prevent floating-point overflow during Newton iteration.
   363	
   364	    Each list entry is a dict with keys:
   365	        z              (int)           — counterion charge number (e.g. -1).
   366	        c_bulk_nondim  (float)         — bulk concentration in nondim units.
   367	        phi_clamp      (float, optional, default 50.0) — exponent clamp.
   368	        steric_mode    (str, optional, default ``"ideal"``) — one of
   369	                       ``"ideal"`` (unbounded ``c_b * exp(-z*phi)``) or
   370	                       ``"bikerman"`` (steric-aware closure that respects
   371	                       the Bikerman packing fraction; see
   372	                       ``docs/steric_analytic_clo4_reduction_handoff.md``).
   373	        a_nondim       (float, required when ``steric_mode='bikerman'``)
   374	                       — the counterion's Bikerman steric size (nondim).
   375	                       Ignored when ``steric_mode='ideal'``.
   376	
   377	    The ``theta_b > 0`` precondition for the bikerman closure is NOT
   378	    validated here (this parser does not see the dynamic-species
   379	    ``a_vals`` or ``c0`` needed to compute it); that validation lives
   380	    in the helper that constructs the closure expression.
   381	
   382	    Returns ``[]`` when not configured (no Boltzmann counterions).
   383	    """
   384	    if not isinstance(params, dict):
   385	        return []
   386	    bv_raw = params.get("bv_bc", {})
   387	    if not isinstance(bv_raw, dict):
   388	        return []
   389	    raw = bv_raw.get("boltzmann_counterions", [])
   390	    if raw in (None, [], ()):
   391	        return []
   392	    if not isinstance(raw, list):
   393	        raise ValueError(
   394	            "bv_bc.boltzmann_counterions must be a list of dicts."
   395	        )
   396	    out: list[dict] = []
   397	    for j, entry in enumerate(raw):
   398	        if not isinstance(entry, dict):
   399	            raise ValueError(
   400	                f"bv_bc.boltzmann_counterions[{j}] must be a dict."
   401	            )
   402	        if "z" not in entry:
   403	            raise ValueError(
   404	                f"bv_bc.boltzmann_counterions[{j}] missing required key 'z'."
   405	            )
   406	        if "c_bulk_nondim" not in entry:
   407	            raise ValueError(
   408	                f"bv_bc.boltzmann_counterions[{j}] missing required key 'c_bulk_nondim'."
   409	            )
   410	        z_val = int(entry["z"])
   411	        c_bulk = float(entry["c_bulk_nondim"])
   412	        phi_clamp = float(entry.get("phi_clamp", 50.0))
   413	        if c_bulk < 0:
   414	            raise ValueError(
   415	                f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}].c_bulk_nondim must be non-negative; got {c_bulk}"
   416	            )
   417	        if phi_clamp <= 0:
   418	            raise ValueError(
   419	                f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}].phi_clamp must be positive; got {phi_clamp}"
   420	            )
   421	        steric_mode = str(entry.get("steric_mode", "ideal")).strip().lower()
   422	        if steric_mode not in ("ideal", "bikerman"):
   423	            raise ValueError(
   424	                f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}].steric_mode must be 'ideal' or "
   425	                f"'bikerman'; got {steric_mode!r}"
   426	            )
   427	        a_nondim_raw = entry.get("a_nondim", None)
   428	        if steric_mode == "bikerman":
   429	            if a_nondim_raw is None:
   430	                raise ValueError(
   431	                    f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}] with steric_mode='bikerman' "
   432	                    f"requires 'a_nondim'."
   433	                )
   434	            a_nondim = float(a_nondim_raw)
   435	            if a_nondim <= 0:
   436	                raise ValueError(
   437	                    f"boltzmann_counterions[{j}].a_nondim must be positive; "
   438	                    f"got {a_nondim}"
   439	                )
   440	        else:
   441	            a_nondim = float(a_nondim_raw) if a_nondim_raw is not None else None
   442	        out.append({
   443	            "z": z_val,
   444	            "c_bulk_nondim": c_bulk,
   445	            "phi_clamp": phi_clamp,
   446	            "steric_mode": steric_mode,
   447	            "a_nondim": a_nondim,
   448	        })
   449	    return out
   450	
   451	
   452	def _get_bv_reactions_cfg(params: Any, n_species: int) -> list[dict] | None:
   453	    """Parse multi-reaction BV config from ``bv_bc.reactions``.
   454	
   455	    Returns a list of reaction dicts if present, or None to signal
   456	    that the caller should use the legacy per-species path.
   457	    """
   458	    if not isinstance(params, dict):
   459	        return None
   460	    raw = params.get("bv_bc", {})
   461	    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
   462	        return None
   463	    reactions_raw = raw.get("reactions")
   464	    if reactions_raw is None:
   465	        return None
   466	    if not isinstance(reactions_raw, list) or len(reactions_raw) == 0:
   467	        return None
   468	
   469	    reactions = []
   470	    for j, rxn in enumerate(reactions_raw):
   471	        cat = rxn.get("cathodic_species")
   472	        anod = rxn.get("anodic_species")
   473	        if cat is None:
   474	            raise ValueError(f"Reaction {j}: 'cathodic_species' is required")
   475	        cat_idx = int(cat)
   476	        if cat_idx < 0 or cat_idx >= n_species:
   477	            raise ValueError(
   478	                f"Reaction {j}: cathodic_species {cat_idx} out of range "
   479	                f"[0, {n_species})"
   480	            )
   481	        anod_idx: int | None
   482	        if anod is None:
   483	            anod_idx = None
   484	        else:
   485	            anod_idx = int(anod)
   486	            if anod_idx < 0 or anod_idx >= n_species:
   487	                raise ValueError(
   488	                    f"Reaction {j}: anodic_species {anod_idx} out of range "
   489	                    f"[0, {n_species})"
   490	                )
   491	        stoi = rxn.get("stoichiometry")
   492	        if stoi is None:
   493	            raise ValueError(f"Reaction {j}: 'stoichiometry' is required")
   494	        if len(stoi) != n_species:
   495	            raise ValueError(
   496	                f"Reaction {j}: stoichiometry length {len(stoi)} != n_species {n_species}"
   497	            )
   498	        # Optional cathodic concentration factors: e.g. (c_H+/c_ref)^2
   499	        cat_conc_factors_raw = rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", [])
   500	        cat_conc_factors = []
   501	        for f_cfg in cat_conc_factors_raw:
   502	            sp_idx = f_cfg.get("species")
   503	            if sp_idx is None:
   504	                raise ValueError(
   505	                    f"Reaction {j}: cathodic_conc_factors entry missing 'species'"
   506	                )
   507	            if int(sp_idx) < 0 or int(sp_idx) >= n_species:
   508	                raise ValueError(
   509	                    f"Reaction {j}: cathodic_conc_factors species {sp_idx} "
   510	                    f"out of range [0, {n_species})"
   511	                )
   512	            cat_conc_factors.append({
   513	                "species": int(sp_idx),
   514	                "power": int(f_cfg.get("power", 1)),
   515	                "c_ref_nondim": float(f_cfg.get("c_ref_nondim", 1.0)),
   516	            })
   517	
   518	        alpha_val = float(rxn.get("alpha", 0.5))
   519	        if not (0.0 < alpha_val <= 1.0):
   520	            raise ValueError(f"alpha must be in (0, 1]; got {alpha_val}")
   521	        n_e = int(rxn.get("n_electrons", 2))
   522	        if n_e <= 0:
   523	            raise ValueError(f"Reaction {j}: n_electrons must be positive; got {n_e}")
   524	        reactions.append({
   525	            "k0": float(rxn.get("k0", 1e-5)),
   526	            "alpha": alpha_val,
   527	            "cathodic_species": cat_idx,
   528	            "anodic_species": anod_idx,
   529	            "c_ref": float(rxn.get("c_ref", 1.0)),
   530	            "stoichiometry": [int(s) for s in stoi],
   531	            "n_electrons": n_e,
   532	            "reversible": _bool(rxn.get("reversible", True)),
   533	            "cathodic_conc_factors": cat_conc_factors,
   534	            "E_eq_v": float(rxn.get("E_eq_v", 0.0)),
   535	        })
   536	    return reactions

   817	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   818	# Parallel 2e/4e ORR reaction set (Ruggiero 2022, M3a.2 — 2026-05-07)
   819	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   820	#
   821	# Used by passing ``bv_reactions=PARALLEL_2E_4E_REACTIONS`` to
   822	# ``make_bv_solver_params`` to override the legacy sequential R_1 + R_2
   823	# topology with the deck/paper-aligned parallel 2e + 4e topology.
   824	#
   825	# Stoichiometry conventions (per-species int list, length n_species=3):
   826	#   index 0 = O₂, index 1 = H₂O₂, index 2 = H⁺
   827	#   negative = consumed at cathode, positive = produced at cathode
   828	#
   829	# R_2e: O₂ + 2H⁺ + 2e⁻ → H₂O₂        stoichiometry [-1, +1, -2], n_e = 2
   830	# R_4e: O₂ + 4H⁺ + 4e⁻ → 2H₂O        stoichiometry [-1,  0, -4], n_e = 4
   831	#
   832	# H+ stoichiometric concentration factor is included on each reaction
   833	# with ``power = n_electrons`` (acid-form ORR consumes one H+ per electron).
   834	# Ruggiero §1 also lists alkaline-form rate laws; not modeled here.
   835	#
   836	# k0_R4e is a PRIOR-SELECTED placeholder (= K0_HAT_R2E) — not calibrated
   837	# to any data.  Per H18 V4: k0_4e is weakly identified from page-15
   838	# peroxide alone; calibrate against disk current / selectivity / Tafel
   839	# slope in M4.  Sweep K0_HAT_R4E ∈ {1, 5, 10} × K0_HAT_R2E in M3a.2 if
   840	# magnitude is far off experimental.
   841	
   842	PARALLEL_2E_4E_REACTIONS: List[Dict[str, Any]] = [
   843	    {

   674	# closure  c_b * exp(phi) * (1-A_dyn) / (theta_b + a_b * c_b * exp(phi))
   675	# instead of the unbounded ideal Boltzmann.  Drop-in replacement for
   676	# DEFAULT_CLO4_BOLTZMANN_COUNTERION when the residual should respect
   677	# steric saturation at high anodic V_RHE.  See

   686	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   687	# Cs+ / SO4²⁻ multi-ion analytic counterion entries (fast-realignment plan
   688	# §2.2, 2026-05-08).  Production-target electrolyte per Ruggiero 2022 §2 and
   689	# the Seitz/Mangan data-folder audit (K₂SO₄ → CsSO₄ in the Linsey deck;
   690	# never ClO₄⁻).
   691	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   692	#
   693	# Hard-sphere ``a_phys = (4/3) π r³ N_A`` in m³/mol; ``a_nondim = a_phys * C_SCALE``.
   694	# Hydrated radii from Linsey 2025 ACS-CATL deck slide 13:
   695	#     Li⁺ 3.4 Å, Na⁺ 2.8 Å, K⁺ 2.3 Å, Cs⁺ 2.2 Å.
   696	# SO₄²⁻ at r = 2.4 Å (Marcus, placeholder pending Linsey-deck check).
   697	#
   698	# Bulk concentrations per Ruggiero §2 (I = 0.3 M, K₂SO₄ baseline; the
   699	# realignment uses Cs⁺ since that's the deck's fast-realignment target):
   700	#   c_SO4²⁻ = 100 mol/m³ ; electroneutrality fixes c_Cs⁺ = 199.9 mol/m³
   701	#   (with H⁺ = 0.1 mol/m³ from pH 4 contributing the remaining +1).
   702	# Verify ionic strength: I = ½ Σ z²c = ½(199.9 + 0.1 + 4·100) = 300 mol/m³
   703	#                       = 0.3 M ✓
   704	# Verify bulk packing: a_Cs · c_Cs_HAT + a_SO4 · c_SO4_HAT
   705	#                    = 3.23e-5 · 166.58 + 4.20e-5 · 83.33

   712	C_CSPLUS_HAT = C_CSPLUS / C_SCALE
   713	C_SO4_HAT    = C_SO4 / C_SCALE

  1160	        (default), at most ONE bikerman counterion entry is allowed —

  1162	        When True, multiple bikerman entries are accepted and the

  1174	        coefficient and I_SCALE).  See

  1176	    enable_water_ionization:
  1177	        Phase 6α opt-in.  When False (default), the residual is
  1178	        byte-equivalent to the pre-Phase-6α stack — existing tests, the
  1179	        production ClO₄⁻ stack, and the Cs⁺/SO₄²⁻ multi-ion stack are
  1180	        untouched.  When True, the H⁺ NP residual is replaced by the
  1181	        proton-condition residual on E = c_H − c_OH with the
  1182	        fast-equilibrium closure c_OH = K_w / c_H, and OH⁻ contributes
  1183	        to Poisson (z = −1) and Bikerman packing.  Forward runs with

   263	
   264	    Phase 6β v9 Gate 1: optional ``roles`` field carries explicit per-
   265	    species role labels (e.g. ``"neutral"``, ``"proton"``, ``"counterion"``)
   266	    used by role-aware solver helpers to disambiguate species when
   267	    ``z_vals`` alone cannot.  The K2SO4 stack has BOTH H⁺ and K⁺ at
   268	    ``z=+1``; without explicit roles the legacy ``z=+1 ⇒ proton``
   269	    inference is ambiguous and hard-fails at form-build time.
   270	
   271	    ``roles=None`` (default) preserves byte-equivalence for every existing
   272	    call site: the role-aware helpers fall back to legacy z-inference.
   273	    """
   274	
   275	    n_species: int
   276	    z_vals: List[int]
   277	    d_vals_hat: List[float]
   278	    a_vals_hat: List[float]
   279	    c0_vals_hat: List[float]
   280	    stoichiometry_r1: List[int]
   281	    stoichiometry_r2: List[int]
   282	    # Legacy per-species fallback for _get_bv_cfg
   283	    k0_legacy: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
   284	    alpha_legacy: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
   285	    stoichiometry_legacy: List[int] = field(default_factory=list)
   286	    c_ref_legacy: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
   287	    # Phase 6β v9 Gate 1 — explicit per-species role labels.
   288	    roles: Optional[List[str]] = None
   289	
   290	    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
   291	        if self.roles is not None and len(self.roles) != self.n_species:
   292	            raise ValueError(
   293	                f"SpeciesConfig.roles length {len(self.roles)} does not match "
   294	                f"n_species {self.n_species} (roles={list(self.roles)!r})"
   295	            )
   296	
   297	
   298	def resolve_role_index(
   299	    roles: Optional[Sequence[str]],
   300	    z_vals: Sequence[int],
   301	    target_role: str,
   302	) -> int:
   303	    """Resolve the species index matching ``target_role``.
   304	
   305	    Two paths:
   306	
   307	    * ``roles is None`` — legacy z-inference.  Currently supports only
   308	      ``target_role='proton'`` (z=+1, exactly one match required); other
   309	      targets raise NotImplementedError.  Existing call sites that need
   310	      counterion lookup with no roles continue to use the inline
   311	      ``z_vals[i] < 0`` check (preserves byte-equivalence for the ClO₄⁻
   312	      stack).
   313	    * ``roles is not None`` — explicit role lookup, case-insensitive on
   314	      the ``roles`` list.  Raises if zero or multiple matches.
   315	
   316	    Phase 6β v9 Gate 1 motivation: with both H⁺ and K⁺ at z=+1 in the
   317	    K2SO4 stack, ``resolve_h_index`` cannot uniquely identify the proton
   318	    from ``z_vals`` alone.  Passing ``roles`` disambiguates and lets the
   319	    solver build cleanly.
   320	    """
   321	    if roles is None:
   322	        if target_role != "proton":
   323	            raise NotImplementedError(
   324	                f"resolve_role_index: legacy z-inference (roles=None) only "
   325	                f"supports target_role='proton'; got {target_role!r}.  Pass "
   326	                f"an explicit roles list."
   327	            )
   328	        candidates = [
   329	            i for i, zv in enumerate(z_vals)
   330	            if abs(float(zv) - 1.0) < 1e-12
   331	        ]
   332	        if not candidates:
   333	            raise ValueError(
   334	                f"resolve_role_index(target_role='proton', roles=None) "
   335	                f"requires a species with z=+1; none found in "
   336	                f"z_vals={list(z_vals)}."
   337	            )
   338	        if len(candidates) > 1:
   339	            raise ValueError(
   340	                f"resolve_role_index(target_role='proton', roles=None) "
   341	                f"requires exactly one species with z=+1; found "
   342	                f"{len(candidates)} (indices {candidates}).  Pass an "
   343	                f"explicit roles list to disambiguate."
   344	            )
   345	        return candidates[0]
   346	
   347	    target = str(target_role).strip().lower()
   348	    matches = [
   349	        i for i, r in enumerate(roles)
   350	        if str(r).strip().lower() == target
   351	    ]
   352	    if not matches:
   353	        raise ValueError(
   354	            f"resolve_role_index: no species with role={target_role!r} in "
   355	            f"roles={list(roles)}."
   356	        )
   357	    if len(matches) > 1:
   358	        raise ValueError(
   359	            f"resolve_role_index: multiple species with role={target_role!r} "
   360	            f"in roles={list(roles)} (indices {matches}); roles must be unique."

   361	        )
   362	    return matches[0]

   415	
   416	def _make_bv_convergence_cfg(*, softplus: bool = False,
   417	                              log_rate: bool = False,
   418	                              u_clamp: float = 100.0,
   419	                              formulation: str = "concentration",
   420	                              initializer: str = "linear_phi",
   421	                              domain_height_hat: float = 1.0,
   422	                              enable_water_ionization: bool = False,
   423	                              kw_eff_hat: float = KW_HAT,
   424	                              d_oh_hat: float = D_OH_HAT,
   425	                              a_oh_hat: float = A_OH_HAT,
   426	                              enable_cation_hydrolysis: bool = False,
   427	                              cation_hydrolysis_config: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
   428	                              lambda_hydrolysis: float = 0.0) -> Dict[str, Any]:
   429	    """Standard BV convergence config sub-dict.
   430	
   431	    Parameters
   432	    ----------
   433	    softplus:
   434	        If True, adds ``softplus_regularization`` to soften the eps_c floor.
   435	    log_rate:
   436	        If True, sets ``bv_log_rate=True`` so the BV residual is built in
   437	        log-rate form (see Change 3 in WeekOfApr27/PNP Inverse Solver
   438	        Revised.tex).  Compatible with both formulations but only useful
   439	        in tandem with the log-c primary variable.
   440	    u_clamp:
   441	        Symmetric clamp on ``u_i = ln c_i`` to prevent overflow during
   442	        Newton iteration in the log-c bulk terms.  Has no effect when
   443	        ``formulation="concentration"``.
   444	    formulation:
   445	        ``"concentration"`` (default, legacy), ``"logc"`` (production), or
   446	        ``"logc_muh"`` (experimental — proton electrochemical-potential
   447	        primary variable; Phase 1 routes to ``logc`` with a warning).
   448	        Selects which weak-form backend the dispatcher in
   449	        ``Forward.bv_solver`` uses.
   450	    domain_height_hat:
   451	        Mesh y-extent in nondim coords (= ``L_eff_m / L_REF``).  Default
   452	        ``1.0`` reproduces the legacy unit-cube mesh (transport-domain
   453	        height = L_REF).  The L_eff sweep uses smaller values
   454	        (e.g. ``0.16`` ≈ 16 µm at L_REF = 100 µm) to test the H+ Levich
   455	        ceiling hypothesis without rescaling the global L_REF.  Read by
   456	        ``forms_logc.py`` / ``forms_logc_muh.py`` ICs to normalize the
   457	        outer linear interpolation by ``y / domain_height_hat`` so the
   458	        bulk anchor lands at the mesh top regardless of L_eff.
   459	    enable_water_ionization:
   460	        Phase 6α opt-in flag.  When True, the H⁺ NP residual is replaced
   461	        by the proton-condition residual on E = c_H − c_OH with the
   462	        fast-equilibrium closure c_OH = K_w / c_H, OH⁻ enters Poisson
   463	        (z = −1) and Bikerman packing (a_OH·c_OH).  When False
   464	        (default), the residual / Poisson / packing are byte-equivalent
   465	        to the pre-Phase-6α stack.  See
   466	        ``docs/PHASE_6A_OH_WATER_IONIZATION_PLAN.md``.
   467	    kw_eff_hat:
   468	        Continuation-controlled K_w in nondim units.  Defaults to the
   469	        physical ``KW_HAT`` (≈ 6.94e-9).  The anchor builder ramps this
   470	        from a tiny floor (or 0) up to ``KW_HAT`` to keep Newton in a
   471	        well-posed regime; production runs leave the default.  Ignored
   472	        unless ``enable_water_ionization`` is True.
   473	    d_oh_hat, a_oh_hat:
   474	        OH⁻ nondim diffusivity and hard-sphere size.  Default to
   475	        ``D_OH_HAT`` / ``A_OH_HAT`` (5.273e-9 m²/s and r=1.76 Å Marcus).
   476	        Ignored unless ``enable_water_ionization`` is True.
   477	    """
   478	    cfg: Dict[str, Any] = {
   479	        "clip_exponent": True,
   480	        # exponent_clip = 100.0 is the only PC-trustworthy setting:
   481	        # at clip=50 (production until 2026-05-04) PC is fictitious
   482	        # below V_RHE = -0.1 V (sign-flipped, 3-4 OOM off; CD is OK).
   483	        # Do not lower this for forward runs whose PC will be compared
   484	        # against experiment.  See docs/clipping_conventions.md.
   485	        "exponent_clip": 100.0,
   486	        "regularize_concentration": True,
   487	        "conc_floor": 1e-12,
   488	        "use_eta_in_bv": True,
   489	        "bv_log_rate": log_rate,
   490	        "u_clamp": u_clamp,
   491	        "formulation": str(formulation).strip().lower(),
   492	        "initializer": str(initializer).strip().lower(),
   493	        "domain_height_hat": float(domain_height_hat),
   494	        "enable_water_ionization": bool(enable_water_ionization),
   495	        "kw_eff_hat": float(kw_eff_hat),
   496	        "d_oh_hat": float(d_oh_hat),
   497	        "a_oh_hat": float(a_oh_hat),
   498	        "enable_cation_hydrolysis": bool(enable_cation_hydrolysis),
   499	        "cation_hydrolysis_config": cation_hydrolysis_config,
   500	        "lambda_hydrolysis": float(lambda_hydrolysis),
   501	    }
   502	    if softplus:
   503	        cfg["softplus_regularization"] = True
   504	    return cfg
   505	
   506	
   507	def _make_nondim_cfg() -> Dict[str, Any]:
   508	    """Standard nondimensionalization config sub-dict."""
   509	    return {
   510	        "enabled": True,
   511	        "diffusivity_scale_m2_s": D_REF,
   512	        "concentration_scale_mol_m3": C_SCALE,
   513	        "length_scale_m": L_REF,
   514	        "potential_scale_v": V_T,
   515	        "kappa_scale_m_s": K_SCALE,
   516	        "time_scale_s": L_REF**2 / D_REF,
   517	        "kappa_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   518	        "diffusivity_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   519	        "concentration_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   520	        "potential_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   521	        "time_inputs_are_dimensionless": True,
   522	    }

   524	
   525	def _make_bv_bc_cfg(
   526	    species: SpeciesConfig,
   527	    *,
   528	    k0_hat_r1: float = K0_HAT_R1,
   529	    k0_hat_r2: float = K0_HAT_R2,
   530	    alpha_r1: float = ALPHA_R1,
   531	    alpha_r2: float = ALPHA_R2,
   532	    E_eq_r1: float = E_EQ_R1_V,
   533	    E_eq_r2: float = E_EQ_R2_V,
   534	    c_hp_hat: float = C_HP_HAT,
   535	    electrode_marker: int = 3,
   536	    concentration_marker: int = 4,
   537	    ground_marker: int = 4,
   538	    boltzmann_counterions: Optional[Sequence[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
   539	    stern_capacitance_f_m2: Optional[float] = None,
   540	    include_h_factor: Optional[bool] = None,
   541	    bv_reactions: Optional[Sequence[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
   542	) -> Dict[str, Any]:
   543	    """Build the ``bv_bc`` config sub-dict for 2-reaction BV.
   544	
   545	    Parameters
   546	    ----------
   547	    boltzmann_counterions:
   548	        Optional list of analytic-Boltzmann counterion entries for Poisson
   549	        (Poisson-Boltzmann-Nernst-Planck reduction).  Each entry is a dict
   550	        with keys ``z`` and ``c_bulk_nondim``.  When provided, the forms
   551	        modules add a residual ``-charge_rhs * z * c_bulk * exp(-z*phi)``
   552	        per entry to Poisson's equation.  See
   553	        ``Forward/bv_solver/boltzmann.py``.
   554	    stern_capacitance_f_m2:
   555	        Optional compact-layer Stern capacitance in physical units
   556	        ``F/m²`` (1 F/m² = 100 µF/cm²).  When ``None`` the cfg key is
   557	        omitted entirely and the no-Stern Dirichlet BC ``phi_s = phi_m``
   558	        is used (the idealised C_S → ∞ limit).  When set to a positive
   559	        value, ``forms_logc.py`` switches to a Robin BC that lets the
   560	        compact-layer voltage drop ``phi_m - phi_s`` be solved for, and
   561	        the BV overpotential becomes ``eta = phi_applied - phi - E_eq``.
   562	        A value of ``0.0`` is written through but is runtime-inactive
   563	        (``forms_logc.py`` requires ``> 0`` to activate Stern).
   564	    include_h_factor:
   565	        Whether to attach H+ stoichiometric concentration factors to each
   566	        reaction's ``cathodic_conc_factors``.  Defaults to True for
   567	        ``species.n_species >= 3`` (works for both the 4sp charged preset
   568	        and the 3sp logc+Boltzmann preset).
   569	    bv_reactions:
   570	        Optional list of fully-specified reaction dicts.  When set, takes
   571	        precedence over the legacy ``k0_hat_r{1,2}, alpha_r{1,2},
   572	        E_eq_r{1,2}`` keyword bundle and the species ``stoichiometry_r{1,2}``
   573	        fields — the BV residual loop iterates over this list directly.
   574	        Each entry must provide ``k0`` (nondim), ``alpha``, ``n_electrons``,
   575	        ``E_eq_v`` (V vs RHE), ``cathodic_species``, ``anodic_species``
   576	        (or None), ``stoichiometry`` (per-species int list of length
   577	        ``n_species``), ``c_ref``, ``reversible``, and optionally
   578	        ``cathodic_conc_factors``.  Used by the parallel-2e/4e topology
   579	        (M3a.2, 2026-05-07) to bypass the hardcoded sequential R_1/R_2
   580	        construction; see ``PARALLEL_2E_4E_REACTIONS`` below.
   581	    """
   582	    if bv_reactions is not None:
   583	        # Caller-supplied reactions list takes precedence over the legacy
   584	        # R_1/R_2 keyword construction.  Deep-copy each entry so internal
   585	        # mutation (e.g. nondimensionalization in
   586	        # ``_add_bv_reactions_scaling_to_transform``) does not leak
   587	        # back to the caller's literal.
   588	        reactions_out = []
   589	        for rxn in bv_reactions:
   590	            rxn_copy = dict(rxn)
   591	            # Deep-copy nested factor lists so they cannot share state.
   592	            if "cathodic_conc_factors" in rxn_copy and rxn_copy["cathodic_conc_factors"]:
   593	                rxn_copy["cathodic_conc_factors"] = [
   594	                    dict(f) for f in rxn_copy["cathodic_conc_factors"]
   595	                ]
   596	            if "stoichiometry" in rxn_copy:
   597	                rxn_copy["stoichiometry"] = list(rxn_copy["stoichiometry"])
   598	            reactions_out.append(rxn_copy)
   599	    else:
   600	        reaction_1: Dict[str, Any] = {
   601	            "k0": k0_hat_r1,
   602	            "alpha": alpha_r1,
   603	            "cathodic_species": 0,
   604	            "anodic_species": 1,
   605	            "c_ref": 1.0,
   606	            "stoichiometry": list(species.stoichiometry_r1),
   607	            "n_electrons": N_ELECTRONS,
   608	            "reversible": True,
   609	            "E_eq_v": E_eq_r1,
   610	        }
   611	        reaction_2: Dict[str, Any] = {
   612	            "k0": k0_hat_r2,
   613	            "alpha": alpha_r2,
   614	            "cathodic_species": 1,
   615	            "anodic_species": None,
   616	            "c_ref": 0.0,
   617	            "stoichiometry": list(species.stoichiometry_r2),
   618	            "n_electrons": N_ELECTRONS,
   619	            "reversible": False,
   620	            "E_eq_v": E_eq_r2,
   621	        }
   622	
   623	        # H+ stoichiometric concentration factor.  Apply automatically when the
   624	        # species set has at least 3 species (i.e. tracks H+ explicitly), unless
   625	        # the caller overrides via include_h_factor.
   626	        if include_h_factor is None:
   627	            attach_h = species.n_species >= 3
   628	        else:
   629	            attach_h = bool(include_h_factor)
   630	        if attach_h:
   631	            h_factor = [{"species": 2, "power": 2, "c_ref_nondim": c_hp_hat}]
   632	            reaction_1["cathodic_conc_factors"] = h_factor
   633	            reaction_2["cathodic_conc_factors"] = [dict(f) for f in h_factor]
   634	
   635	        reactions_out = [reaction_1, reaction_2]
   636	
   637	    cfg: Dict[str, Any] = {
   638	        "reactions": reactions_out,
   639	        # Legacy per-species fallback (used by _get_bv_cfg for markers)
   640	        "k0": list(species.k0_legacy),
   641	        "alpha": list(species.alpha_legacy),
   642	        "stoichiometry": list(species.stoichiometry_legacy),
   643	        "c_ref": list(species.c_ref_legacy),
   644	        "E_eq_v": 0.0,
   645	        "electrode_marker": electrode_marker,
   646	        "concentration_marker": concentration_marker,
   647	        "ground_marker": ground_marker,
   648	    }
   649	    if boltzmann_counterions:
   650	        cfg["boltzmann_counterions"] = [dict(entry) for entry in boltzmann_counterions]
   651	    if stern_capacitance_f_m2 is not None:
   652	        cfg["stern_capacitance_f_m2"] = float(stern_capacitance_f_m2)
   653	    # Phase 6β v9 Gate 1: surface explicit per-species role labels so the
   654	    # solver-side resolvers can disambiguate stacks with two z=+1 species
   655	    # (K2SO4: H⁺ + K⁺).  Absent ``species.roles`` falls through and the
   656	    # legacy z-inference path stays byte-equivalent.
   657	    if species.roles is not None:
   658	        cfg["species_roles"] = list(species.roles)
   659	    return cfg
   660

     1	"""SolverParams — frozen dataclass for PNP solver parameters.
     2	
     3	Entry layout
     4	------------
     5	Index  Name             Type   Description
     6	-----  ---------------  -----  ------------------------------------------
     7	  0    n_species        int    Number of ionic species
     8	  1    order            int    Finite-element polynomial order
     9	  2    dt               float  Time step (physical or model, see nondim)
    10	  3    t_end            float  Final simulation time
    11	  4    z_vals           list   Per-species charge numbers
    12	  5    D_vals           list   Per-species diffusivities
    13	  6    a_vals           list   Per-species activities (unused, kept for API compat)
    14	  7    phi_applied      float  Applied boundary voltage
    15	  8    c0_vals          list   Initial bulk concentrations
    16	  9    phi0             float  Reference potential (echoed, kept in sync with phi_applied
    17	                               by configure_robin_solver_params)
    18	 10    solver_options   dict   PETSc/SNES options + ``robin_bc`` + ``nondim`` sub-dicts
    19	"""
    20	
    21	from __future__ import annotations
    22	
    23	import copy
    24	import dataclasses
    25	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    26	from typing import Any, Dict, Iterator, List, Optional, Sequence, Union
    27	
    28	
    29	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    30	class SolverParams:
    31	    """Frozen dataclass for PNP solver parameters.
    32	
    33	    Construct via :func:`build_default_solver_params` in :mod:`Inverse.inference_runner`,
    34	    or directly::
    35	
    36	        params = SolverParams(
    37	            n_species=2, order=1, dt=0.1, t_end=20.0,
    38	            z_vals=[1, -1], D_vals=[1.0, 1.0], a_vals=[0.0, 0.0],
    39	            phi_applied=0.05, c0_vals=[0.1, 0.1], phi0=0.05,
    40	            solver_options={...},
    41	        )
    42	        # Immutable: use replace helpers for mutation
    43	        new_params = params.with_phi_applied(0.10)
    44	    """
    45	
    46	    n_species: int
    47	    order: int
    48	    dt: float
    49	    t_end: float
    50	    z_vals: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
    51	    D_vals: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
    52	    a_vals: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
    53	    phi_applied: float = 0.0
    54	    c0_vals: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)
    55	    phi0: float = 0.0
    56	    solver_options: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    57	
    58	    _NAMES = (
    59	        "n_species", "order", "dt", "t_end",
    60	        "z_vals", "D_vals", "a_vals",
    61	        "phi_applied", "c0_vals", "phi0", "solver_options",
    62	    )
    63	    _N = len(_NAMES)  # 11
    64	
    65	    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
    66	        # Normalize types on construction (using object.__setattr__ since frozen)
    67	        object.__setattr__(self, "n_species", int(self.n_species))
    68	        object.__setattr__(self, "order", int(self.order))
    69	        object.__setattr__(self, "dt", float(self.dt))
    70	        object.__setattr__(self, "t_end", float(self.t_end))
    71	        object.__setattr__(self, "z_vals", list(self.z_vals))
    72	        object.__setattr__(self, "D_vals", list(self.D_vals))
    73	        object.__setattr__(self, "a_vals", list(self.a_vals))
    74	        object.__setattr__(self, "phi_applied", float(self.phi_applied))
    75	        object.__setattr__(self, "c0_vals", list(self.c0_vals))
    76	        object.__setattr__(self, "phi0", float(self.phi0))
    77	
    78	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    79	    # Backward compat: iteration, indexing, length
    80	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    81	
    82	    def __iter__(self) -> Iterator:
    83	        """Yield values in the same order as the original 11-entry list."""
    84	        return iter(self.to_list())
    85	
    86	    def __getitem__(self, index: int) -> Any:
    87	        """Support ``params[i]`` index access for backward compat."""
    88	        return self.to_list()[index]
    89	
    90	    def __setitem__(self, index: int, value: Any) -> None:
    91	        """Support ``params[i] = value`` for backward compat with code that
    92	        deep-copies then mutates. Uses object.__setattr__ to bypass frozen."""
    93	        name = self._NAMES[index]
    94	        if name in ("z_vals", "D_vals", "a_vals", "c0_vals"):
    95	            value = list(value)
    96	        elif name in ("n_species", "order"):
    97	            value = int(value)
    98	        elif name in ("dt", "t_end", "phi_applied", "phi0"):
    99	            value = float(value)
   100	        object.__setattr__(self, name, value)
   101	
   102	    def __len__(self) -> int:
   103	        return self._N
   104	
   105	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   106	    # Conversion helpers
   107	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   108	
   109	    def to_list(self) -> List[Any]:
   110	        """Return a plain 11-entry list (same order as the original layout)."""
   111	        return [
   112	            self.n_species,
   113	            self.order,
   114	            self.dt,
   115	            self.t_end,
   116	            self.z_vals,
   117	            self.D_vals,
   118	            self.a_vals,
   119	            self.phi_applied,
   120	            self.c0_vals,
   121	            self.phi0,
   122	            self.solver_options,
   123	        ]
   124	
   125	    @classmethod
   126	    def from_list(cls, params: Sequence[Any]) -> "SolverParams":
   127	        """Construct from a legacy 11-entry list or any sequence."""
   128	        if len(params) != cls._N:
   129	            raise ValueError(
   130	                f"Expected {cls._N}-entry solver params list; got length {len(params)}."
   131	            )
   132	        return cls(
   133	            n_species=params[0],
   134	            order=params[1],
   135	            dt=params[2],
   136	            t_end=params[3],
   137	            z_vals=params[4],
   138	            D_vals=params[5],
   139	            a_vals=params[6],
   140	            phi_applied=params[7],
   141	            c0_vals=params[8],
   142	            phi0=params[9],
   143	            solver_options=params[10],
   144	        )
   145	
   146	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   147	    # Deep copy
   148	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   149	
   150	    def deep_copy(self) -> "SolverParams":
   151	        """Return an independent deep copy."""
   152	        return SolverParams(
   153	            n_species=self.n_species,
   154	            order=self.order,
   155	            dt=self.dt,
   156	            t_end=self.t_end,
   157	            z_vals=copy.deepcopy(self.z_vals),
   158	            D_vals=copy.deepcopy(self.D_vals),
   159	            a_vals=copy.deepcopy(self.a_vals),
   160	            phi_applied=self.phi_applied,
   161	            c0_vals=copy.deepcopy(self.c0_vals),
   162	            phi0=self.phi0,
   163	            solver_options=copy.deepcopy(self.solver_options),
   164	        )
   165	
   166	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   167	    # Mutation helpers (return new frozen instances)
   168	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   169	
   170	    def with_phi_applied(self, phi: float) -> "SolverParams":
   171	        """Return a new SolverParams with updated phi_applied."""
   172	        return dataclasses.replace(self, phi_applied=float(phi))
   173	
   174	    def with_dt(self, dt: float) -> "SolverParams":
   175	        """Return a new SolverParams with updated dt."""
   176	        return dataclasses.replace(self, dt=float(dt))
   177	
   178	    def with_solver_options(self, opts: Dict[str, Any]) -> "SolverParams":
   179	        """Return a new SolverParams with updated solver_options."""
   180	        return dataclasses.replace(self, solver_options=opts)
   181	
   182	    def with_D_vals(self, D_vals: Sequence[float]) -> "SolverParams":
   183	        """Return a new SolverParams with updated D_vals."""
   184	        return dataclasses.replace(self, D_vals=list(D_vals))
   185	
   186	    def with_c0_vals(self, c0_vals: Sequence[float]) -> "SolverParams":
   187	        """Return a new SolverParams with updated c0_vals."""
   188	        return dataclasses.replace(self, c0_vals=list(c0_vals))
   189	
   190	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   191	    # Display
   192	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   193	
   194	    def __repr__(self) -> str:
   195	        return (
   196	            f"SolverParams(n_species={self.n_species}, order={self.order}, "
   197	            f"dt={self.dt}, t_end={self.t_end}, "
   198	            f"z_vals={self.z_vals}, D_vals={self.D_vals}, "
   199	            f"phi_applied={self.phi_applied}, c0_vals={self.c0_vals})"
   200	        )

codex
The key sign conventions look mostly consistent with the weak form, but I’m seeing a more serious mismatch around the Stern surface potential: with Stern enabled, the manufactured electrode `φ` is not the metal potential, so the BV exponent can be very different from the no-Stern MMS intuition. I’m checking the nondimensional reaction scaling to see whether the planned pre-flight bounds actually protect that.

     1	"""Nondimensionalization helpers for Butler-Volmer BV parameters."""
     2	
     3	from __future__ import annotations
     4	
     5	from Nondim.constants import FARADAY_CONSTANT, GAS_CONSTANT
     6	
     7	
     8	def _add_bv_scaling_to_transform(
     9	    scaling: dict,
    10	    bv_cfg: dict,
    11	    *,
    12	    n_species: int,
    13	    nondim_enabled: bool,
    14	    kappa_inputs_dimless: bool,
    15	    concentration_inputs_dimless: bool = False,
    16	) -> dict:
    17	    """Augment the ModelScaling dict with BV-specific nondimensional quantities.
    18	
    19	    Returns a new dict (does not mutate scaling).
    20	
    21	    Parameters
    22	    ----------
    23	    concentration_inputs_dimless:
    24	        If True, ``bv_bc.c_ref`` values are already dimensionless (divided by the
    25	        concentration scale) and must NOT be scaled again.  If False (default),
    26	        c_ref values are in physical units (mol/m³) and will be divided by
    27	        ``concentration_scale_mol_m3``.  Mirror of ``kappa_inputs_dimless``.
    28	    """
    29	    kappa_scale = scaling.get("kappa_scale_m_s", 1.0)
    30	    thermal_voltage_v = scaling.get("thermal_voltage_v", 0.02569)
    31	    conc_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
    32	    potential_scale = scaling.get("potential_scale_v", 1.0)
    33	
    34	    k0_raw = bv_cfg["k0_vals"]
    35	    c_ref_raw = bv_cfg["c_ref_vals"]
    36	    E_eq_raw = bv_cfg["E_eq_v"]
    37	
    38	    if not nondim_enabled:
    39	        # Dimensional: keep physical values, apply F/(RT) as EM prefactor for exponents
    40	        k0_model = k0_raw
    41	        c_ref_model = c_ref_raw
    42	        # Exponent in BV: exp(±α · F · η / RT).  In dimensional mode phi is in Volts.
    43	        # The BV exponent prefactor = F/(RT).
    44	        bv_exponent_scale = FARADAY_CONSTANT / (GAS_CONSTANT * scaling["temperature_k"])
    45	        E_eq_model = E_eq_raw
    46	    else:
    47	        # Nondimensional: k0 → k0/κ_scale, c_ref → c_ref/c_scale
    48	        # Exponent: exp(±α · η̂) where η̂ = η/V_T (dimensionless potential already)
    49	        # Since potential is already in V_T units, exponent prefactor = 1.
    50	        bv_exponent_scale = 1.0
    51	        if kappa_inputs_dimless:
    52	            k0_model = k0_raw  # already dimensionless
    53	        else:
    54	            k0_model = [v / kappa_scale for v in k0_raw]
    55	        if concentration_inputs_dimless:
    56	            c_ref_model = c_ref_raw  # already dimensionless, do not divide by c_scale
    57	        else:
    58	            c_ref_model = [v / conc_scale for v in c_ref_raw]
    59	        # E_eq in thermal voltage units
    60	        E_eq_model = E_eq_raw / potential_scale
    61	
    62	    # Stern layer capacitance nondimensionalization.
    63	    # Physical BC: epsilon * grad(phi).n = C_stern * (phi_m - phi)
    64	    #
    65	    # In the weak form, the IBP boundary integral is eps_coeff * grad(phi_hat).n.
    66	    # The Stern BC replaces this, so the weak-form coefficient must satisfy:
    67	    #   stern_model * (phi_m_hat - phi_hat) = eps_coeff * grad(phi_hat).n
    68	    #   = eps_coeff * (C_stern * L / epsilon) * (phi_m_hat - phi_hat)
    69	    #
    70	    # In dimensional mode:
    71	    #   eps_coeff = permittivity, boundary integral = permittivity * grad(phi).n
    72	    #   Physical BC: permittivity * grad(phi).n = C_stern * (phi_m - phi)
    73	    #   stern_model = C_stern  (direct physical value, used without eps_coeff)
    74	    #
    75	    # In nondim mode:
    76	    #   eps_coeff = epsilon * V_T / (F * c_ref * L^2)
    77	    #   stern_model = eps_coeff * C_stern * L / epsilon
    78	    #              = C_stern * V_T / (F * c_ref * L)  [dimensionless]
    79	    stern_raw = bv_cfg.get("stern_capacitance_f_m2")
    80	    if stern_raw is not None and float(stern_raw) > 0:
    81	        if not nondim_enabled:
    82	            stern_model = float(stern_raw)
    83	        else:
    84	            length_scale = scaling.get("length_scale_m", 1.0)
    85	            concentration_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
    86	            stern_model = (
    87	                float(stern_raw) * potential_scale
    88	                / (FARADAY_CONSTANT * concentration_scale * length_scale)
    89	            )
    90	    else:
    91	        stern_model = None
    92	
    93	    out = dict(scaling)
    94	    out["bv_k0_model_vals"] = k0_model
    95	    out["bv_c_ref_model_vals"] = c_ref_model
    96	    out["bv_exponent_scale"] = bv_exponent_scale
    97	    out["bv_E_eq_model"] = E_eq_model
    98	    out["bv_alpha_vals"] = bv_cfg["alpha_vals"]
    99	    out["bv_stoichiometry"] = bv_cfg["stoichiometry"]
   100	    out["bv_stern_capacitance_model"] = stern_model
   101	    return out
   102	
   103	
   104	def _add_bv_reactions_scaling_to_transform(
   105	    scaling: dict,
   106	    reactions: list[dict],
   107	    *,
   108	    nondim_enabled: bool,
   109	    kappa_inputs_dimless: bool,
   110	    concentration_inputs_dimless: bool = False,
   111	    E_eq_v: float = 0.0,
   112	) -> dict:
   113	    """Augment ModelScaling with multi-reaction BV quantities.
   114	
   115	    Each reaction's k0 and c_ref are nondimensionalized individually.
   116	    """
   117	    kappa_scale = scaling.get("kappa_scale_m_s", 1.0)
   118	    conc_scale = scaling.get("concentration_scale_mol_m3", 1.0)
   119	    potential_scale = scaling.get("potential_scale_v", 1.0)
   120	
   121	    if not nondim_enabled:
   122	        bv_exponent_scale = FARADAY_CONSTANT / (GAS_CONSTANT * scaling["temperature_k"])
   123	        E_eq_model = E_eq_v
   124	    else:
   125	        bv_exponent_scale = 1.0
   126	        E_eq_model = E_eq_v / potential_scale
   127	
   128	    scaled_reactions = []
   129	    for rxn in reactions:
   130	        srxn = dict(rxn)
   131	        if not nondim_enabled:
   132	            srxn["k0_model"] = rxn["k0"]
   133	            srxn["c_ref_model"] = rxn["c_ref"]
   134	            srxn["E_eq_model"] = rxn.get("E_eq_v", 0.0)
   135	        else:
   136	            if kappa_inputs_dimless:
   137	                srxn["k0_model"] = rxn["k0"]
   138	            else:
   139	                srxn["k0_model"] = rxn["k0"] / kappa_scale
   140	            if concentration_inputs_dimless:
   141	                srxn["c_ref_model"] = rxn["c_ref"]
   142	            else:
   143	                srxn["c_ref_model"] = rxn["c_ref"] / conc_scale
   144	            srxn["E_eq_model"] = rxn.get("E_eq_v", 0.0) / potential_scale
   145	
   146	        # Scale cathodic_conc_factors c_ref_nondim values
   147	        scaled_factors = []
   148	        for f_cfg in rxn.get("cathodic_conc_factors", []):
   149	            sf = dict(f_cfg)
   150	            if nondim_enabled and not concentration_inputs_dimless:
   151	                sf["c_ref_nondim"] = f_cfg["c_ref_nondim"] / conc_scale
   152	            else:
   153	                sf["c_ref_nondim"] = f_cfg["c_ref_nondim"]
   154	            scaled_factors.append(sf)
   155	        srxn["cathodic_conc_factors"] = scaled_factors
   156	
   157	        scaled_reactions.append(srxn)
   158	
   159	    # Stern layer capacitance is not set via the reactions path directly;
   160	    # it comes from the bv_cfg which is handled by build_forms.  Store None
   161	    # so downstream code can check uniformly.
   162	    out = dict(scaling)
   163	    out["bv_reactions"] = scaled_reactions
   164	    out["bv_exponent_scale"] = bv_exponent_scale
   165	    out["bv_E_eq_model"] = E_eq_model
   166	    if "bv_stern_capacitance_model" not in out:
   167	        out["bv_stern_capacitance_model"] = None
   168	    return out
