     1	"""Nondimensionalization transform for PNP solver parameters.
     2	
     3	This module converts physical (dimensional) or model-space solver parameters
     4	into a unified ``ModelScaling`` dict consumed by :mod:`Forward.robin_solver`.
     5	
     6	Nondimensional PDE form
     7	-----------------------
     8	Starting from the dimensional PNP system in a domain of length L_ref with
     9	reference diffusivity D_ref, concentration c_ref, and thermal voltage V_T = RT/F:
    10	
    11	**Nernst-Planck** (per species i, nondimensional)::
    12	
    13	    ∂ĉᵢ/∂t̂  +  ∇̂ · [ -D̂ᵢ (∇̂ĉᵢ  +  ẑᵢ · ĉᵢ · ∇̂φ̂) ]  =  0
    14	
    15	where  D̂ᵢ = Dᵢ/D_ref,  ĉᵢ = cᵢ/c_ref,  φ̂ = φ/V_T,  t̂ = t/t_ref,
    16	t_ref = L_ref²/D_ref.  The electromigration coefficient is implicitly 1
    17	because we scaled by V_T.
    18	
    19	**Poisson** (nondimensional)::
    20	
    21	    (λ_D/L_ref)² · Δφ̂  =  − Σᵢ zᵢ ĉᵢ
    22	
    23	where  λ_D = √(ε·V_T / (F·c_ref))  is the Debye length.
    24	
    25	In the code the Poisson residual is assembled as::
    26	
    27	    eps_coeff * (∇φ̂, ∇w)  −  rhs_coeff * Σᵢ zᵢ ĉᵢ w  =  0
    28	
    29	so  eps_coeff  corresponds to  (λ_D/L_ref)²  and  rhs_coeff = 1  in the
    30	nondimensional case.  See below for the dimensional (``enabled=False``) case.
    31	
    32	Dimensional mode (``enabled=False``)
    33	-------------------------------------
    34	When nondimensionalization is disabled, no input rescaling is applied.
    35	The PDE still must be assembled with correct coefficients:
    36	
    37	    ε · Δφ  =  F · Σᵢ zᵢ cᵢ          (SI)
    38	
    39	so the weak-form coefficients are::
    40	
    41	    eps_coeff  = ε  (absolute permittivity, e.g. ~6.95e-10 F/m for water)
    42	    rhs_coeff  = F  (Faraday constant, 96485 C/mol)
    43	
    44	**Note on previous behaviour**: prior to this refactor, ``enabled=False``
    45	incorrectly set ``eps_coeff=1.0``.  This had no effect for the symmetric
    46	two-species case (z=[+1,−1], equal concentrations) because the RHS is
    47	identically zero in that case.  It would produce a wrong Poisson equation
    48	for non-symmetric species.  The corrected default now uses the actual
    49	permittivity of water.  If you relied on ``eps_coeff=1.0`` in a non-symmetric
    50	setup, pass ``permittivity_f_m=1.0`` explicitly in ``solver_params[10]["nondim"]``.
    51	
    52	Input flags
    53	-----------
    54	All flags live in ``solver_params[10]["nondim"]``:
    55	
    56	``diffusivity_inputs_are_dimensionless`` (default ``False``)
    57	    If True, D_vals are already in model units (D̂ = D/D_ref).
    58	``concentration_inputs_are_dimensionless`` (default ``False``)
    59	    If True, c0_vals and c_inf are already in model units.
    60	``potential_inputs_are_dimensionless`` (default ``False``)
    61	    If True, phi_applied and phi0 are already in model units.
    62	``time_inputs_are_dimensionless`` (default ``False``)
    63	    If True, dt and t_end are already in model units.
    64	``kappa_inputs_are_dimensionless`` (default ``True``)
    65	    If True, kappa values are already dimensionless (model units).
    66	    **Default True** because the Robin kappa optimizer works in model space.
    67	    Set to False when passing physical kappa values in m/s.
    68	"""
    69	
    70	from __future__ import annotations
    71	
    72	import warnings
    73	from typing import Any, List, Mapping, Optional, Sequence
    74	
    75	import numpy as np
    76	
    77	from Nondim.constants import (
    78	    FARADAY_CONSTANT,
    79	    GAS_CONSTANT,
    80	    DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE_K,
    81	    VACUUM_PERMITTIVITY_F_PER_M,
    82	    DEFAULT_RELATIVE_PERMITTIVITY_WATER,
    83	)
    84	
    85	
    86	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    87	# Internal helpers
    88	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    89	
    90	def _as_list(values: Any, n: int, name: str) -> List[float]:
    91	    if np.isscalar(values):
    92	        return [float(values)] * n
    93	    try:
    94	        out = [float(v) for v in values]
    95	    except TypeError as exc:
    96	        raise ValueError(f"{name} must be a scalar or sequence of length {n}") from exc
    97	    if len(out) != n:
    98	        raise ValueError(f"{name} must have length {n}; got {len(out)}")
    99	    return out
   100	
   101	
   102	def _pos(value: Any, name: str) -> float:
   103	    v = float(value)
   104	    if v <= 0.0:
   105	        raise ValueError(f"{name} must be > 0; got {v}.")
   106	    return v
   107	
   108	
   109	def _bool(value: Any) -> bool:
   110	    if isinstance(value, bool):
   111	        return value
   112	    if isinstance(value, str):
   113	        norm = value.strip().lower()
   114	        if norm in {"1", "true", "yes", "on"}:
   115	            return True
   116	        if norm in {"0", "false", "no", "off", ""}:
   117	            return False
   118	        raise ValueError(
   119	            f"Cannot interpret {value!r} as bool. "
   120	            f"Use true/false, yes/no, on/off, or 1/0."
   121	        )
   122	    if value is None:
   123	        raise ValueError("Cannot interpret None as bool; provide an explicit value.")
   124	    return bool(value)
   125	
   126	
   127	def _get_nondim_cfg(params: Any) -> dict:
   128	    if not isinstance(params, dict):
   129	        return {}
   130	    cfg = params.get("nondim", {})
   131	    return cfg if isinstance(cfg, dict) else {}
   132	
   133	
   134	def _get_robin_cfg(params: Any, n_species: int) -> dict:
   135	    """Extract validated Robin BC settings from solver_params[10]."""
   136	    robin_raw: dict = {}
   137	    if isinstance(params, dict):
   138	        maybe = params.get("robin_bc", {})
   139	        if isinstance(maybe, dict):
   140	            robin_raw = maybe
   141	        kappa = robin_raw.get("kappa", params.get("robin_kappa", 1.0))
   142	        c_inf = robin_raw.get("c_inf", params.get("robin_c_inf", 0.01))
   143	        electrode_marker = robin_raw.get(
   144	            "electrode_marker", params.get("robin_electrode_marker", 1)
   145	        )
   146	        concentration_marker = robin_raw.get(
   147	            "concentration_marker", params.get("robin_concentration_marker", 3)
   148	        )
   149	        ground_marker = robin_raw.get(
   150	            "ground_marker", params.get("robin_ground_marker", 3)
   151	        )
   152	    else:
   153	        kappa = 1.0
   154	        c_inf = 0.01
   155	        electrode_marker = 1
   156	        concentration_marker = 3
   157	        ground_marker = 3
   158	
   159	    return {
   160	        "kappa_vals": _as_list(kappa, n_species, "robin_kappa"),
   161	        "c_inf_vals": _as_list(c_inf, n_species, "robin_c_inf"),
   162	        "electrode_marker": int(electrode_marker),
   163	        "concentration_marker": int(concentration_marker),
   164	        "ground_marker": int(ground_marker),
   165	    }
   166	
   167	
   168	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   169	# Public API
   170	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   171	
   172	def build_model_scaling(
   173	    *,
   174	    params: Any,
   175	    n_species: int,
   176	    dt: float,
   177	    t_end: float,
   178	    D_vals: Sequence[float],
   179	    c0_vals: Sequence[float],
   180	    phi_applied: float,
   181	    phi0: float,
   182	    robin: Optional[Mapping[str, Any]] = None,
   183	) -> dict:
   184	    """Convert physical solver inputs to model-space values for PDE assembly.
   185	
   186	    This function is the single authoritative place where nondimensionalization
   187	    is applied.  It reads the ``solver_params[10]["nondim"]`` config block and
   188	    returns a ``ModelScaling`` dict used by :func:`Forward.robin_solver.build_forms`.
   189	
   190	    Parameters
   191	    ----------
   192	    params:
   193	        ``solver_params[10]`` (the options dict).
   194	    n_species:
   195	        Number of ionic species.
   196	    dt, t_end:
   197	        Physical or model-space time parameters.
   198	    D_vals:
   199	        Per-species diffusivities.
   200	    c0_vals:
   201	        Per-species bulk concentrations.
   202	    phi_applied:
   203	        Applied boundary voltage.
   204	    phi0:
   205	        Reference potential (echoed into context for inspection).
   206	    robin:
   207	        Pre-parsed Robin settings dict (keys: kappa_vals, c_inf_vals, markers).
   208	        If None, parsed from ``params["robin_bc"]``.
   209	
   210	    Returns
   211	    -------
   212	    dict
   213	        ModelScaling dict with keys: enabled, temperature_k, thermal_voltage_v,
   214	        potential_scale_v, length_scale_m, concentration_scale_mol_m3,
   215	        diffusivity_scale_m2_s, time_scale_s, kappa_scale_m_s, permittivity_f_m,
   216	        electromigration_prefactor, poisson_coefficient, charge_rhs_prefactor,
   217	        dt_model, t_end_model, D_model_vals, c0_model_vals, c_inf_model_vals,
   218	        kappa_model_vals, phi_applied_model, phi0_model,
   219	        flux_scale_mol_m2_s, current_density_scale_a_m2,
   220	        debye_length_m, debye_to_length_ratio.
   221	    """
   222	    nondim_cfg = _get_nondim_cfg(params)
   223	    enabled = _bool(nondim_cfg.get("enabled", False))
   224	
   225	    if robin is None:
   226	        robin = _get_robin_cfg(params, n_species)
   227	
   228	    temperature_k = _pos(
   229	        nondim_cfg.get("temperature_k", DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE_K), "nondim.temperature_k"
   230	    )
   231	    thermal_voltage_v = (GAS_CONSTANT * temperature_k) / FARADAY_CONSTANT
   232	
   233	    D_raw = _as_list(D_vals, n_species, "D_vals")
   234	    if any(v <= 0.0 for v in D_raw):
   235	        raise ValueError("All D_vals must be strictly positive.")
   236	
   237	    c_inf_raw = _as_list(robin["c_inf_vals"], n_species, "robin_c_inf")
   238	    kappa_raw = _as_list(robin["kappa_vals"], n_species, "robin_kappa")
   239	    c0_raw = _as_list(c0_vals, n_species, "c0")
   240	
   241	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   242	    # Dimensional mode  (enabled=False)
   243	    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   244	    if not enabled:
   245	        # Permittivity for the Poisson equation:
   246	        #   ε · Δφ  =  F · Σᵢ zᵢ cᵢ   (SI, see module docstring)
   247	        # Previously this was hardcoded to 1.0 which is incorrect for physical
   248	        # units.  We now read (or default) the permittivity from the config.
   249	        permittivity_f_m = _pos(
   250	            nondim_cfg.get(
   251	                "permittivity_f_m",
   252	                DEFAULT_RELATIVE_PERMITTIVITY_WATER * VACUUM_PERMITTIVITY_F_PER_M,
   253	            ),
   254	            "nondim.permittivity_f_m",
   255	        )
   256	        return {
   257	            "enabled": False,
   258	            "temperature_k": temperature_k,
   259	            "thermal_voltage_v": thermal_voltage_v,
   260	            "potential_scale_v": 1.0,

   390	
   391	    # PDE coefficients — see module docstring for derivation
   392	    #
   393	    # Nernst-Planck electromigration factor:
   394	    #   drift = (F/RT) · V_T · z · φ̂  →  prefactor = (F/RT) · V_T
   395	    #   When potential_scale = V_T this equals 1.0 exactly.
   396	    electromigration_prefactor = (FARADAY_CONSTANT / (GAS_CONSTANT * temperature_k)) * potential_scale
   397	
   398	    # Nondimensional Poisson equation:
   399	    #   (λ_D/L)² · Δφ̂ = −Σᵢ zᵢ ĉᵢ  →  poisson_coefficient = (λ_D/L)²
   400	    #   equivalently: ε·V_T/(F·c_ref·L²)
   401	    poisson_coefficient = (
   402	        permittivity_f_m * potential_scale
   403	    ) / (FARADAY_CONSTANT * concentration_scale * (length_scale * length_scale))
   404	
   405	    debye_length_m = float(
   406	        np.sqrt(
   407	            (permittivity_f_m * potential_scale) / (FARADAY_CONSTANT * concentration_scale)
   408	        )
   409	    )
   410	
   411	    # NOTE: This is the single-electron current density scale. For multi-electron
   412	    # reactions, callers must multiply by n_electrons (e.g., n_e * current_density_scale).
   413	    flux_scale = diffusivity_scale * concentration_scale / length_scale
   414	    current_density_scale = FARADAY_CONSTANT * flux_scale
   415	
   416	    scaling = {
   417	        "enabled": True,
   418	        "temperature_k": temperature_k,
   419	        "thermal_voltage_v": thermal_voltage_v,
   420	        "potential_scale_v": potential_scale,
   421	        "length_scale_m": length_scale,
   422	        "concentration_scale_mol_m3": concentration_scale,
   423	        "diffusivity_scale_m2_s": diffusivity_scale,
   424	        "time_scale_s": time_scale,
   425	        "kappa_scale_m_s": kappa_scale,
   426	        "permittivity_f_m": permittivity_f_m,
   427	        "electromigration_prefactor": electromigration_prefactor,
   428	        "poisson_coefficient": poisson_coefficient,
   429	        "charge_rhs_prefactor": 1.0,
   430	        "dt_model": dt_model,
   431	        "t_end_model": t_end_model,
   432	        "D_model_vals": D_model,
   433	        "c0_model_vals": c0_model,
   434	        "c_inf_model_vals": c_inf_model,
   435	        "kappa_model_vals": kappa_model,
   436	        "phi_applied_model": phi_applied_model,
   437	        "phi0_model": phi0_model,
   438	        "flux_scale_mol_m2_s": flux_scale,
   439	        "current_density_scale_a_m2": current_density_scale,
   440	        "debye_length_m": debye_length_m,
   441	        "debye_to_length_ratio": debye_length_m / length_scale,
   442	    }
   443	
   444	    verify_model_params(scaling, n_species=n_species)
   445	    return scaling
   446	
   447	
   448	def verify_model_params(scaling: dict, *, n_species: int = 2) -> None:
   449	    """Warn if model-space parameters look suspicious.
   450	
   451	    Checks are heuristic, not exhaustive.  A warning is printed (not raised)
   452	    so the solver can still attempt a solve.
   453	    """
   454	    if not scaling.get("enabled", False):
   455	        return
   456	
   457	    D_model = scaling.get("D_model_vals", [])
   458	    for i, d in enumerate(D_model):
   459	        if not (1e-8 <= float(d) <= 1e4):
   460	            print(
   461	                f"[nondim warn] D_model[{i}]={float(d):.3e} is outside [1e-8, 1e4]. "
   462	                "Check that diffusivity_scale_m2_s matches your physical inputs."
   463	            )
   464	
   465	    c0_model = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", [])
   466	    for i, c in enumerate(c0_model):
   467	        if float(c) < 0.0:
   468	            print(f"[nondim warn] c0_model[{i}]={float(c):.3e} is negative.")
   469	        elif float(c) > 1e3:
   470	            print(

codex
1. WHAT: Step 7 never asserts `formulation == "logc_muh"` or `ctx["logc_muh_transform"] is True`.
WHY: A factory regression to `logc` would not fail at the invariant layer; it would only surface later as confusing convergence failure or, worse, a misleading primary-variable comparison.
WHAT TO DO: Add hard asserts for `conv_cfg["formulation"] == "logc_muh"`, `ctx["logc_muh_transform"]`, and `ctx["mu_species"] == [h_idx]`.

2. WHAT: The stack invariants are too weak for the reaction schema.
WHY: `len(bv_reactions) == 2` does not prove this is R2e/R4e. Wrong `E_eq`, swapped reactions, missing H powers, wrong stoichiometry, or unscaled `K0_R4e` can pass.
WHAT TO DO: Assert exact reaction identities: `E_eq`, `alpha`, `n_electrons`, `reversible`, cathodic/anodic species, stoichiometry, H powers `2/4`, and `k0_R4e == K0_HAT_R4E * 1e-18`.

3. WHAT: The source builder reads static scaling values, but production residual uses live Firedrake coefficients for `phi_applied_func`, `stern_coeff_const`, `bv_k0_funcs`, `bv_alpha_funcs`, and `boltzmann_z_scale`.
WHY: Any continuation-style mutation between `build_forms` and source injection makes the manufactured source inconsistent with the actual residual.
WHAT TO DO: Either build source terms from the live ctx coefficients or assert live values equal the scaling values immediately before source construction.

4. WHAT: Clip/floor inactivity is assumed, not asserted.
WHY: `_build_bv_rates_ex` omits production eta clipping; closure helper may omit `phi_clamp`, `free_dyn_floor`, and `packing_floor`. That is only valid if every branch is provably inactive.
WHAT TO DO: Add runtime margin checks for `abs(eta_raw_j) < exponent_clip`, `abs(phi_ex) < min(phi_clamp_k)`, `abs(u_recon_i) < u_clamp`, `1 - A_dyn_ex > free_dyn_floor`, and `theta_inner_ex > packing_floor`.

5. WHAT: The planned “θ_inner discrete-min” check is not actually a discrete minimum.
WHY: `assemble(conditional(theta < threshold, 1, 0)*dx)` can miss pointwise or nodal violations depending on quadrature sampling. It proves little if the bad set is small.
WHAT TO DO: Interpolate/project `theta_inner_ex` to a suitable space and inspect `.dat.data_ro.min()`, and also keep a quadrature-point indicator check.

6. WHAT: `run_mms` return shape does not include `newton_converged`, `newton_iterations`, convergence reason, or residual norms, but Step 11 tests those.
WHY: The test plan is internally inconsistent; the convergence test cannot assert all solves converged unless the loop returns per-mesh solve status, including failures.
WHAT TO DO: Return a `per_mesh` diagnostics list or arrays for convergence flags, iteration counts, SNES reason, initial/final residual, and errors with `NaN` on failure. Do not silently drop failed meshes.

7. WHAT: Starting Newton from `U_manuf` can make the test pass as an interpolation test.
WHY: If the initial residual is already below tolerance, SNES may take zero iterations and all slopes can look perfect even with broken source terms.
WHAT TO DO: Add a pilot solve from a small deterministic perturbation of `U_manuf`, assert residual reduction and convergence back to the manufactured solution, and record initial residuals for the normal run.

8. WHAT: The risk table demands `||F_res||_final < snes_atol`, but the configured solve may converge by relative tolerance.
WHY: With large source magnitudes, final residual can legitimately exceed `1e-5`; conversely, absolute convergence alone does not prove discretization errors are solver-independent.
WHAT TO DO: Record SNES convergence reason and run a tolerance sweep at least on `N=32` and `N=64` to prove errors are insensitive to tighter `atol/rtol`.

9. WHAT: Quadrature sweep at only `N=32` is insufficient.
WHY: It can show a plateau at one mesh while quadrature error still contaminates the `N=64` convergence slope.
WHAT TO DO: Sweep degree on at least `N=32` and `N=64`, or run the full convergence chain at the candidate degree and one higher degree before pinning.

10. WHAT: No algebra-equivalence smoke test for the independently reimplemented shared-θ closure.
WHY: Step 4 is high-risk transcription work. Waiting for the full MMS pilot to catch a denominator/sign/packing mistake wastes time.
WHAT TO DO: As a pre-flight diagnostic only, compare independent `c_k_ex`, packing, and charge density against production `ctx["steric_boltzmann"]` after assigning `U_manuf`.

11. WHAT: Source independence is asserted by policy, not tested.
WHY: Accidentally using `ctx["ci_exprs"]`, production `steric_boltzmann`, or `U` in the source can self-cancel production mistakes and invalidate MMS.
WHAT TO DO: Add a source-form inspection test using UFL coefficient extraction, or a stricter code path, to verify source terms do not depend on `ctx["U"]` or `ctx["U_prev"]`.

12. WHAT: `TestMMSProductionGradedMesh` omits the acceptance criterion `newton_iterations < 30`.
WHY: Criterion 3 says fewer than 30 iterations; the planned test only checks convergence.
WHAT TO DO: Add `assert graded_mesh_results["newton_iterations"] < 30`.

13. WHAT: Graded-mesh thresholds are planned as one global L2/H1 threshold.
WHY: A loose global threshold can hide a single-field regression, especially for `mu_H` and `phi`.
WHAT TO DO: Pin per-field thresholds from pilot data, with separate entries for `u_O2`, `u_H2O2`, `mu_H`, and `phi`.

14. WHAT: The proton concentration diagnostic is missing.
WHY: Primary-variable convergence of `mu_H` is necessary, but users will compare against existing logc MMS concentration reporting. A reconstruction bug in reporting could go unnoticed.
WHAT TO DO: Report `c_H_L2` using `exp(U.sub(h_idx) - em*z_H*U.sub(phi_idx))`, not `exp(U.sub(h_idx))`. Keep assertions on primaries, but save concentration diagnostics.

15. WHAT: Factory verification claims it can inspect `bv_stern_capacitance_model` on the returned tuple.
WHY: That converted Stern coefficient is created during `build_forms` and stored in `ctx["nondim"]`, not directly by the factory.
WHAT TO DO: Make Step 2 verification build a context/forms once, then inspect `ctx["nondim"]["bv_stern_capacitance_model"]` and `ctx["stern_coeff_const"]`.

16. WHAT: The broken-config acceptance criterion is marked “optional but recommended.”
WHY: It is the only direct proof that the invariant layer catches factory drift. Optional means it will be skipped when time gets tight.
WHAT TO DO: Make `TestMMSAsserts` mandatory and parametrize broken configs: wrong formulation, no Stern, log-rate off, one counterion, wrong counterion identity, water on, cation hydrolysis on, small `dt`, loose SNES, wrong R4e factor, suppressed Poisson.

17. WHAT: Pytest-xdist/cache collision risk is acknowledged but not handled.
WHY: Fixed `/tmp/firedrake-tsfc`, `/tmp/pyop2`, and fixed `StudyResults/...` paths can collide across workers.
WHAT TO DO: Set worker-specific cache dirs before importing Firedrake when `PYTEST_XDIST_WORKER` exists, or mark these tests serial. Also make artifact writes atomic or worker-scoped.

18. WHAT: The test file may import Firedrake/MMS code too early.
WHY: `skip_without_firedrake` does not protect collection if the module import itself imports Firedrake and Firedrake is absent.
WHAT TO DO: Mirror the existing test’s lazy-import pattern: import `run_mms` and `verify_on_graded_production_mesh` inside fixtures/helpers only.

VERDICT: ISSUES_REMAIN
